##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Devour
--- CONTENT: When an opponent’s Infantry II is destroyed during combat, the Vuil’raith player captures an infantry token, and the opponent rolls for resurrection, placing the destroyed infantry on the Infantry II unit upgrade card if successful.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Devour
--- CONTENT: The Vuil’raith player cannot capture the Ul player’s Hel Titan PDS.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Devour
--- CONTENT: For additional information, see theCapture rules reference page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Amalgamation
--- CONTENT: If the Vuil’raith player produces multiple units, theirAmalgamationability may be applied to each.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Amalgamation
--- CONTENT: If the Vuil’raith player has captured their own units, they may use theirAmalgamationability when producing a unit of that type, even of they have no other units of that type in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Amalgamation
--- CONTENT: Amalgamationdoes not change the cost of the produced units, only the resources spent.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Amalgamation
--- CONTENT: The Vuil’raith player produces one fighter or infantry without spending resources for each captured fighter or infantry they spend.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Amalgamation
--- CONTENT: If the Vuil’raith player has the Naalu or Yin player’sAlliancepromissory note, they may spend one resource for one fighter or infantry, but spend a captured unit instead of that resource, then get one additional fighter or infantry for no cost, which will not count towards their production limit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Crucible(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Each gravity rift will still provide its usual +1 to each ship’s move value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Crucible(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Cruciblewill provide an additional +1 to each ship’s move value, which will not increase if that ship moves through two or more gravity rifts.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Crucible(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a ship could move from its current system to the active system through a gravity rift if its move value were +2, it may do so usingCrucible. This is true even if that ship could not reach the gravity rift withoutCrucible.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Crucible(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If the active player receivedCrucibleon a previous turn, they may play it and immediately perform a transaction with the Vuil’raith player to regain it. However,Cruciblecannot be played twice in one timing window. The active player cannot playCrucibleagain until their next turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Crucible(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Any deal between the Vuil’raith player and another player regarding whenCruciblewill be played, if made beforeCrucibleis exchanged, is non–binding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Crucible(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player plays bothCrucibleand theNav Suiteaction card during the same tactical action, they will still apply +1 to the move value of their ships that move through or out of a gravity rift.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Vortex(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A unit is not adjacent to the system it is in; theVortexability cannot target a ground force on another planet in the same systems as one of the Vuil’raith player’s Dimensional Tears, unless there is a second space dock in an adjacent system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Vortex(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Vortexcannot be used if there are no units that can be targeted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Vortex(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If a player has all their units of a particular type on the board, other than fighters or infantry, that type of unit belonging to that player cannot be targeted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Vortex(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If another player is blockading a Dimensional Tear, their units cannot be targeted withVortex.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Tear(Unit)
--- CONTENT: This system is a gravity rift, and thus an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Tear(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If a ship moves through or out of multiple gravity rifts, and/or the same gravity rift multiple times, each instance will provide a +1 to movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Tear(Unit)
--- CONTENT: Multiple Dimensional Tears in a single system have no additional effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Tear(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If a Dimensional Tear is in a system that is normally a gravity rift (e.g. the Cormund system), the Vuil’raith player will not have to roll for removal when moving out of or through that system. There are no additional effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Tear(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If a Dimensional Tear is in a system with a Nebula, then the +1 to move values will be applied after the nebula sets each ship’s move value to 1.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Tear(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If the Dimensional Tear plastic figure is destroyed or removed, the Dimensional Tear token is also removed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Terror Between(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: WhenThe Terror Betweenis destroyed, it still captures units that were destroyed at the same time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Terror Between(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If ships are destroyed outside of combat, those ships will still be captured byThe Terror Between.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Stillness of Stars(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If a player loses their commodities immediately after replenishing them, most commonly via that player’sTrade Agreementpromissory note, the Vuil’raith player may still target them. If they do, they still use that player’s full commodity value to determine which units may be captured.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Stillness of Stars(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The Vuil’raith player cannot capture a unit without a cost. Notably, they cannot capture a PDS, a space dock, or a war sun of a player without their war sun unit upgrade.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Stillness of Stars(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Vuil’raith player chooses to capture a fighter or infantry, they will capture one, not two.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Stillness of Stars(Agent)
--- CONTENT: When the primary ability of theTradestrategy card is resolved, the Vuil’raith player must choose if they will use The Stillness of Stars or not after the active player has replenished their commodities, but before players are chosen to perform the secondary ability without spending a command token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Stillness of Stars(Agent)
--- CONTENT: When the secondary ability of theTradestrategy card is resolved, the Vuil’raith player must choose if they will use The Stillness of Stars or not after the current player has replenished their commodities, but before the next player has decided if they will spend a command token to perform the secondary.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: The Stillness of Stars(Agent)
--- CONTENT: When The Stillness of Stars converts a player’s commodities to trade goods, those trade goods are not treated as being gained for the purpose of triggering other abilities. In particular, the Mentak player’sPillagefaction ability is not triggered by this ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: It Feeds on Carrion — Dimensional Anchor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Units captured while resolvingDimensional Anchorare not destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: It Feeds on Carrion — Dimensional Anchor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If a player’s units are blockading one of the Vuil’raith player’s Dimensional Tears, dice will not be rolled for that player’s units when resolvingDimensional Anchor.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: It Feeds on Carrion — Dimensional Anchor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Each non–fighter ship affected will roll only once, regardless of how many Dimensional Tears it is adjacent to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: It Feeds on Carrion — Dimensional Anchor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The player that owns the ground forces and fighters chooses which are removed. They are not assigned to particular ships beforehand.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: It Feeds on Carrion — Dimensional Anchor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player has used aValefar Assimilatorfaction technology to copy Dimensional Tear II, ships in systems containing or adjacent to the Nekro player’s space docks will also have to roll for capture when resolvingDimensional Anchor. This includes the Nekro player’s own ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Reanimator(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If the Vuil’raith player owns the Infantry II unit upgrade technology, and one is destroyed during ground combat on a planet with a Reanimator, the Vuil’raith player captures an infantry token, and they roll for resurrection, placing the destroyed infantry on the Infantry II unit upgrade card if successful.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Reanimator(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If the Vuil’raith player’s infantry on a planet with a Reanimator are destroyed outside of combat, such as with thePlagueaction card, those infantry will be captured.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Al’raith Ix Ianovar(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: When The Fracture is brought into play byAl’raith Ix Ianovar, they will choose four systems containing planets with different technology specialties to place ingress tokens in, instead of using the warfare and biotic synergy ofAl’raith Ix Ianovarto determine where the ingress tokens are placed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Vuil’raith Cabal
--- SECTION_ID: Al’raith Ix Ianovar(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Vuil’raith player may move the ingress tokens into systems that contain their Dimensional Tears.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attacker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During combat, the active player is the attacker.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attacker
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The attacker’s opponent is the defender.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attacker
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The attacker will have the first opportunity to resolve abilities during each timing window.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attacker
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When the Mahact player resolves theirBenedictionhero ability, the player that had their ships moved will be the attacker.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player has several faction–specific leader cards that represent characters with unique abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each faction has three leaders; one agent, one commander, and one hero.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player’s leaders are placed on their leader sheet during setup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: An agent does not need to be unlocked and begins the game in a readied state. They can be exhausted by resolving their abilities, and they ready during theReady Cardsstep of the status phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A commander must be unlocked to use its abilities. A player unlocks their commander if they fulfill the conditions listed after the “Unlock” header.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A commander cannot be exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheAlliancepromissory note allows a player to share their commander’s ability with another player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A hero needs to be unlocked to use their abilities. A player unlocks their hero if they fulfill the conditions listed after the “Unlock” header.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A hero cannot be exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A hero is purged after its abilities are resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A commander’s ability cannot be applied to the instance of the effect that unlocked it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A commander may be unlocked between two abilities that occur in the same timing window.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about a leader of a specific faction, see that faction’s page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leaders
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Planets and some space areas can be explored, yielding varying results determined by the cards drawn from the exploration decks.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player takes control of a planet that is not already controlled by another player, they explore that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player explores a planet, they draw and resolve a card from the exploration deck that corresponds to that planet’s trait.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Certain abilities may allow a planet to be explored multiple times.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can explore space areas that contain frontier tokens if they own theDark Energy Taptechnology or if another game effect allows them to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player explores a frontier token, they draw and resolve a card from the frontier exploration deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a frontier token is explored, it is discarded and returned to the supply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve an exploration card, a player reads the card, makes any necessary decisions, and resolves its ability. If the card was not a relic fragment or an attachment, it is discarded into its respective discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player resolves an exploration card that has an “attach” header, they attach that card to the planet card of the planet being explored.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player resolves an exploration card that has “relic fragment” in the title, they place that card faceup in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: An exploration cards that purges itself is not discarded into its respective discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Enigmatic DeviceandIon Stormare placed into play, not into the frontier discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is to gain multiple planets in a system, they choose the order in which they gain them, and explore each planet as they gain it before gaining the next.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may perform transactions after revealing an exploration card and before resolving it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Before resolving an exploration card, it is revealed to all players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific exploration cards, see theexploration cards notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Attach

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The primary way that a player produces new units is by resolving theProductionabilities of existing units during a tactical action. However, other game effects also allow players to produce units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each unit that a player can produce has a cost value presented on its faction sheet or technology card. To produce a unit, a player must spend a number of resources equal to or greater than the cost value of the unit they are producing.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the cost is accompanied by two icons – typically for fighters and infantry – a player produces two of that unit for that cost.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player produces a unit through the use of their units’Productionabilities during a tactical action, that player follows the rules of theProductionability to determine where in the active system the units can be placed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player produces a unit through an ability outside of the tactical action, that ability will state how many units that player can produce and where that player can place those units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player is limited by the number of units in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot produce ships in a system that contains other players’ ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Whenever a unit is produced, its cost must be paid, unless the effect that is producing the unit explicitly says otherwise.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot produce one fighter and one infantry for one resource.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an effect allows a player to produce a unit of a specific type, then factional variations do not prevent that player from producing that type of unit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player removes a unit in order to place it, because they have none of that unit type in their reinforcements, that unit is placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Blockaded
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Producing Units
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Component Limitations
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Cost

##################################################

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Supernova
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A supernova is an anomaly that affects movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Supernova
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ship cannot move through or into a supernova.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Supernova
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a ship finds itself in a supernova by some uncommon game effect, it may remain there and move out without harm.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Supernova
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will place the ship movement restrictions of anomalies upon all units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Supernova
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Anomalies
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Supernova
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Frontier Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Frontier tokens can be explored for a variety of game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Frontier Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Frontier tokens are placed on the game board during setup. One frontier token is placed in each system that does not contain any planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Frontier Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Players may explore space areas that contain frontier tokens if they own theDark Energy Taptechnology or if another game effect allows them to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Frontier Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Exploration
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding coexistence.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Some game effects allow two or more players’ units to exist on a planet without triggering combat; this is coexistence.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: One player controls the planet; all other players are coexisting on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A coexisting structure is always blockaded, regardless of what ships, if any, are in the system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If additional units are added to those already coexisting, by, for example, committing additional ground forces during an invasion, or resolving an effect that allows a unit to be placed directly on a planet, the added units immediately coexist.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If only one player has units on a planet that was in coexistence, the coexistence ends, and that player gains control of that planet if they were the coexisting player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a player uses theBombardmentability of 1 of their units against a planet in coexistence, they choose which player’s units on that planet will have the hits assigned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who controls a planet may start a ground combat against a coexisting player during the invasion step of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who is coexisting on a planet may start a ground combat against the player that controls that planet during the invasion step of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who had no units on a planet, but commits 1 or more ground forces during the invasion step of a tactical action must start a ground combat against the player that controls that planet (unless they have an ability that would allow them to coexist).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Should a player win the ground combat on a planet resulting from one of these aforementioned methods, they gain control of that planet, if they were not in control of it already. Then, they may start an additional ground combat against another coexisting player, if present, and may continue to do so until they decline to start another ground combat or there are no more coexisting players. Any coexisting players that they do not resolve a ground combat against remain coexisting.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player is considered to control a planet they are coexisting on solely when scoring an objective. For any other game ability or effect, they are not considered to control that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Control
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Coexistence
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Mecatol Rex
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Mecatol Rex is the planet placed in the center of the game board during setup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Mecatol Rex
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During setup, the custodians token is placed on Mecatol Rex. This token prevents a player from committing ground forces to land on the planet unless they spend six influence to remove the token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Mecatol Rex
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Mecatol Rex is not a legendary planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Mecatol Rex
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Custodians Token
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Mecatol Rex
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Imperial
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Mecatol Rex
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leader Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player has a leader sheet that contains slots for their faction’s three leader cards as well as their faction’s mech unit card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leader Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The leader slots of the leader sheet are where players place their three leader cards during setup. Each slot displays the name of the type of leader that is placed in that slot (agent, commander, and hero) as well as a symbol in the upper–right that helps players quickly determine which side of those leaders begins the game faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leader Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The mech slot of the leader sheet is where players place their mech unit cards during setup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leader Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players who are familiar with the game can hide the quick reference by placing that portion of the leader sheet under their faction sheets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leader Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Leaders
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leader Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Mechs
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Politics (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: ThePoliticsstrategy card allows players to draw action cards. Additionally, the active player chooses a new speaker and looks at cards in the agenda deck. This card’s initiative value is “3”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Politics (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has thePoliticsstrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Politics (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on thePoliticsstrategy card, the active player resolves the following effects in order:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Politics (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of thePoliticsstrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend one command token from their strategy pool to draw two action cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Politics (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If there are few cards remaining in the action card deck, they will be dealt out in clockwise order from the active player. After those players have discarded down to their seven card hand limit, if necessary, the discard pile will be shuffled to form a new deck. The remaining players (including the player who received the last action card from the previous deck, if applicable) will then be dealt their action cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Politics (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When resolving the primary ability of thePoliticscard, the active player cannot show the agenda cards they drew to any other player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player begins the game with control of each planet in their home system. During the game, players can gain control of additional planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player gains control of a planet, they take the planet card that corresponds to that planet and place it in their play area; that card is exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot gain control of a planet that they already control.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: While a player controls a planet, that planet’s card remains in their play area until they lose control of that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can control a planet that they do not have any units on; that player places a control token on that planet to mark that they control it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player loses control of a planet if they no longer have units on it and another player has units on it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can lose control of a planet through some game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player loses control of a planet that contains their control token, they remove their control token from the planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Control tokens are not component limited; a player may control an unlimited number of planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Attach
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Exhausted
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Invasion
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Control
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The active system is the system that is activated during a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player performs a tactical action, they activate a system by placing a command token from their tactic pool in that system. That system is the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A playercannotactivate a system that already contains one of their command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A playercanactivate a system that contains command tokens that match other players’ factions.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A system remains the active system for the duration of the tactical action during which it was activated.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may only move into a nebula if it is the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: No system is the active system during a component or strategic action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: After activating a system during a tactical action, play will proceed to theMovementstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active System
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Nebula
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: System Tiles
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding entropic scars.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: An entropic scar is an anomaly that affects unit abilities and faction technologies.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A unit in an entropic scar cannot use unit abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A unit outside of an entropic scar cannot use unit abilities against units that are in an entropic scar.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Wormhole tokens that would be placed in an entropic scar are returned to the supply or a player’s reinforcements as appropriate.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: At the start of the status phase, a player with ships in an entropic scar may spend a command token from their strategy pool to gain one of their faction–specific technologies.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Entropic Scars
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Anomalies
##################################################

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheImperialstrategy card allows players to score victory points and draw secret objectives. This card’s initiative value is “8”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has theImperialstrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on theImperialstrategy card, the active player can score one public objective of their choice if they meet that objective’s requirements as described on its card. Then, if the active player controls Mecatol Rex, they gain one victory point; if they do not control Mecatol Rex, they can draw one secret objective card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theImperialstrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend one command token from their strategy pool to draw one secret objective card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player has more than three secret objective cards after drawing a secret objective, they must choose one of theirunscoredsecret objectives and return it to the secret objective deck. This number includes the secret objective cards in the player’s handandthe cards that player has already scored. Then, they shuffle the secret objective deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player must control every planet in their home system to score a public objective using the first primary ability ofImperial.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who controls Mecatol Rex does not need to control every planet in their home system to gain a victory point from the second primary ability ofImperial.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who controls Mecatol Rex while resolving the primary ability ofImperialmust gain a victory point; they cannot instead draw a secret objective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who needs to discard a secret objective must do so and reshuffle the deck before the next player may draw from the deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Imperial (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Initiative Order
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Mecatol Rex

### RULE_SOURCE: Initiative Order
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Initiative order is the order in which players resolve steps of the action and status phases.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Initiative Order
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Initiative order is determined by the initiative numbers on strategy cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Initiative Order
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Initiative order begins with the player who has the lowest–numbered strategy card and proceeds to the player who has the strategy card that is next in numerical order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Initiative Order
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When playing with three or four players, a player’s initiative is determined only by their lowest–numbered strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Initiative Order
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If there are multiple abilities that players wish to resolve at the same time during the action phase, initiative order will determine the order they are resolved in. See theabilities pagefor more details.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Initiative Order
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The initiative order of all strategy cards is:
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: The Atrament — Primor
--- CONTENT: Both infantry must be placed on the same planet.

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Dok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yard — Garbozia
--- CONTENT: Cards onDok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yarddo not count towards a player’s action card hand limit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Dok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yard — Garbozia
--- CONTENT: The player withThe Codexcannot take cards that are onDok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yard.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Dok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yard — Garbozia
--- CONTENT: If another player gains control of Garbozia, any action cards onDok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yardwill remain there when the legendary planet ability card is transferred; the new controller of Garbozia may play those action cards in the future.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Dok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yard — Garbozia
--- CONTENT: Dok ’N Pic’s Salvage Yardneed not be readied for a player to play the action cards on it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: The Galactic Council — Mecatol Rex
--- CONTENT: The Galactic Councilcannot be exhausted by a player that has no unscored secret objective cards in their hand.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Maxis Central Control — Faunus
--- CONTENT: If the gained planet was not controlled by another player, it is explored.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit with theAnti–Fighter Barrageability may be able to destroy an opponent’s fighters at the onset of a space battle. During theAnti–Fighter Barragestep of the first round of space combat, players perform the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1: Each player rolls dice for each of their units in the combat that has theAnti–Fighter Barrageability; this is called an anti–fighter barrage roll. A hit is produced for each die roll that is equal to or greater than the unit’sAnti–Fighter Barragevalue.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2: Each player must choose and destroy one of their fighters in the active system for each hit their opponent’s anti–fighter barrage roll produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A non–fighter ship cannot use itsSustain Damageability to cancel a hit produced by an anti–fighter barrage roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Effects such as theShields Holdingaction card, which trigger on hits produced during space combat, may be used to cancel a hit produced by an anti–fighter barrage roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The “0” side of the d10 represents a result of 10.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Destroyed
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anti–Fighter Barrage (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Space Combat

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Blood Ties
--- CONTENT: The Winnu player must still commit at least one ground force to Mecatol Rex to remove the custodians token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Reclamation
--- CONTENT: Placing the structure will occur after theProductionstep. If the Winnu player places a Space Dock, they cannot produce out of it during the same action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Reclamation
--- CONTENT: If the Winnu player has no PDS or Space Docks left in their reinforcements, they may remove a unit from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that unit on Mecatol Rex when resolvingReclamation.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Acquiescence(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If either strategy card had trade goods on it at the start of the strategy phase, those trade goods remain with the player that originally chose the strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Acquiescence(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: In a three– or four–player game, the player that playedAcquiescencechooses which one strategy card from each player are swapped.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Acquiescence Ω(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player playsAcquiescence Ωwhen the Winnu player is resolving theConstructionstrategy card, that player will not place a command token in the system they placed their structure in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Acquiescence Ω(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player has their commander, Magmus, unlocked, and they playAcquiescence Ω, they will not gain a trade good from their commander ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Hegemonic Trade Policy(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Changing a planet’s resource value will affect theProductionvalue of a Space Dock on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Lazax Gate Folding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: WhileLazax Gate Foldingis exhausted, the wormhole passive effect still applies if its conditions are met.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Lazax Gate Folding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Lazax Gate Foldingmay cause the Mecatol Rex system to be adjacent to other systems containing an alpha or beta wormhole for all players during the Winnu player’s tactical actions.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Lazax Gate Folding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Winnu player may use the component action ofLazax Gate Foldingif they do not control Mecatol Rex. If they do, they must exhaust it, and there will be no additional effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Salai Sai Corian(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the Winnu player’s opponent has only fighters participating in the combat, theSalai Sai Corianwill roll no dice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Salai Sai Corian(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: During a combat against the Nekro player in a system containing each player’s flagships, theSalai Sai Corianwill count the Nekro player’s infantry participating in the combat when determining how many dice to roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Berekar Berekon(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Productionlimits still apply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Rickar Rickani(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If Rickar Rickani is unlocked via a combat in the Mecatol Rex system, then the +2 will apply to combat rolls during that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Rickar Rickani(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If a system meets two (or more) of the conditions listed (such as by attaching theNano–Forgerelic to Mecatol Rex), Rickar Rickani will only apply +2 to combat rolls, not +4 (or +6).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Mathis Mathinus — Imperial Seal(Hero)
--- CONTENT: A player chosen to perform the secondary ability must still spend a command token from their strategy pool to do so, except for theLeadershipstrategy card and potentially theTradestrategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Mathis Mathinus — Imperial Seal(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Winnu player chooses theTradestrategy card for this ability and the Winnu player chooses a player to resolve the secondary without spending a command token via the primary ability, the chosen player must resolve the secondary ability. Additionally, if the Winnu player chooses a player to resolve the secondary via the Hero’s ability, it is optional for that player to resolve the secondary, but if they do, they must spend a strategy token to do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Mathis Mathinus — Imperial Seal(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Acquiescence Ωcannot be triggered by this ability.

--- CONTENT: Placing the structure will occur after theProductionstep. If the Winnu player places a Space Dock, they cannot produce out of it during the same action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Reclaimer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If the Winnu player has no PDS or Space Docks left in their reinforcements, they may remove a unit from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that unit on the newly controlled planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Reclaimer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If the Winnu player gains control of a planet with multiple Reclaimers, they may place a structure for each one, if they may do so without exceeding the maximum number of that structure allowed on a planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Reclaimer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Reclaimer need only be on the planet at the end of the tactical action the Winnu player gained it, not when the Winnu player gains control of it. This can occur from effects such as theInfiltrateaction card, or some exploration cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Imperator(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Winnu player applies the +1 to their combat rolls even if it is the Winnu player’s ownSupport for the Thronein their opponent’s play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Winnu
--- SECTION_ID: Imperator(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If their opponent receives aSupport for the Throneduring a combat, the Winnu player will apply +1 to the remaining combat rolls during that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Two players are neighbors if they both have a unit or control a planet in the same system. They are also neighbors if they both have a unit or control a planet in systems that are adjacent to each other.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can resolve transactions with their neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players are neighbors if the adjacency of systems is granted by a wormhole.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players are neighbors with the Ghosts of Creuss if the Ghosts of Creuss’ “Quantum Entanglement” faction ability is causing adjacency from the perspective of the Ghosts of Creuss player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may make a deal with any player, however, these deals may only include a transaction if the two players are neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may resolve one transaction with each other player per each agenda during the agenda phase, however, the agenda phase does not make all players neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Adjacency
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neighbors
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Transactions
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheTechnologystrategy card allows players to research new technology. This card’s initiative value is “7”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has theTechnologystrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on theTechnologystrategy card, the active player can research one technology of their choice. Then, they may research one additional technology of their choice by spending six resources.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theTechnologystrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may research one technology of their choice by spending one command token from their strategy pool and four resources.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The speaker is the player who has the speaker token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the strategy phase, the speaker is the first player to choose a strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the agenda phase, the speaker reveals the top agenda card from the agenda deck before each vote. The speaker is always the last player to vote and decides which outcome to resolve if the outcomes are tied.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During setup, the speaker prepares the objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the status phase, the speaker reveals a public objective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A random player gains the speaker token during setup before the game begins.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if a player resolves the primary ability on thePoliticsstrategy card, that player chooses any player other than the current speaker to gain the speaker token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the speaker is eliminated from the game, the speaker token is passed to the player to the speaker’s left.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Speaker
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: During the strategy and agenda phases, the speaker will have the first opportunity to resolve abilities during each timing window.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A game round consists of the following four phases:Strategy PhaseAction PhaseStatus PhaseAgenda Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players skip the agenda phase during the early portion of each game. After the custodians token is removed from Mecatol Rex, the agenda phase is added to each game round.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Player turns occur during the action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Abilities that last until the end of a player’s turn do not persist for the duration of a game round or into the other phases of that game round. Those effects end at the end of that player’s turn, before the next player’s turn begins.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: During the strategy, status and agenda phases, players to not take turns for the purpose of game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A game has a maximum of nine game rounds.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Round
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Action Phase

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Planets provide players with resources and influence. Planets are on system tiles and each has a name, a resource value, and an influence value. Some planets also have traits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet’s resources are indicated by the value on its planet card and system tile that is surrounded by a yellow triangular border.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet’s influence is indicated by the value on its planet card and system tile that is surrounded by a blue hexagonal border.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet’s trait has no inherent effects, but some game effects refer to a planet’s trait. There are three traits: cultural, hazardous, and industrial.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some planets have a technology specialty, which allows those planets to be exhausted to satisfy a prerequisite when researching technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some planets are legendary planets, as indicated by the legendary planet icon. When a player gains control of a legendary planet, they also gain control of its legendary planet ability card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet card has both a readied and exhausted state. When a planet is readied, it is placed faceup. When a planet is exhausted, it is placed facedown.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can spend a readied planet’s resources or influence.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot spend an exhausted planet’s resources or influence.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Mecatol Rex and planets in home systems do not have traits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Planets with traits can be explored.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A planet cannot be spent for both its influence and resources during a single exhaustion.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a planet is exhausted for its technology specialty, it does not provide influence or resources.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may only exhaust their own planets, unless a game effect specifies otherwise.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Control
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Exploration
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Exhausted
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Modifiers
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A modifier is a number that is applied by an ability to increase or decrease the attribute values of a unit or the results of a die roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Modifiers
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A modifier is always preceded by the word “apply” followed by a numerical value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Modifiers
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A modifier value preceded by a “+” is added to the attribute or result being modified; a modifier value preceded by a “−” is subtracted from the attribute or result being modified.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Modifiers
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: “Combat roll” modifiers do not modify anti–fighter barrage, bombardment or space cannon rolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Modifiers
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When an effect moves a unit to an adjacent system, modifying that unit’s move value will have no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Modifiers
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Two system tiles are adjacent to each other if any of the tiles’ sides are touching each other.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A system that has a wormhole is treated as being adjacent to a system that has a matching wormhole.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit or planet is adjacent to all system tiles that are adjacent to the system tile that contains that unit or planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet is treated as being adjacent to the system that contains that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Systems that are connected by lines drawn across one or more hyperlane tiles are adjacent for all purposes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A unit is not adjacent to the system it is in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The Wormhole Nexus and the Creuss home system are only adjacent to tiles via wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Game Board
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Hyperlanes
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Adjacency
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Neighbors
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Warfare (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheWarfarestrategy card allows a player to remove a command token from the board and redistribute their command tokens between their tactic, fleet, and strategy pools. This card’s initiative value is “6”. During the action phase, if the active player has theWarfarestrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Warfare (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on theWarfarestrategy card, the active player performs the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Warfare (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1: The active player removes any one of their command tokens from the game board. Then, that player gains that command token by placing it in a pool of their choice on their command sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Warfare (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2: The active player can redistribute their command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Warfare (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theWarfarestrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend one command token from their strategy pool to resolve theProductionability of one space dock in their home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Warfare (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the player withWarfarehas no command tokens on the game board, they may still perform a strategic action. However, they will not gain a command token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A structure is a type of unit. PDS units and space docks are structures.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Structures are always placed on planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Structures are primarily placed on planets using theConstructionstrategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Structures cannot move or be transported.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can have a maximum ofonespace dock on each planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can have a maximum oftwoPDS units on each planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot place a structure on a planet if it would exceed the maximum number of allowed structures of that type on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Structures
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
