### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Threat
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player may still play rider action cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Threat
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player has the Xxcha player’sAlliancepromissory note, the Nekro player may vote, without losing their ability to predict outcomes for theirGalactic Threatability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Threat
--- CONTENT: If the speaker breaks a tie without casting any votes, then the speaker’s technology are ineligible to be gained.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Technology Singularity
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player gains a technology during a space combat, this does not prevent them from gaining technology during ground combats in theInvasionstep of the same tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Technology Singularity
--- CONTENT: If multiple ground combats happen on separate planets as part of a singleInvasionstep during one action, the Nekro player may gain a technology during each combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Technology Singularity
--- CONTENT: Any method that destroys a unit during combat will triggerTechnology Singularity, including an anti–fighter barrage roll, theDirect Hitaction card, the Creuss player’sDimensional Splicerfaction technology, etc.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Technology Singularity
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player chooses to gain a unit upgrade technology, that upgrade will be in effect from that point in the combat onwards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Technology Singularity
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player destroys a unit, and gains a technology with an ability that is used during the same timing window, they may use that ability immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Technology Singularity
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player gains the Infantry II unit upgrade from theirTechnology Singularityability during a combat, any of the Nekro player’s infantry destroyed at the same time as the unit used to trigger theTechnology Singularityability will be returned to their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Propagation
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player resolves an ability that instructs them to “gain” a technology, instead of “research” that technology, they will get that technology instead of the command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Propagation
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player may still resolve the primary or secondary abilities of theTechnologystrategy card, which will instead gain them command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Propagation
--- CONTENT: If an ability triggers “when” a player researches a technology, that ability will still be triggered by the Nekro player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Propagation
--- CONTENT: If an ability triggers “after” a player researches a technology, that ability will never be triggered by the Nekro player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Propagation
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player may play any action card that would allow them to research a technology, even if there is no viable technology that the Nekro player could have researched.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Antivirus(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The effect ofAntivirusdoes not prevent the Nekro player gaining a technology from a player via theirGalactic Threatability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Antivirus(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The player holdingAntivirusmay only play it at the start of a combat they are participating in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Antivirus(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Antivirushas no effect while it is in a player’s hand.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Antivirus(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Antivirusis returned when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the Nekro player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Antivirus(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Activating a system containing only the Nekro player’s structures will still causeAntivirusto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Antivirus(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the Nekro player’s units (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeAntivirusto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: When copying another technology, eachValefar Assimilatorretains its original text; it may later be used to copy a different faction technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: When copying another technology,Valefar Assimilatorwill retain its exhausted/readied state. It will not copy the target technology’s exhausted/readied state.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player would copy a faction–specific unit upgrade, and they are already copying a faction–specific unit upgrade of the same type, they must use the same Valefar Assimilator token; they lose the previous faction unit upgrade.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player cannot copy faction–specific units that have not been upgraded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A faction’s mech is not a technology. The Nekro player cannot use aValefar Assimilatorto copy a mech.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player has a generic unit upgrade, and gains a faction–specific unit upgrade, then the faction–specific version will be in effect. If the faction–specific unit upgrade is later lost, they revert to the generic unit upgrade.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If another player returns a technology which is currently being copied by aValefar Assimilator, it will remain copied with a Valefar Assimilator token on it while in that player’s technology deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: For theAdapt New Strategiesobjective, aValefar Assimilatortechnology will count if and only if it is currently copying another technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: For notes about technologies of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player has copied certain technology (possibly two or more at different points in time), the following apply:

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: Valefar Assimilator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player may lose a technology if they copy a new one. If they lose certain technologies, the following apply:

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Any effect that may target ships or non–fighter ships may target a ground force that is participating in space combat due to the effect ofThe Alastor.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: After the Nekro player uses the ability ofThe Alastor, all other players will have the opportunity to resolve an “at the start of combat” or an “at the start of a round of combat” ability before the Nekro player may resolve another ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Some abilities may destroyThe Alastorat the start of a combat before the Nekro player has used its ability, such as theAssault Cannontechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Ground forces on planets remain there while participating in combat. Effects that target units in a space area cannot target these ground forces.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: IfThe Alastoris destroyed during space combat, any ground forces in that combat remain in that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player copies another player’s flagship unit upgrade technology with one of theirValefar Assimilatortechnologies during a space combat, any ground forces in that combat remain in that combat. If the Nekro player starts the space combat copying another player’s flagship unit upgrade technology, ground forces cannot participate in that combat, unless the Nekro player stops copying that flagship unit upgrade technology during the “start of combat” window.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: The ground forces in the space area during the combat still retain their ability to be transported. Since transported units do not count against capacity during combat, these ground forces will not count toward the Nekro player’s fleet pool limit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A mech in the space combat may be targeted with theDirect Hitaction card if it uses itsSustain Damageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player has one of theirValefar Assimilatortokens on the Ul player’s Hel Titan II faction unit upgrade technology, they may useThe Alastorto have their PDS in the active system participate in the space combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Nekro Virus
--- SECTION_ID: The Alastor(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A ground force participating in a space combat may count towards scoring theDemonstrate Your Powersecret objective.

--- CONTENT: A PDS unit is placed on a planet. Each planet can have a maximum oftwoPDS units.

--- CONTENT: If a player’s PDS is ever on a planet that does not contain any of their own ground forces and contains a unit that belongs to another player, that PDS is destroyed.

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A gravity rift is an anomaly that affects movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ship that will move out of or through a gravity rift at any time during its movement, applies +1 to its move value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: For each ship that would move out of or through a gravity rift, one die is rolled immediately before it exits the gravity rift system; on a result of 1–3, that ship is removed from the board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A gravity rift can affect the same ship multiple times during a single movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A system that contains multiple gravity rifts is treated as a single gravity rift.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Moving into a gravity rift, usually when it is the active system, will not provide the +1, nor will the ships have to roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship removed by a gravity rift is not destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: All ship movement must be declared before any of them roll for gravity rift removal. A player may not choose additional ships to move after seeing the result of this roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship that is removed by a gravity rift will not count toward the fleet limit in the destination system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Retreating from a gravity rift will result in the following:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a ship moves through or out of multiple gravity rifts, and/or the same gravity rift multiple times, each instance will provide a +1 to movement, and requires a separate roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a ship with capacity would transport another unit after moving out of or through a gravity rift, but is removed, that unit remains where it is.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A system containing a Vuil’raith Dimensional Tear is a gravity rift, and thus an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will place the ship movement restrictions of anomalies upon all units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Anomalies
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Gravity Rift
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Transport
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player’s unit withProductionis blockaded if it is in a system that does not contain any of their ships and contains other players’ ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot use a blockaded unit to produce ships; that player can still use a blockaded unit to produce ground forces.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player blockades another player’s space dock, if the blockaded player has captured any of the blockading player’s units, those units are returned to the blockading player’s reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: While a player is involved in a space combat in a system, their units in that system are not blockaded, as both players will have ships in the system. Consequently, they may capture their opponent’s units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If, at the end of a combat, one player has no ships, but a space dock in the system, and the other player has only fighters, the space dock will be blockaded before the fighters are removed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a ship moves, it does not blockade units in systems it moves through.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Capture
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Producing Units
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Production
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Ships
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Blockaded
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Space Dock
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Cards have a readied state, which indicates that a player can exhaust or resolve the abilities on those cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A card that is readied is placed faceup in a player’s play area; a card that is exhausted is placed facedown in a player’s area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can exhaust a readied planet card to spend resources or influence from that card’s planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can exhaust certain readied technology cards to resolve those cards’ abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a card is exhausted, a player cannot resolve that card’s abilities or spend resources or influence on that card until it is readied.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During aReady Cardsstep, each player readies all of their exhausted cards by flipping them faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player performs a strategic action, they exhaust their chosen strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Passive abilities on an exhausted card are still in effect while that card is exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Planets will also ready at the end of each agenda phase. Leaders, relics and technologies will not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a game effect instructs a player to ready a planet, the readied planet must be controlled by that player, unless the game effect specifies otherwise.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Diplomacy
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Exhausted
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Leaders
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Readied
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Relics
##################################################

##################################################

--- CONTENT: Technology
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The active player is the player taking a turn during the action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, the player who is first in initiative order is the first active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player takes a turn, the next player in initiative order becomes the active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the last player in initiative order takes a turn, the player who is first in initiative order becomes the active player again, and turns begin again in initiative order, ignoring any players who have already passed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: During the strategy, status and agenda phases, no player is the active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: During combat, the active player is the attacker.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The active player will have the first opportunity to resolve abilities during each timing window.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: All transactions during the action phase must involve the active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a non–active player produces hits using theSpace Cannon Offenseability of one of their units, those hits must be assigned to the active player’s units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Action Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Attacker
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Initiative Order
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Active Player
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Space Cannon
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some game effects instruct a player to reroll dice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a die is rerolled, its new result is used instead of its previous result.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The same ability cannot be used to reroll the same die multiple times, but multiple abilities can be used to reroll a single die.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Die rerolls must occur after rolling the dice, before other abilities are resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Effects that reroll “combat rolls” do not reroll anti–fighter barrage, bombardment or space cannon rolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Anti–Fighter Barrage
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Bombardment
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Combat
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Rerolls
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Space Cannon
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Star Forge
--- CONTENT: The Muaat player cannot useStar Forgeif the do not have a war sun on the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Fires of the Gashlai(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player already owns their war sun unit upgrade technology, they cannot playFires of the Gashlai.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus Reactor(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The war sun must be in the system prior to the use ofProductionto gain the trade good.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus Reactor(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The trade good is gained after the use ofProduction; it cannot be used to pay for the produced units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus Reactor Ω(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player has a unit in a system containing a supernova, they cannot be eliminated.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Umbat(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The produced units must be paid for.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Umbat(Agent)
--- CONTENT: No unit is using itsProductionability. TheSarween Toolstechnology and similar effects will not allow a more expensive ship to be produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Umbat(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If ground forces are produced, they may be placed in the space area or on a planet the player controls in the system with their war sun or flagship.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Umbat(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Naalu or Yin players are chosen, and choose to produce fighters or infantry, they will only be able to produce two of those units; their commander will have no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: When a command token is spent to resolve the secondary ability of a strategy card, the trade good is gained after resolving the secondary ability. As such, it cannot be spent to pay for costs of the secondary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player spends multiple tokens from their strategy pool (e.g. for theLead From the Frontobjective), they gain that many trade goods, one at a time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player uses the ability of theScepter of Emelparrelic, they will be unable to benefit from the ability of Magmus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Magmus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Muaat player must have Magmus unlocked before spending the strategy token in order to gain the trade good.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any method of movement is sufficient to trigger this ability, not only tactical action movement. For example, the Muaat player may triggerNova Seedwhen they retreat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the war sun is in the target system when it is activated, it must move out of the system, and back in, forNova Seedto be able to be triggered.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any command tokens, frontier tokens and the Muaat player’s units on the replaced system tile are transferred to the new supernova tile. Any Creuss wormhole tokens are returned to the Creuss player and any Ul sleeper tokens are returned to the Ul player. All other tokens are purged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Muaat player’s units may exist in and move out of the supernova system, even if the Muaat player does not ownMagmus Reactor.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player ownsMagmus Reactor Ω, and resolves this ability during a tactical action, they will be able to produce units during theProductionstep, if the Muaat player still has units in the system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Nova Seedcannot target the home system of an eliminated player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Nova Seedmay target the Creuss Gate (tile 17) or the Wormhole Nexus (tile 82).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Adjudicator Ba’al — Nova Seed(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Empyrean player cannot use the ability of their agent, Acamar, on the Muaat player after they useNova Seedif the original system tile contained planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Genesis(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Muaat player explores Avernus when they gain it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Genesis(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Muaat player may move Avernus even if another player controls it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Genesis(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Avernus may be moved into a system containing another player’s units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Genesis(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Structures may be placed on Avernus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Avernus — The Nucleus(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player usesThe Nucleus, they will not gain a trade good from the ability of their commander, Magmus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Avernus — The Nucleus(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player usesThe Nucleus, they will still place infantry with their adjacent mechs.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Embers of Muaat
--- SECTION_ID: Avernus — The Nucleus(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: If another player controls Avernus, they may useThe Nucleusonly if they have a war sun on the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Entanglement
--- CONTENT: The effect of theEnforced Travel Banlaw does not affect the Creuss player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Entanglement
--- CONTENT: If the Creuss player has units or controls planets in a system with an alpha wormhole, and another player has units or controls planets in a system with a beta wormhole, or vice versa, then the Creuss player and that player are neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Entanglement
--- CONTENT: If Mecatol Rex contains an alpha wormhole, then the “For” effect of theIxthian Artifactagenda will not affect the Creuss player’s units in a system with a beta wormhole (and no alpha wormhole), and vice versa.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Entanglement
--- CONTENT: The Creuss player’sQuantum Entanglementability applies to their units with theDeep Space Cannonability. Other players cannot useQuantum Entanglementto produce hits from a unit with theDeep Space Cannonability against the Creuss player’s units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Slipstream
--- CONTENT: Slipstreamdoes not apply to the Creuss Gate or to theHil Colish, or to gamma wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Creuss Gate
--- CONTENT: A frontier token is placed in the Creuss Gate system during setup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Creuss Gate
--- CONTENT: Both the Creuss Gate and the Creuss home system (in standard game board setups) are on the edge of the board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Creuss IFF(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may receive theCreuss IFFin a transaction during their turn. If received at the start of that player’s turn, that player may play it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Creuss IFF(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Any deal between the Creuss player and another player regarding where the wormhole tokens will be placed, if made before theCreuss IFFis exchanged, is non–binding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Creuss IFF(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: TheCreuss IFFmay be played even if the Creuss player has not researchedWormhole Generator.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Creuss IFF(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: TheCreuss IFFcannot place wormhole tokens in the home system of an eliminated player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Splicer(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Any wormhole may triggerDimensional Splicer, including the one produced by the ability of theHil Colish
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Splicer(Technology)
--- CONTENT: One hit will be produced even if the system contains multiple wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Splicer(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Creuss player chooses which ship the hit is assigned to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Splicer(Technology)
--- CONTENT: TheShields Holdingaction card may be used to cancel the hit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Dimensional Splicer(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The chosen ship may cancel the hit by using itsSustain Damageability, if present. A different ship with theSustain Damageability cannot do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Generator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: This ability is mandatory for the Creuss player in every status phase after it has been researched.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Generator(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Wormhole Generatorcannot place wormhole tokens in the home system of an eliminated player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Generator Ω(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Creuss player may move a wormhole token from the system it is in into the same system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Generator Ω(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Wormhole Generatorcannot place wormhole tokens in the home system of an eliminated player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If theHil Colishmoves first, then the Creuss player uses the new position of theHil Colishwhen determining if the active system may be reached by their other ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If theHil Colishmoves last, then it may move itself into (or through, if its move value is increased) the Creuss Gate or Creuss home system. Before it does so, the Creuss player’s other ships may move through the wormhole created by theHil Colish.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: The Creuss player must declare all ships that will moving before they move theHil Colishor their other ships. They then declare the path that the first ship(s) to move will travel along, and move those ship(s). They then declare the path that the other ship(s) to move will travel along, and move those ships. Any ships that were declared to move must, if it is possible to do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If theHil Colishmoves before or after other ships, it does not generate a secondSpace Cannon Offensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A unit with theDeep Space Cannonability may produce hits in systems adjacent to that unit via the delta wormhole in theHil Colish’s system. Most commonly, this will allow the Creuss player to target units in theHil Colish’s system from the space cannon rolls of units in their home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If an effect allows another player to move through a system that contains the Creuss player’s ships (such as theLight/Wave Deflectortechnology), that player may move through the delta wormhole in theHil Colish’s system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: During space combat involving theHil Colish, either player may retreat to another system containing a delta wormhole, if that system meets the other requirements for retreating.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Hil Colish(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: When theHil Colishretreats, it may retreat before or after the Creuss player’s other ships, but cannot retreat in such a way that would prevent the other ships from retreating to the same system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Emissary Taivra(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The Creuss player may use this ability to access the inactive wormhole nexus without a gamma wormhole. Moving ships into the wormhole nexus this way will cause it to flip.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Emissary Taivra(Agent)
--- CONTENT: A delta wormhole in the system (such as from theHil Colish) does not prevent this ability from being usable.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Emissary Taivra(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If this ability is used, the active system will be adjacent to systems with delta wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Emissary Taivra(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If a ship moves from the system containing the Ion Storm, it will not flip, unless the active player may move ships through the Ion Storm wormhole and chooses to do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Emissary Taivra(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The system must have a non–delta wormhole in it at the moment of activation. If a wormhole is placed in a system with no other wormholes using the ability of an Icarus Drive, then Emissary Taivra cannot be used during the same activation.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Sai Seravus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The fighters are placed one at a time, until either one has been placed for each ship with capacity that moved through a wormhole, or the capacity of the system is reached.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Sai Seravus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: This ability may be used whenever the Creuss player’s ships move, not just during the movement step of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Sai Seravus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: A ship may move out of a system and back into the same system during tactical action movement, if its move value is high enough. If the Creuss player does this with a ship with capacity, and moves in this manner via a wormhole, they may place a fighter, if possible.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Sai Seravus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: When the Creuss player moves a ship through a wormhole, ending in a system that contains an alpha or beta wormhole and unlocks Sai Seravus, they cannot apply its ability to that movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Riftwalker Meian — Singularity Reactor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any units and tokens on either system are moved with their system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Riftwalker Meian — Singularity Reactor(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Systems that comprise The Fracture and the Rebellion player’s home system cannot be swapped with other system tiles.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Icarus Drive(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Icarus Drive does not have to be in the activated system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Icarus Drive(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The wormhole token is placed in the system the Icarus Drive was in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Particle Synthesis(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Each wormhole in the system provides theProductionvalue and discount, even those of the same type.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Ghosts of Creuss
--- SECTION_ID: Particle Synthesis(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Creuss player moves theHil Colishinto a system, the Creuss player may use theProductionability of the associated delta wormhole during the production step of the same tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Units cannot use theBombardmentability against a planet that contains a unit that has thePlanetary Shieldability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: ThePlanetary Shieldability does not prevent a planet from being affected by theX–89 Bacterial Weapontechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: ThePlanetary Shieldability prevents an L1Z1X player from using theirHarrowfaction ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a war sun is in a system with any number of other players’ units that have thePlanetary Shieldability, those units are treated as if they do not have that ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A unit with thePlanetary Shieldability on a planet does not stop of the use of a unit’sBombardmentability on other planets in the same system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If thePlanetary Shieldability prevents the use of the the use of aBombardmentability, then the abilities of theX–89 Bacterial Weapon ΩorX–89 Bacterial Weapon ΩΩtechnologies cannot be used.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a war sun causes a unit to be treated as if it does not have aPlanetary Shieldability, that unit may still use the ability of theMagen Defense Grid ΩorMagen Defense Grid ΩΩtechnologies.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Planetary Shield (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a war sun causes a unit to be treated as if it does not have aPlanetary Shieldability, all units in that system with aBombardmentability may use it against the planet that unit is on.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Awaken
--- CONTENT: Only sleeper tokens present in the system when it is activated may be replaced with PDS.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Awaken
--- CONTENT: A sleeper token that is placed during theActivationstep, most commonly by using theScanlink Drone Networktechnology and theTerragenesisability, cannot be replaced via theAwakenability during the same tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Awaken
--- CONTENT: If the Ul player wishes to place a PDS, but there are none left in their reinforcements, they may remove a PDS from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. The PDS will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Awaken
--- CONTENT: If the Ul player places a PDS on a planet controlled by another player, and that player does not have any ground forces on that planet, the Ul player will destroy all of the other player’s structures, and gain control of that planet immediately. If the other player has ground forces, then a ground combat will be resolved during theInvasionstep of the tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Coalescence
--- CONTENT: Units placed on planets via theAwakenability are not committed. They cannot be assigned hits during theSpace Cannon Defensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Coalescence
--- CONTENT: If the Ul player’s units exist in the same location as another player’s units, no game effect can prevent the combat from occuring, including effects that end the Ul player’s turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Coalescence
--- CONTENT: If another player plays the Ul player’sCeasefirepromissory note, the Ul player may still place units into the active system using their flagship orAwakenability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Coalescence
--- CONTENT: Only the active player may use theBombardmentability of their units during an invasion. As such, any ships in the active system will be unable to use theirBombardmentability during the Ul player’s turn, unless they belong to the Ul player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Terraform(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Once played,Terraformis never returned to the Ul player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Terraform(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Once played,Terraformcounts as being in the play area of the player who controls the planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Terraform(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a planet has multiple traits, the player exploring the planet chooses which of the corresponding exploration decks to draw from.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hel–Titan(Unit)
--- CONTENT: The Ul player cannot use the secondary ability of theWarfarestrategy card to use theProductionability of a Hel–Titan.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hel–Titan(Unit)
--- CONTENT: When multiple units use theirProductionability, theProductionvalue is pooled. As such, if the Ul player has two Hel–Titans in a system, they may produce two infantry or two fighters for one resource, rather than two resources.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hel–Titan(Unit)
--- CONTENT: Effects that remove ground forces, and then place them on the game board without transporting them, such as theDecoy Operationaction card or theTransit Diodestechnology, may be used on a Hel–Titan.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hel–Titan(Unit)
--- CONTENT: Effects that move ground forces, such as theGhost Squadaction card or the ability of the N’orr player’s commander, G’hom Sek’kus, (via theAlliancepromissory note), cannot be used to move a Hel–Titan to another planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hel–Titan(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If a player is able to ignorePlanetary Shield, then Hel–Titan are eligible units to assign any hits produced by a bombardment roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Ouranos(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Only PDS present in the system when it is activated may be replaced with theOuranos.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Ouranos(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A PDS that is placed during the activation step, most commonly by using theAwakenability, cannot be replaced with theOuranosduring the same tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Tellurian(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Cancelling a hit cannot be used to stop an effect that directly destroys a unit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Tungstantus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The trade good may be spent on the units produced by theProductionability that triggered Tungstantus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Tungstantus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Other effects that produce units without a unit using itsProductionability will not trigger Tungstantus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Ul the Progenitor — Geoform(Hero)
--- CONTENT: TheSpace Cannonability is controlled by whichever player controls Elysium.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hecatoncheires(Mech)
--- CONTENT: When the Ul player would place multiple PDS during a single step, they may resolve aDeployability to place one Hecatoncheires for any or all of those PDS.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hecatoncheires(Mech)
--- CONTENT: ADeployability may only be resolved for units in a player’s reinforcements. If all four of the Hecatoncheires are already on the board, no Hecatoncheires may be deployed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hecatoncheires(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Ul player cannot place a PDS on a planet that already has two of their PDS on it. As such, they are unable to place a Hecatoncheires on a planet with two of their PDS using itsDeployability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Hecatoncheires(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Ul player must have at least one PDS in their reinforcements to place in order to use theDeployability of a Hecatoncheires. However, when they would place a PDS, they may remove a PDS from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and put it in their reinforcements. They may then use theDeployability of a Hecatoncheires.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Slumberstate Computing(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Ul player does not have to be neighbors with the player that agrees to have a sleeper token placed on their planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Titans of Ul
--- SECTION_ID: Slumberstate Computing(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Agreeing to have a sleeper token placed is not in and of itself a transaction, though the deal may involve a transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a component type is depleted during the game, players obey the following rules:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Dice: Dice are limitless. If a player needs to roll more dice than the game provides, that player should roll as many as possible, record the results, and then reroll dice as necessary.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Tokens: Tokens are limited to those included in the game, except for the following:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If any of the above tokens are depleted, players can use a suitable substitute, such as a coin or bead.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Units: Units are limited to those included in the game, except for fighters and ground forces.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Cards: When a deck is depleted, players shuffle the deck’s discard pile and place it facedown to create a new deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: As each player only has ten plastic fighter figures and twelve plastic infantry figures, a player cannot have fighters in more than ten systems, and cannot have infantry on more than twelve planets or being carried in more than twelve space areas, or any combination thereof.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Players may also swap infantry and fighter plastic pieces for tokens at any time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Players may swap between three value tokens and one value tokens as desired.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may only resolve a deploy ability to place a unit that is in their reinforcements. A player cannot remove a unit from the board to use its deploy ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Each faction has sixteen command and seventeen control tokens included in the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a discard pile is shuffled to form a new deck, any cards that have been purged are not included.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player removes a unit in order to place it, because they have none of that unit type in their reinforcements, that unit is placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Limitations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is instructed to “replace” one unit with another, and they have none of the replacement unit type in their reinforcements, they may remove a unit of that type from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that unit instead.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Ground Forces
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ground force is a type of unit. All infantry and mech units in the game are ground forces. Some races have unique infantry units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Ground Forces
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Ground forces are always on planets, in a space area with ships that have capacity values, or being transported by those ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Ground Forces
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Ground forces being transported by a ship are placed in a system’s space area along with the ship that is transporting them.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Ground Forces
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There is no limit to the number of ground forces a player can have on a planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding breakthroughs.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A breakthrough is a faction specific card. Players start the game without their faction’s breakthrough.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A breakthrough is commonly gained through an expedition, or the Thunder’s Edge legendary planet ability card. There are other game effects that can gain a player their faction’s breakthrough.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a player gains their faction’s breakthrough, they perform a breakthrough roll, which may cause The Fracture to enter play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A breakthrough has 1 or more abilities, and a synergy (other than for the Nekro player).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about a breakthrough of a specific faction, see that faction’s page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Expedition
##################################################

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Breakthroughs

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The fleet pool is an area of a player’s command sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The number of command tokens in a player’s fleet pool indicates the maximum number of non–fighter ships that a player can have in a system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players place command tokens in their fleet pools with the ship silhouette faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If at any time the number of a player’s non–fighter ships in a system exceeds the number of tokens in that player’s fleet pool, they choose and remove excess ships in that system, returning those units to their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players do not spend command tokens from this pool unless a game effect specifically allows it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Fighters and ground forces do not count towards capacity during combat. As such, any number of Fighter II may be in a system during combat, regardless of capacity and fleet pool. This will usually only be caused by effects that place units in a system during combat. When combat ends however, units will need to be removed to meet capacity and fleet pool requirements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Ships may be moved into, produced in or placed in a system even if doing so would exceed the fleet pool limit. However, some of those ships must immediately be removed to satisfy the limit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: During movement, a ship may move through a system regardless of how many ships are in that system relative to the fleet pool limit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Capacity
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Command Sheet
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Command Tokens
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Ships
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fleet Pool
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: System Tiles
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the status phase, players score objectives and prepare for the next game round. To resolve the status phase, players perform the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – Score Objectives: Following initiative order, each player may score up to one public objective and one secret objective that can be fulfilled during the status phase. To score an objective, a player must fulfill the requirements on the card; if that player does, they gain a number of victory points indicated on the card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Reveal Public Objective: The speaker reveals an unrevealed public objective card by flipping that card faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 3 – Draw Action Cards: Following initiative order, each player draws one action card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 4 – Remove Command Tokens: Each player removes all of their command tokens from the game board. Each player returns each removed token to their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 5 – Gain and Redistribute Command Tokens: Each player gains two command tokens. A player takes each gained token from their reinforcements. Then, each player can redistribute each command token on their command sheet, including the two they just gained, among their strategy, tactic, and fleet pools.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 6 – Ready Cards: Each player readies all of their exhausted cards, including strategy cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 7 – Repair Units: Each player repairs all of their damaged units by turning those units upright.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 8 – Return Strategy Cards: Each player returns their strategy card to the common play area. Then, if a player has removed the custodians token from Mecatol Rex, the game round continues to the agenda phase. Otherwise, a new game round begins with the strategy phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot score public objectives if that player does not control each planet in their home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If there are few cards remaining in the action card deck, they will be dealt out first to the players lowest in initiative order. After those players have discarded down to their seven card hand limit, if necessary, the discard pile will be shuffled to form a new deck. The remaining players (including the player who received the last action card from the previous deck, if applicable) will then be dealt their action cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: All damaged units will be repaired, even if a game effect has caused those units to no longer have theSustain Damageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Action Cards
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Agenda Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Custodians Token
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Command Tokens
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Game Round
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Status Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics

##################################################

--- CONTENT: Objective Cards
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Legendary planets grant the player that controls them unique, planet–specific abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A legendary planet is indicated by the legendary planet icon.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player gains control of a legendary planet, they also place its legendary planet ability card in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can use the abilities on the legendary planet ability cards in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a legendary planet’s planet card is purged, its corresponding legendary planet ability card is also purged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to resolve theImperial Arms Vaultability of Hope’s End, but they have no mechs left in their reinforcements, they may remove a mech from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. The mech will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an effect instructs a player to “end your turn”, that player may still resolve any “at the end of your turn” abilities, including those of legendary planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may resolve multiple legendary planet abilities at the end of a single turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Legendary planet ability cards exhaust and ready independently from their respective planet card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: An ability that readies a plannet cannot be used to ready a legendary planet ability card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A legendary planet ability card will ready in the status phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Mecatol Rex is not a legendary planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For the system that contains Malice, see thewormhole nexus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Control
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Exhausted
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Legendary Planets
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Hyperlanes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Hyperlanes are tiles that are used in some game board setups to create adjacency of system tiles that are not touching each other.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Hyperlanes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Systems that are connected by lines drawn across one or more hyperlane tiles are adjacent for all purposes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Hyperlanes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Hyperlane tiles are not systems. They cannot have units on them and they cannot be targets for effects or abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Hyperlanes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the edge of a system tile is touching a hyperlane tile, that edge does not cause that system tile to be on the edge of the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Hyperlanes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: “Adjacent for all purposes” includes:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Hyperlanes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Hyperlanes on the same tile that converge at a point on the tile edge are not connected. For example, with the “Five–Player Galaxy Setup (With Hyperlanes)” in theProphecy of KingsMap Appendix, the hyperlanes on tile 87A do not connect tiles 39 and 63, and the hyperlanes on tile 88A do not connect tiles 41 and 80.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Voidborn
--- CONTENT: This effect also applies outside theMovementstep.

--- SECTION_ID: Voidborn
--- CONTENT: The Empyrean player treats nebulae as nebulae and as anomalies for all other game purposes.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Aetherpassage
--- CONTENT: The Empyrean player does not decide to use this ability until after the other player has activated a system. Any deal made to use this ability before the system has been activated is non–binding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Blood Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Both players must cast at least one vote to trigger the additional votes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Blood Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Blood Pacthas no effect while it is in a player’s hand.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Blood Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Blood Pactis returned when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the Empyrean player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Blood Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Activating a system containing only the Empyrean player’s structures will still causeBlood Pactto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Blood Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the Empyrean player’s units (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeBlood Pactto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dark Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player cannot have more commodities than their commodity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dark Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If the Empyrean player plays a player’sTrade Agreementpromissory note, this will count for that player giving the Empyrean player all their commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dark Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The trade goods gained fromDark Pactare gained simultaneously with the commodities transacted between the two players. As a pair of players is limited to one transaction per turn (which must involve the active player) or per agenda, the two players cannot then perform a transaction for these trade goods on the same turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dark Pact(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: As the trade goods fromDark Pactare gained simultaneously with any commodities and/or trade goods transacted, the Mentak player may only use theirPillageability on each player once perDark Pacttransaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Aetherstream(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A system is not adjacent to itself. If a system with an anomaly is activated,Aetherstreamwill not give any ships +1 to their move value, unless that system is adjacent to another anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Voidwatch(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The active player chooses which promissory note they give the Empyrean player.
