### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dynamo(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A unit may only use itsSustain Damageability once in eachAssign Hitsstep, even if it is repaired.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dynamo(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A unit that becomes damaged without using itsSustain Damageability will not trigger this effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dynamo(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A player may play aDirect Hitaction card during the same timing window as this ability. If they do so, the ship is destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Dynamo(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Each unit using itsSustain Damageability creates a separate timing window. As such, any excess influence used to repair a ship is wasted, and cannot be used to repair a different ship.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Acamar(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Exhausting Acamar is a cost. Acamar cannot be used if it is exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Acamar(Agent)
--- CONTENT: A system that contains a planet destroyed by theStellar Converterrelic, and no other planets, is considered to contain no planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Xuange(Commander)
--- CONTENT: While the agenda phase and the Hacan player’sTrade Convoyspromissory note allow a player to resolve transactions with all other players, they do not make that player neighbors with all other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Xuange(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Any movement of ships can trigger this ability, not just movement during theMove Shipsstep of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Xuange(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Empyrean player becomes neighbors with all players when the final player moves ships into a system containing one of the Empyrean player’s command tokens, Xuange will unlock, but the Empyrean player will not be able to resolve its ability from that movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Xuange(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Empyrean player moves a ship into a system containing one of the Saar player’s Floating Factories, and no other ships, that Floating Factory will by blockaded and destroyed before the Empyrean player can unlock Xuange. If the Empyrean and Saar players are not neighbors in any other way, then Xuange will not unlock.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Conservator Procyon — Multiverse Shift(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Empyrean player chooses the order of exploration.

--- CONTENT: A system that contains a planet destroyed by theStellar Converterrelic, and no other planets, is considered to contain no planets.Multiverse Shiftwill place a frontier token in such a system.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Conservator Procyon — Multiverse Shift(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If The Fracture is in play when the Empyrean player resolvesMultiverse Shift, frontier tokens will be placed in the systems in The Fracture that do not contain a planet, and then the Empyrean player will explore those tokens if they have ships present.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: This effect may cancel aSabotageaction card.

--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Watcher must be adjacent to the other player’s units during the timing window when the action card is played in order to cancel it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If a player has a second copy of an action card, they may play it if the first was cancelled by a Watcher.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If an action card is cancelled by a Watcher, no costs are paid.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: A player playing an action card announces the following before a Watcher may be triggered:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: Any dice are rolled and any cards are drawn only after the Empyrean player has declined to remove a Watcher.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If an action card instructs a player to research a technology, that player need not announce what technology they are researching until the Empyrean player has declined to remove a Watcher.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If an action card is played that will have an effect later, such as a rider, that card may only be cancelled by a Watcher when it is originally played.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Watcher(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If the action card that was cancelled by a Watcher was to be used to perform a component action, the active player must perform a different action, or pass.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Empyrean
--- SECTION_ID: Void Tether(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Other players treat the systems that share the border with the Void Tether token as not being adjacent for all game effects. The Empyrean player continues to treat them as adjacent.

--- SECTION_ID: Valkyrie Particle Weave(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the opponent produces a hit,Valkyrie Particle Weavemandatorily produces a hit.

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Exotrireme(Unit)
--- CONTENT: When resolving the ability of an Exotrireme II, the N’orr player chooses which ships are destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Exotrireme(Unit)
--- CONTENT: Effects that cancel hits, such as theSustain Damageability, cannot be used to prevent ships from being destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Exotrireme(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If a player retreats, the N’orr player will be unable to use the ability of an Exotrireme II to destroy an opponent’s ship.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Exotrireme(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If the N’orr player is in a combat with the Yin player, then the two players will alternate when resolving end of combat round abilities, starting with the attacker.

--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Planets in the home system of an eliminated player will not contribute to unlocking G’hom Sek’kus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: This ability allows the N’orr player to commit ground forces to a planet even if they have no ships in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: TheParleyaction card will place the committed ground forces in the space area of the active system. If the N’orr player does not have enough capacity in the space area for the extra ground forces, including zero capacity, they will have to remove fighters and ground forces to meet capacity limits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The N’orr player may commit up to one ground force from each eligible planet during eachInvasionstep, regardless of the number of planets they are committing ground forces to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The N’orr player may only commit ground forces as the active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Only the active player may use theBombardmentability of their units during an invasion. As such, any ships in the active system will be unable to use theirBombardmentability unless they belong to the N’orr player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Another player may still produce hits against the N’orr player’s ground forces committed using G’hom Sek’kus during theSpace Cannon Defensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The N’orr player must legally be able to move into the destination system in order to commit ground forces with G’hom Sek’kus
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The N’orr player may use this ability to commit ground forces to any planet in the active system, regardless of who, if anyone, controls it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the N’orr player purges theDominus Orbrelic during theMovementstep of a tactical action, they may use G’hom Sek’kus to commit ground forces from systems that contain their command tokens during that tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: TheCommit Ground Forcesstep is entirely resolved before theEstablish Controlstep (with other steps between). When the N’orr player gains control of their fifth non–home system planet, an unlocks G’hom Sek’kus, they cannot then use G’hom Sek’kus to commit additional ground forces during that tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: G’hom Sek’kus(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Ground forces cannot be committed to a planet if it has theDemilitarized Zoneexploration card attached.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Sh’val, Harbinger — Tekklar Conditioning(Hero)
--- CONTENT: TheParleyaction card will place the committed ground forces in the space area of the active system. As the N’orr player will not have enough capacity in the space area for their ground forces, they will have to remove all ground forces from that planet, that are now in the space area of that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Sh’val, Harbinger — Tekklar Conditioning(Hero)
--- CONTENT: TheSpace Cannon Offense,Space CombatandBombardmentsteps are skipped.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Sh’val, Harbinger — Tekklar Conditioning(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Another player may still produce hits against the N’orr player’s ground forces committed usingTekklar Conditioningduring theSpace Cannon Defensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sardakk N’orr
--- SECTION_ID: Sh’val, Harbinger — Tekklar Conditioning(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that trigger “after a player moves ships…” or similar cannot be used followingTekklar Conditioning.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: N’orr Supremacy(Breakthrough)

### RULE_SOURCE: Destroyed
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Various game effects can cause a unit to be destroyed. When a player’s unit is destroyed, it is removed from the game board and returned to their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Destroyed
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player assigns hits that were produced against their units, that player chooses a number of their units to be destroyed equal to the number of hits produced against those units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Destroyed
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player’s unit is removed from the board by a game effect, it is not treated as being destroyed; effects that trigger when a unit is destroyed are not triggered.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit with theBombardmentability may be able to destroy another player’s ground forces during an invasion. During theBombardmentstep, players perform the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1– The active player chooses which planet each of their units that has aBombardmentability will bombard. Then, that player rolls dice for each of those units; this is called a bombardment roll. A hit is produced for each die roll that is equal to or greater than the unit’sBombardmentvalue.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2– The player who controls the planet that is being bombarded chooses and destroys one of their ground forces on that planet for each hit result the bombardment roll produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: TheBombardmentstep happens outside of combat. No combat effects may affect a bombardment roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Mechs may use theirSustain Damageability to cancel a hit produced by a bombardment roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Only the active player may bombard. Usually, but not always, only the active player will have ships in the system during an invasion.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes aboutHarrow, see theL1Z1X faction notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The “0” side of the d10 represents a result of 10.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A single planet must be chosen for each unit with theBombardmentability; any hits generated by that unit will be assigned to units on that planet. For example, when a war sun rolls for itsBombardmentability, all three dice must be rolled to produce hits against units on a single planet; they can not be split between two or more planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may choose not to use theBombardmentabilities of their units during their tactical actions. However, if they choose to use theBombardmentability, they must use theBombardmentability of each unit in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Bombardment (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Destroyed

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some systems contain wormholes. Systems that contain identical wormholes are adjacent.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There are two basic types of wormholes: alpha and beta.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player has a PDS unit upgrade technology, they can use theSpace Cannonabilities of their PDS units through wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can be neighbors and perform transactions through wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There are two advanced types of wormhole: delta and gamma. These wormholes follow all other wormhole rules.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A system with a wormhole is not an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a system contains multiple wormholes of the same type, those are treated as separate wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A system cannot be adjacent to itself, even if it has multiple wormholes in it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player chooses the path of adjacent systems each ship moves through during movement. If two systems on that path are adjacent because of a wormhole, that ship moves through that wormhole.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For additional information on how the Creuss interact with wormholes, seetheir faction notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Adjacency
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Neighbors
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: System Tiles
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormholes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Wormhole Nexus
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Scavenge
--- CONTENT: If the Saar player gains control of multiple planets during one invasion, the trade goods are gained one at a time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Scavenge
--- CONTENT: When the Saar player gains control of a planet that is not already controlled by another player, they will explore it before gaining the trade good from this ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Ragh’s Call(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: PlayingRagh’s Callwill prevent ground combat from occurring on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Ragh’s Call(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Any PDS on the planet remain. They might produce hits during theSpace Cannon Defensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Ragh’s Call(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: All of the Saar player’s ground forces must be placed on the same planet.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Ragh’s Call(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Any damaged mechs remain damaged.

--- CONTENT: A unit may be produced on each of the Saar player’s turns;Chaos Mappingis not exhausted.

--- SECTION_ID: Chaos Mapping(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A player may still use abilities such as action cards orDeep Space Cannonthat affect the Saar player’s units located in asteroid fields.

--- SECTION_ID: Chaos Mapping(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If an asteroid field contains only non–ship units belonging to the Saar player, it may still be activated by other players.

--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: A floating Factory does not count towards the Saar player’s fleet pool.

--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)

--- CONTENT: Hits produced by space cannon rolls cannot be assigned to a Floating Factory.

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: A Floating Factory moving through or out of a gravity rift must roll for removal. It will receive the +1 to its movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If the Saar player announces a retreat during a space combat, but all their ships are destroyed that round, any Floating Factories in that system are destroyed without retreating.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If the Saar player has their last ship destroyed during combat by aDirect Hitaction card, a Floating Factory in the system will be blockaded and destroyed, even if the Saar player produced enough hits to destroy their opponent’s remaining ships during that round of combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If, at the end of the combat, the Saar player has no ships, an their opponent has only fighters, then any Floating Factories in the system will be blockaded, and thus destroyed, before the fighters are removed due to lack of capacity.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If an effect allows a Floating Factory to move through a system that contains another player’s ships (such as theLight/Wave Deflectorstechnology), it will not be blockaded in systems it moves through.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Clan of Saar
--- SECTION_ID: Floating Factory(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If a Floating Factory is in a system that contains none of the Saar player’s ships, and another player moves ships into that system, the Floating Factory is immediately destroyed.

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheLeadershipstrategy card allows players to gain command tokens. This card’s initiative value is “1”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has theLeadershipstrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on theLeadershipstrategy card, the active player gains three command tokens. Then, that player can spend any amount of their influence to gain one command token for every three influence they spend.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theLeadershipstrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend any amount of influence to gain one command token for every three influence they spend.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player gains command tokens, that player places each token on their command sheet in the pool of their choice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The secondary ability ofLeadershipdoes not require a player to spend a strategy token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Leadership (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may spend one or two more influence than the amount necessary for the tokens they gain; however, this influence is wasted.

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A fighter token functions as a plastic fighter unit for all game purposes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When producing a fighter unit, a player can use a fighter token from the supply instead of a plastic piece.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can replace their plastic fighters with tokens at any time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player ever has a fighter token in a system that does not contain one of their plastic fighters, that player must replace it with a plastic fighter from their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Fighter tokens come in values of one and three. A player can swap between these tokens as necessary.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: As each player only has ten plastic fighter figures, a player cannot have fighters in more than ten systems.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Players may also swap fighter tokens for plastic pieces at any time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Fighter tokens are not component limited.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will have any unaccompanied fighter tokens removed, instead of destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Component Limitations
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Fighter Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Infantry Tokens
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Producing Units
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Purge
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Purge is a cost that permanently removes a component from the game. If an ability requires that its component is purged, that component can only be used once per game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Purge
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an ability instructs a player to purge a component, that component is removed from the game and returned to the box.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Purge
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Purged components cannot be used or otherwise returned to the game by any means.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Purge
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player is instructed to purge a component, that component is purged even if its ability was only partially resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: An infantry token functions as a plastic infantry unit for all game purposes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When producing an infantry unit, a player can use an infantry token from the supply instead of a plastic piece.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can replace their plastic infantry with tokens at any time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player ever has an infantry token on a planet that does not contain one of their plastic infantry or in the space area of a system that does not contain one of their plastic infantry, that player must replace it with one of their plastic infantry from their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Infantry tokens come in values of one and three. A player can swap between these tokens as necessary.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: As each player only has twelve plastic infantry figures, a player cannot have infantry on more than twelve planets or being transported in more than twelve space areas, or any combination thereof.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Players may also swap infantry tokens for plastic pieces at any time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Infantry tokens are not component limited.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may remove a plastic infantry figure from a planet or space area, along with any accompanying infantry tokens, if doing so allows them to swap it into the active system and allows them to commit ground forces to and fight ground combats on multiple planets during theInvasionstep of the tactical action in that system when they could otherwise not do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Infantry Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will have any unaccompanied infantry tokens removed, instead of destroyed.

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A component action is a type of action that a player can perform during their turn of an action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Component actions can be found on various game components, including action cards, technology cards, leaders, exploration cards, relics, promissory notes, and faction sheets. Each component action is indicated by an “Action” header.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To perform a component action, a player reads the action’s text and follows the instructions as described.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A component action cannot be performed if its ability cannot be completely resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a component action is canceled, it does not use that player’s action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Action cards without the “Action” header are not used to perform component actions.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Component Action
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Political Data Nexus(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Effects from agenda outcomes that occur “at the start of the next strategy phase” will still occur.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Political Data Nexus Ω(Hero)
--- CONTENT: During the status phase, public and secret objectives are scored simultaneously. The Xxcha player cannot score a public objective, unlock Xxekir Grom, and then usePolitical Data Nexus Ωin order to score a secret objective, or vice versa.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Political Data Nexus Ω(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The combined value may be spent as either influence or resources, not both, and cannot be split between the two.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Political Data Nexus Ω(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Political Data Nexus Ωonly changes the spendable influence and resources. It does not change the value for any other game effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Political Data Nexus Ω(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The resource value of a planet will be added to its influence value when the Xxcha player casts votes during the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Planetary Defense Nexus ΩΩ(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The units may be placed on a readied planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Xxekir Grom — Planetary Defense Nexus ΩΩ(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Multiple units may be placed on the same planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Indomitus(Mech)
--- CONTENT: During theSpace Cannon Offensesupstep of a tactical action, the active player resolves theSpace Cannonabilities of their units first. If the Xxcha player is not the active player, and their ships are removed by another player’s space cannon roll, they must immediately remove units to meet their capacity limit. They will not resolve theSpace Cannonabilities of any of their removed mechs.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Indomitus(Mech)
--- CONTENT: During theSpace Cannon Defensesubstep of a tactical action, only non–active players can use theSpace Cannonability of their units. The Xxcha player cannot use theSpace Cannonability of their mechs immediately after committing them to a planet against units owned by that planet’s controller.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Archon’s Gift(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: A source of both influence and resources, such as a planet, may be spent for one or the other, but not both.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Archon’s Gift(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: A source of both influence or resources, such as a planet, may be spent as one or the other, but cannot be split to be spent as both.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Xxcha Kingdom
--- SECTION_ID: Archon’s Gift(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Archon’s Giftonly changes how a planet’s influence and resources may be spent. It does not change the value for any other game effect.

### RULE_SOURCE: Combat (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Combat is an attribute of some units that is presented on faction sheets and unit upgrade technology cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Combat (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During combat, if a unit’s combat roll produces a result equal to or greater than its combat value, it produces a hit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Combat (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a unit’s combat value contains two or more burst icons, instead of rolling a single die, the player rolls one die for each burst icon when making that unit’s combat rolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Combat (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The “0” side of the d10 represents a result of 10.

--- SECTION_ID: Pillage
--- CONTENT: Effects that force players to give objects to other players are not transactions.

--- CONTENT: If the Creuss player has units or controls planets in a system with an alpha wormhole, and the Mentak player has units or controls planets in a system with a beta wormhole, or vice versa, then the Creuss player and Mentak player are neighbors. The Mentak player may thus use theirPillageability against the Creuss player.

--- SECTION_ID: Pillage

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mentak Coalition
--- SECTION_ID: Pillage
--- CONTENT: If a game effect instructs a player to convert their commodities to trade goods, that player does not gain any trade goods from that effect. The Mentak player cannot use theirPillageability for those trade goods.

--- SECTION_ID: Pillage

As such, the Mentak player may place a ship that was destroyed in the same round of combat, if they destroyed one of their opponent’s ships of the same type, even if they had none of that ship type in their reinforcements.

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some units have theSustain Damageability. Immediately before a player assigns hits to their units, that player can use theSustain Damageability of any of their units in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: For eachSustain Damageability that a player uses, one hit produced by another player’s units is canceled. Then, each unit using this ability is placed on its side to indicate that it is damaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A damaged unit does not have reduced capabilities and is functionally the same as an undamaged unit, except that it cannot use theSustain Damageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A damaged unit cannot use theSustain Damageability until it is repaired during the status phase or by another game effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit can use itsSustain Damageability any time a hit is produced against it. This includes hits produced during combat and from unit abilities such as theSpace Cannonability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheSustain Damageability cannot be used to cancel an effect that directly destroys a unit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Sustain Damage
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The Barony of Letnev’sNon–Euclidean Shieldingfaction technology allows the Letnev player’s units with theSustain Damageability to cancel up to two hits instead of one.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Capacity is an attribute of some units that is presented on faction sheets and unit upgrade technology cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit’s capacity value indicates the maximum combined number of fighters and ground forces that it can transport.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The combined capacity values of a player’s ships in a system determine the number of fighters and ground forces that player can have in that system’s space area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player has more fighters and ground forces in the space area of a system than the total capacity of that player’s ships in that system, that player must remove the excess units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Fighters and ground forces are not assigned to specific ships, except while they are being transported.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player moves more fighters and/or ground forces into a system containing another player’s ships, capacity limits must be met before proceeding to theSpace Cannon Offensesubstep or theSpace Combatstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a ship with capacity is destroyed during theSpace Cannon Offensestep, capacity limits must be met before space combat starts.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Capacity is checked after the winner of a space combat is determined. As such, it is possible to win a space combat with only fighters remaining, before removing those fighters due to lack of capacity.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship cannot pick up more units from a planet than it has capacity. However, a ship may pick up any units (including zero) in a system as it transports, even if doing so would cause units to be removed due to capacity limits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Fleet Pool
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capacity (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Space Combat
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Transport

### RULE_SOURCE: Deploy
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some units have deploy abilities. Deploy abilities are indicated by theDeployheader and provide the means to place specific units on the game board without producing them as normal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deploy
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can use a unit’sDeployability when the ability’s conditions are met to place that unit on the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deploy
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can only resolve aDeployability to place a unit that is in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deploy
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit’sDeployability can be resolved only once per timing window.

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A trade good represents a player’s buying and trading power beyond their planet’s raw resources.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Trade goods and commodities are represented by opposite sides of the same token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player gains a trade good, they take a trade good token from the supply and place it on the trade good area on their command sheet, making sure the trade good side is faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can spend trade goods at any time during the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can spend a trade good in one of the following ways:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can exchange their trade goods with other players during a transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player receives a commodity token from another player, the player who received that token places it in their trade good area with the trade good side of the token faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade Goods
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Trade good tokens come in values of one and three. A player can swap between these tokens as necessary.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Command tokens are a currency that players use to perform actions and expand their fleets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player begins the game with eight tokens on their command sheet: three in their tactic pool, three in their fleet pool, and two in their strategy pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player gains a command token, they choose which of their three pools to place it in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player is limited by the amount of command tokens in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, a player can perform a tactical action by spending a command token from their tactic pool; they place the command token in a system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a player performs a strategic action during the action phase, each other player can resolve the secondary ability of that strategy card by spending a command token from their strategy pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a game effect would place a player’s command token in a system where they already have one, they place the token in their reinforcements instead. Any effects that resolve by placing that token are resolved as normal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Tokens
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Command Sheet
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Fleet Pool
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Leadership
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit is represented by a plastic figure.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There are three types of units: ships, ground forces, and structures.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each color of plastic comes with the following units:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Units exist either on the game board or in a player’s reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an effect allows a player produce a ship of a specific type, then factional variations do not prevent that player from producing that type of ship.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Units are component limited.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A transaction is a way for a player to exchange commodities, trade goods, promissory notes, and relic fragments.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the active player’s turn, they may resolve up to one transaction with each of their neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve a transaction, a player gives any number of trade goods and commodities and up to one promissory note to a neighbor in exchange for any number of trade goods, commodities, and relic fragments, and up to one promissory note.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can exchange commodities, trade goods, promissory notes, and relic fragments, but cannot exchange other types of cards or tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A transaction does not have to be even. A player may exchange components of unequal value or give components without receiving something in return.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can resolve a transaction as part of a deal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: While resolvingeachagenda during the agenda phase, a player may perform one transaction with each other player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Relic fragments may be traded. Relics themselves cannot be.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Captured units may be returned to the player that originally owned them as part of a transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player becomes neighbors with another player on their turn, they may then perform a transaction with that player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player may perform multiple actions on their turn, they may still only resolve one transaction with each of their neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an agenda is discarded and replaced with another, players who resolved a transaction during the discarded agenda may resolve another transaction during the replacement agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Active Player
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Agenda Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transactions
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Capture
##################################################

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can move their ships by resolving a tactical action during the action phase. Additionally, some abilities can move a unit outside of the tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ship’s move value is presented along with its other attributes on faction sheets and unit upgrade technology cards. This value indicates the distance from its current system that a ship can move.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – Move Ships: A player can move any number of their eligible ships into the active system, obeying the following rules:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a ship with a capacity value moves or is moved, it may transport ground forces and fighters.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The active player declares which of their ships are moving before any ships move. Those ships arrive in the active system simultaneously.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Space Cannon Offense: After theMove Shipsstep, players can use theSpace Cannonabilities of their units in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an ability moves a unit outside of theMovementstep of a tactical action, players follow the rules specified by that ability; neither a unit’s move value nor the rules specified above apply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When an effect moves a unit to an adjacent system, modifying that unit’s move value will have no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: An ability may move a player’s ship out of a system containing one of the player’s faction’s command tokens. However, the transport rules prevent a player’s units from being transported from systems containing one of that player’s command tokens, other than the active system. An ability that moves a player’s ship must also explicitly allow it to transport units from non–active systems containing that player’s faction’s command token for it to be able to do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship that can both move and be transported (i.e. Fighter II) cannot do both by “meeting” a ship with capacity partway through a tactical action movement, as all movement is simultaneous.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Ships only move “into” the destination system. A ship may move “through” other systems.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Fighters alone will block other player’s ships from moving through that system, whether they are accompanied by a Space Dock or they are Fighters II.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Movement
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Active System
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Adjacency
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Anomalies
