### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding expeditions.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may perform an expedition, which will unlock their breakthrough, and potentially put The Fracture and/or Thunder’s Edge into play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: At the end of their turn, a player may perform an expedition. To do so they choose one of the unclaimed slices on the expedition token. They pay the indicated cost, and place one of their control tokens in the indicated area to claim it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a player performs an expedition, they gain their faction’s breakthrough if they do not already have it. This will trigger a breakthrough roll to possibly place The Fracture into play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The costs to perform an expedition are, in clockwise order from the top of the expedition token:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: One player may claim multiple slices. A single slice cannot be claimed multiple times (neither by the same or different players).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Once the sixth and final slice has been claimed, Thunder’s Edge will enter play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player has not gained their breakthrough by the time Thunder’s Edge is placed, they will be unable to gain their breakthrough by performing an expedition.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Breakthroughs
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Expeditions
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: The Fracture
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Scheming
--- CONTENT: No other abilities may resolve until the Yssaril player has discarded the action card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Scheming
--- CONTENT: Schemingapplies whenever the Yssaril player draws action cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Scheming
--- CONTENT: The Yssaril player will draw only one additional action card, regardless of how many action cards they are instructed to draw.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Scheming
--- CONTENT: The discarded action card may be any card in the Yssaril player’s hand; it does not have to be one of the cards they just drew.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Scheming
--- CONTENT: Effects that give the Yssaril player action cards without drawing them, such asThe Codexrelic or theReverse Engineeraction card, will not triggerScheming.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Crafty
--- CONTENT: The effect of theExecutive Sanctionslaw does not affect the Yssaril player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Spy Net(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The player that playsSpy Netmust look at the Yssaril player’s hand of action cards. They do not have to read or memorize what they look at.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Spy Net(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may receiveSpy Netin a transaction during their turn. If received at the start of that player’s turn, that player may play it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Spy Net(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Any deal between the Yssaril player and another player regarding which action card will be chosen, if made beforeSpy Netis exchanged, is non–binding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Mageon Implants(Technology)
--- CONTENT: When resolvingMageon Implants, the Yssaril player is not drawing a card. As such,Schemingwill not trigger.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Mageon Implants(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Yssaril player must target a player with at least one action card in their hand when they resolveMageon Implants.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Mageon Implants(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Yssaril player cannot show the other player’s hand of action cards to any other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Transparasteel Plating(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Other players may resolve faction abilities, leader abilities or technology abilities during the Yssaril player’s turns.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Y’sia Y’ssrila(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the Yssaril player owns theLight/Wave Deflectortechnology, it will have no additional effect on theY’sia Y’ssrila
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Yssaril player duplicates an agent that allows a unit to roll an additional die, and both the duplicated agent and Ssruu target the same unit, that unit will roll two additional dice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Yssaril player duplicates the Saar player’s Captain Mendosa agent, they may do so before or after other effects are used to modify any ship’s move value. This includes the Saar player’s Captain Mendosa agent effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If both the Yssaril player and the Vuil’raith player wish to target the same player with the Vuil’raith The Stillness of Stars agent ability, then they will both be able to capture a ship, resolving in initiative order from the active player. Both players will still use the target player’s full commodity value to determine which units they may capture. Should the first player to resolve capture the last of a type of unit from the target player’s reinforcements, the latter player cannot capture a unit of the same type.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Yssaril player duplicates the Mentak player’s Suffi An agent, then the Yssaril player and the player targeted by the Mentak player’sPillageability will draw action cards. The Mentak player will not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Duplicating the effect of the Argent player’s Trillossa Aun Mirik agent, the Creuss player’s Emissary Taivra agent or the Jol–Nar player’s Doctor Sucaban agent during the same timing window as that agent is used will have no additional effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If either the Yssaril player or the Nomad player resolve the effect of the Nomad player’s The Thundarian agent, the other will be unable to resolve the same effect immediately. They must wait until dice are rolled again before they may resolve the effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Ssruu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: For notes about an agent of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: So Ata(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Yssaril player cannot unlock So Ata if they are yet to discard a card for theirSchemingability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Kyver, Blade and Key — Guild of Spies(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Each other player chooses which action card they show the Yssaril player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Kyver, Blade and Key — Guild of Spies(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Taking action cards from a player usingGuild of Spieswill not trigger the Yssaril player’sSchemingability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Deepgloom Executable(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Yssaril player may perform a transaction with another player without being neighbors with that player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yssaril Tribes
--- SECTION_ID: Deepgloom Executable(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Yssaril player may perform a transaction with another player even if neither player is the active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the agenda phase, players can cast votes on agendas that can change the rules of the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players skip the agenda phase during the early portion of each game. After the custodians token is removed from Mecatol Rex, the agenda phase is added to each game round. To resolve the agenda phase, players perform the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – First Agenda: Players resolve the first agenda by following these steps in order:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Second Agenda: Players repeat theFirst Agendastep of this phase for a second agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 3 – Ready Planets: Each player readies each of their exhausted planets. Then, a new game round begins starting with the strategy phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To cast votes, a player exhausts any number of their planets and chooses an outcome. The number of votes cast for that outcome is equal to the combined influence values of the planets that the player exhausts.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot cast votes for multiple outcomes of the same agenda. Each vote a player casts must be for the same outcome.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some agendas have “For” and “Against” outcomes. When a player casts votes on such an agenda, that player must cast their votes either “For” or “Against”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some agendas instruct players to elect either a player or a planet. When a player casts votes for such an agenda, that player must cast their vote for an eligible player or planet as described on the agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When electing a player, a player can cast votes for themselves.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When electing a planet, a player must cast votes for a planet that is controlled by a player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When casting votes, a player must declare aloud the outcome for which their votes are being cast.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Trade goods cannot be spent to cast votes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player may choose to abstain by not casting any votes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some game effects allow a player to cast additional votes for an outcome. These votes cannot be cast for a different outcome than other votes cast by that player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player cannot vote on an agenda because of a game effect, that player cannot cast votes for that agenda by exhausting planets or through any other game effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve an outcome, the speaker follows the instructions on the agenda card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If there is a tie for the outcome that received the most votes, or if no outcome receives any votes, the speaker decides which of the tied outcomes to resolve.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an “Elect” or “For” outcome of a law was resolved, that card remains in play and permanently affects the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a directive or an “Against” outcome of a law was resolved, that card is placed in the agenda discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some game effects instruct a player to predict an outcome. To predict an outcome, a player declares aloud the outcome they think will receive the most votes. That player must make this prediction after the agenda is revealed but before any votes have been cast.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot cast zero votes for an outcome. Casting zero votes is the same as abstaining.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a player casts votes during the agenda phase, it is not that player’s turn for the purpose of game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an agenda outcome affects multiple players, it does so in speaker order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Riders are resolved after the agenda is fully resolved, in speaker order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player successfully predicts multiple riders, they resolve one at a time, in the order that player chooses, with each other player having the opportunity to resolve an ability between each.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Each pair of players may resolve one transaction during each agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Only planets ready at the end of the phase. Technologies, leaders, relics, and other cards do not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific agenda cards, see theagenda card component notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Agenda Cards
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Custodians Token
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Game Round
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Influence
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Speaker
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Transactions
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player begins the game with one unique and five generic promissory note cards that can be given to other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each promissory note contains timing text and ability text. A player can resolve any of their promissory note cards by following the text on the card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot play their color’s or faction’s promissory notes. Since the cards are only valuable to other players, promissory notes can be traded as powerful negotiation tools.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Promissory notes that are returned to a player are returned after their abilities have been completely resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a promissory note is returned to a player, that player may give it to other players again as part of a future transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When resolving a transaction, a player can trade a maximum of one promissory note from their hand to another player, even if that card originally belonged to another player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players should keep their hands of promissory notes hidden.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player is eliminated, all of the promissory notes that match their color or faction are returned to the game box, including those that are in play or owned by other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The number of promissory notes in a player’s hand is public information.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When two players make a trade for a promissory note, the specific promissory note that was traded may be hidden from other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may choose to reveal any or all of the promissory notes in their hand, if they so choose.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific generic promissory notes, see thepromissory notes notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about a promissory note of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Abilities
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Component Action
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Elimination
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Transactions
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The first player to gain 10 victory points wins the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players gain victory points in a variety of ways. A common way that a player can gain victory points is by scoring objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player uses the victory point track to indicate the number of victory points they have gained.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player places one of their control tokens on space “0” of the victory point track during setup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player gains a victory point, they advance their control token a number of spaces along the victory point track equal to the number of victory points gained.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an ability refers to the player with the “most” or “fewest” victory points, and more than one player is tied in that respect, the effect applies to all of the tied players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player gains a victory point from a law, and that law is discarded, that player does not lose that victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The game ends immediately when one player has 10 victory points. If multiple players would simultaneously gain their 10thvictory point, the player who is earliest in initiative order among those players is the winner; if this occurs when players do not have strategy cards, the player who is nearest the speaker (including the speaker) in clockwise order is the winner.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the game ends because the speaker cannot reveal an objective card, the player with the most victory points is the winner. If one or more players are tied for having the most victory points, the tied player who is first in initiative order is the winner.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Agenda Card
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Imperial
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Objective Cards
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Victory Points

--- CONTENT: Relics

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding neutral units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Neutral units are placed in some system within The Fracture when it enters play. Several other game effects also place neutral units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player has ships in a space area that contains neutral units, they will resolve a space combat against those units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player has ground forces on a planet that contains neutral units, they will resolve a ground combat against those units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Any player other than the active player may roll the combat and unit ability dice during a combat involving neutral units. The combat values and unit abilities are found on the neutral unit reference card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Neutral units will always use each and every unit ability that they can.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Neutral units do not take turns, own technology, or draw action cards, and so on. They cannot retreat from combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a hit is assigned against a group of neutral units, it is assigned to the unit that is lowest on the neutral unit reference card; generally, this corresponds to the unit with the lowest cost.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Neutral units are considered to be another player’s ships for abilities and other game effects. However, there is no neutral player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: The Fracture
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Ground Combat
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Neutral Units
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Space Combat
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Resources
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Resources represent a planet’s material value and industry. Many game effects, such as producing units, require players to spend resources.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Resources
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet’s resources are the leftmost value that is surrounded by a yellow border on the planet’s system tile and planet card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Resources
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player spends a planet’s resources by exhausting its card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Resources
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can spend a trade good as if it were one resource.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Resources
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Cost
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: An anomaly is a system tile that has unique rules.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: An anomaly is identified by a red border located on the tile’s corners.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There are four types of anomalies: asteroid fields, nebulae, supernovas, and gravity rifts.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each type of anomaly is identified by its art.See rulebook for images.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Abilities can cause a system tile to become an anomaly; that system tile is an anomaly in addition to its other properties.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Abilities can cause a system to be two different anomalies; that system has the properties of both anomalies.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: An empty system is not an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A system containing a wormhole is not an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A system with a Vuil’raith Dimensional Tear is a gravity rift, and thus an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Asteroid Field
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Gravity Rift
##################################################

--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Nebula
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Anomalies

--- CONTENT: System Tiles
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Agenda cards represent galactic laws and policies. During each agenda phase, players cast votes for specific outcomes on two agenda cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There are two types of agenda cards: laws and directives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Laws can permanently change the rules of the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When resolving a law, if a “For” outcome received the most votes, or if the law requires an election, the law’s ability becomes a permanent part of the game. Players resolve the outcome and place the agenda card either in the common play area or in a player’s play area, as dictated by the card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a law is in a player’s play area as opposed to the common play area, that player owns that law.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a law is discarded from play, that law’s ability is no longer in effect. Place that card on the top of the agenda card discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an “Against” outcome of a law received the most votes, players resolve the outcome and discard the agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Directives provide one–time game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When resolving a directive, players resolve the outcome that received the most votes and discard the agenda card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When resolving the primary ability of thePoliticscard, the active player cannot show the agenda cards they drew to any other player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the outcome of an agenda affects multiple players, it will do so in speaker order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific agenda cards, see theagenda card component notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Agenda Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Attach
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Politics
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Speaker
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agenda Card
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Victory Points
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding synergy.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Certain abilities, primarily breakthroughs, grant synergy between two colors of technology, allowing components of one color to be treated as the other for some game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When researching a technology, a player may treat each technology they own and/or each technology speciality on a planet they control that matches one color of their synergy as any color of that synergy.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When scoring an objective, a player may treat each technology they own that matches one color of their synergy as any color of that synergy.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: These choices are made individually for each technology and/or each technology speciality.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Each technology and/or each technology speciality can only be one color of technology at any given point in time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A technology and/or each technology speciality may be treated as different colors of technologies at different points in time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Synergy
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Breakthroughs
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheDiplomacystrategy card can be used to preemptively prevent other players from activating a specific system. It can also be used to ready planets. This card’s initiative value is “2”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has theDiplomacystrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on theDiplomacystrategy card, the active player chooses a system that contains a planet they control other than the Mecatol Rex system; each other player places one command token from their reinforcements in that system. Then, the active player readies any two of their exhausted planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend one command token from their strategy pool to ready up to two exhausted planets they control.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the player withDiplomacycontrols no planets, or controls only Mecatol Rex, they may still perform a strategic action. However, other players will no place a command token in any system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the player withDiplomacycontrols fewer than two exhausted planets, they may still perform a strategic action. They will ready as many planets as possible.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The Diplomacy token represents a command token from each player other than the player with theDiplomacystrategy card. It may be used to simplify play when no player is expected to interact with the command tokens placed by the primary ability, especially during early rounds.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Active System
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Command Tokens
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Initiative Order
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Diplomacy (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Readied

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Telepathic
--- CONTENT: The Naalu player retains the Naalu 0 token, even if an effect such as theImperial Arbiterlaw causes them to lose the strategy card it was on. The Naalu player will place the Naalu 0 token on another strategy card in this scenario.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: UsingForesightis not a retreat. As such, it cannot be cancelled with theInterceptaction card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: The command token is not spent. The Naalu player cannot use theScepter of Emelpar, nor will they gain a trade good if they have the Muuat player’sAlliancepromissory note.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: Fighters are moved without being transported. Ground forces may be transported.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: The Naalu player cannot useForesightto move into a nebula or supernova.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: If the Naalu player usesForesightto move out of a gravity rift, they will have to roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: After moving, capacity and fleet pool limits apply in the destination system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: If the destination system already contains one of the Naalu player’s command tokens, the command token from the Naalu player’s strategy pool is instead placed in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Foresight
--- CONTENT: After resolvingForesight, play continues to theSpace Cannon Offensestep. Only the active player’s ships in the active system may be assigned hits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Gift of Prescience(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The player withGift of Prescienceretains the Naalu 0 token, even if an effect such as theImperial Arbiterlaw causes them to lose the strategy card it was on. That player will place the Naalu 0 token on another strategy card in this scenario.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Neuroglaive(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The active player must meet fleet pool limits in all systems that contain their ships before they may proceed to theMovementstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Neuroglaive(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player only has other players’ command tokens in their fleet pool when they trigger Neuroglaive, they must return one of those command tokens to that player’s reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Matriarch(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: The committed fighters are returned to the space area when combat ends, and thus will not be on the planet for theEstablish Controlstep. If the Naalu player does not commit at least one ground force to a planet and have it survive the combat, they will be unable to gain control of that planet, and the ground combat will end in a draw.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Matriarch(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Any structures on the planet will not be destroyed if the Naalu player committed no ground forces.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Matriarch(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: TheDaxcive Animatorstechnology will not allow the Naalu player to gain control of a planet without committing a ground force.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Matriarch(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: The committed fighters may be assigned hits during theSpace Cannon Defensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu(Agent)
--- CONTENT: When theCovert Legislationagenda is revealed during the agenda phase, the Naalu player cannot look at the hidden agenda. Once the speaker has read the hidden agenda, the Naalu player may look at the next card of the agenda deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: All other rules applying to tactical actions apply, other than placing a command token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The chosen player is considered to be the active player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the chosen player is not the Naalu player, it is not considered their turn for game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the chosen player is not the Naalu player, they may use any “before/after you perform an action” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the chosen player is not the Naalu player, abilities that would end their turn instead end their tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the chosen player is not the Naalu player, they cannot use theFleet Logisticstechnology to perform an additional action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the chosen player is not the Naalu player, and they had previously passed, they are still considered passed during their action. They do not pass at the end of the action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu Ω(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Any deal between the Naalu player and another player regarding which system will be activated, if made before Z’eu Ω is exhausted, is non–binding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Z’eu ΩΩ(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Z’eu ΩΩ may be used whenever a command token is placed in a system. For example, it may be used when a player activates a system, when a player resolves the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card, or when a player resolves theSignal Jammingaction card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: M’aban(Commander)
--- CONTENT: When producing units, the Naalu player must produce all the units they intend to produce before they may unlock M’aban. M’aban cannot be applied to the instance of producing the units that unlocks it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: M’aban(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If theRegulated Conscriptionlaw is in play, the Naalu player may produce two fighters for one resource. This will count one towards theirProductionlimit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: M’aban(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If a game effect instructs the Naalu player to produce ships without using theProductionability, they may only produce additional fighters if that game effect allows them to produce fighters.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: M’aban(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Naalu player may choose to produce one fighter for one resource. If they do, they may produce one additional fighter.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: M’aban Ω(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Naalu player cannot look at the agenda deck while a player is resolving the primary ability of the Politics strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: M’aban Ω(Commander)
--- CONTENT: When theCovert Legislationagenda is revealed during the agenda phase, the Naalu player cannot look at the hidden agenda. Once the speaker has read the hidden agenda, the Naalu player may look at the next card of the agenda deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: The Oracle — C–Radium Geometry(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Each other player chooses which promissory note they give the Naalu player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Iconoclast(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The +1 will not apply to an opponent who has a relic but zero relic fragments.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Iconoclast Ω(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The ability will apply regardless of if the Iconoclast is in the space area or on a planet in the system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Iconoclast ΩΩ(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Naalu player must mandatorily place a mech when another player gains a relic, if they have at least one in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Naalu Collective
--- SECTION_ID: Mindsieve(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Naalu player may only give promissory notes from their hand; they cannot give promissory notes that are in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After resolving theSpace Cannon Offensestep of a tactical action, if two players have ships in the active system, those players must resolve a space combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the active player is the only player with ships in the system, they skip theSpace Combatstep of the tactical action and proceeds to theInvasionstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an ability occurs “before combat”, it occurs immediately before theAnti–Fighter Barragestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – Anti–Fighter Barrage: If this is the first round of a space combat, the players may simultaneously use theAnti–Fighter Barrageability of any of their units in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Announce Retreats: Each player may announce a retreat, beginning with the defender.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 3 – Roll Dice: Each player rolls one die for each ship they have in the active system; this is called a combat roll. If a unit’s combat roll produces a result that is equal to or greater than that unit’s combat value, that result produces a hit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 4 – Assign Hits: Each player in the combat must choose and destroy one of their own ships in the active system for each hit their opponent produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 5 – Retreat: If a player announced a retreat duringstep 2, and there is still an eligible system for their units to retreat to, they must retreat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After theRetreatstep, if both players still have ships in the active system, those players resolve another round of space combat beginning with theAnnounce Retreatsstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Space combat ends when only one player – or neither player – has a ship in the space area of the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a combat ends, the player with one or more ships remaining in the system is the winner of the combat; the other player is the loser of the combat. If neither player has a ship remaining, the combat ends in a draw and there is no winner.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player’s fighters and ground forces do not count against capacity during combat. At the end of combat, any excess units are removed and returned to that player’s reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may retreat into an asteroid field only if that player owns theAntimass Deflectorstechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may retreat into a supernova only if that player owns theMagmus ReactorMuaat factional technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot retreat into a nebula.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may attempt to retreat from a combat in a gravity rift, but will still be affected by it. See thegravity rift pagefor more details.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player only has fighters I in the combat when they retreat, those will be removed from the board, and they will not place a command token in an adjacent system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: TheNav Suiteaction card will not allow a player to ignore an anomaly while retreating.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: TheDark Energy Taptechnology allows a player to retreat into a system that does not contain their ships or a planet they control.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Modifying the move value of a ship will have no effect when retreating. Retreats are limited to adjacent systems.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: While retreating, a player may transport zero or more ground forces from planets they control in the active system. The player need not decide which fighters and ground forces they transport until they execute the retreat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot leave fighters and ground forces in the space area behind in the active system if they would have unused capacity during the retreat. However, if they have fighters and ground forces in both the space area and on one or more planets in the active system, they may choose which units they transport. If this choice results in all their available capacity being used, they may leave units behind in the space area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: While retreating, a player cannot transport more fighters and/or ground forces than they have capacity in the retreating ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Capacity is checked after the winner of a space combat is determined. As such, it is possible to win a space combat with only fighters remaining, before removing those fighters due to lack of capacity.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The “0” side of the d10 represents a result of 10.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Combat
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Liberate
--- CONTENT: If the Bastion player gains control of an uncontrolled planet, they may choose if they resolveLiberatebefore or after they explore that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Liberate
--- CONTENT: The number of mechs is irrelevant for determining which effect to resolve.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Proxima Targeting VI(Technology)
--- CONTENT: When the Bastion player makes theBombardmentroll against their own units, they will be able to cancel a hit for each of their present galvanized units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Proxima Targeting VI(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Other players with galvanised units cannot cancel theBombardmenthits produced byProxima Targeting VI.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: 4X31C “Helios”(Unit)
--- CONTENT: TheProductionvalue of the 4X31C “Helios” will be calculated from the modified resource value of the planet, after the increase from the 4X31C “Helios” present.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: The Egeiro(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the Bastion player controls multiple planets in a system,The Egeirowill apply +1 to its combat rolls just once.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: The Egeiro(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the Bastion player controls a planet in a system, and other players control other planets in that system,The Egeirowill still apply +1 to its combat rolls from that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Dame Briar(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Any type of unit in the same system may be galvanized; it need not match the type of the destroyed unit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Nip and Tuck(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Bastion player’s action cards may still be cancelled by other game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Nip and Tuck(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player already has a Valefar Assimilator token on one of the Bastion player’s components, it will remain there when Nip and Tuck are unlocked.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Lura Keen — Entity 4X41A “Apollo”(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any combat roll modifiers will not apply to the dice roll forEntity 4X41A “Apollo”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Lura Keen — Entity 4X41A “Apollo”(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Units can only be destroyed by the dice specifically allocated to it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Lura Keen — Entity 4X41A “Apollo”(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Effects that cancel hits, such asSustain Damage, cannot be used to prevent units from being destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Last Bastion
--- SECTION_ID: Lura Keen — Entity 4X41A “Apollo”(Hero)
--- CONTENT: All units belonging to other players in the system may be destroyed, including structures.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Strategy cards determine initiative order and provide each player with a powerful ability that they can use one time during the action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the strategy phase, each player chooses a strategy card from the common play area and places it in their play area faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each strategy card has a readied and an exhausted side.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can only resolve theprimaryability oftheir ownstrategy cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can only resolve thesecondaryability of strategy cards that were chosen byother players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There are eight strategy cards, each of which has a name and an initiative number.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The initiative number on a player’s strategy card determines the initiative order for the action phase and status phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A strategy card has both a primary ability and a secondary ability. These abilities are resolved during a strategic action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each strategy card exists in either the common play area or a player’s play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: During three– and four–player games, each player will choose two strategy cards during the strategy phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Card
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Construction

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: There currently does not exist a Living Rules Reference section regarding space stations.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Several systems contain space stations, which are mechanically similar to planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player gains control of a space station when they are the only player with units in that space station’s system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Each space station has a corresponding planet card. The space station may be exhausted for resources or influence as though it were a planet. The space station will be readied during the status phase as though it were a planet, or by other game effects that can ready planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Structures and ground forces cannot be committed to or placed on a space station.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Space stations do not count as planets for the purpose of voting, or scoring objectives, and a player may still score public objectives even if another player controls a space station in their home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For each space station a player controls, their commodity value is increased by one.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player who controls one or more space stations may resolve transactions with other players who control one or more space stations.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may exhaust a space station at any time to convert any commodities that they have into trade goods.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a system tile contains a space station, but no planets, then a frontier token will be placed in that system during game setup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Control
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Exhausted
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Influence
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Readied
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Stations

### RULE_SOURCE: ⚪ The Firmament✖ The Obsidian
--- SECTION_ID: ⚪ Plots Within Plots
--- CONTENT: If the Firmament player scores a secret objective that has been made into a public objective by a game effect, such as theClassified Document Leaksagenda, they will gain a victory point as normal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: ⚪ The Firmament✖ The Obsidian
--- SECTION_ID: ⚪ Puppets of the Blade
--- CONTENT: When the Firmament player flips their home system, the Obsidian player places any units that were on Cronos onto Cronos Hollow, and places any units on Tallin onto Tallin Hollow. Any units that were in the space area pre–flip are placed in the space area post–flip.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: ⚪ The Firmament✖ The Obsidian
--- SECTION_ID: ⚪ Planesplitter(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If The Fracture is already in play when the Firmament player gainsPlanesplitter, it will have no immediate effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: ⚪ The Firmament✖ The Obsidian
--- SECTION_ID: ✖ Planesplitter(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The ingress token must be moved when the Obsidian player performs the primary ability of their strategy card, before any other players decide if they wish to perform the secondary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: ⚪ The Firmament✖ The Obsidian
--- SECTION_ID: ⚪ Captain Aroz(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Captain Aroz does not assist in scoring secret objectives that do not require controlling planets, such as theMechanize the MilitaryorOccupy the Fringesecret objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: ⚪ The Firmament✖ The Obsidian
--- SECTION_ID: ✖ The Reaping(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Any trade goods that were onThe Sowingare transferred toThe Reapingwhen it flips.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Commerce
--- CONTENT: Players must still be neighbors on the game board for the purpose of resolving game effects that depend on players being neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Commerce
--- CONTENT: The Hacan player’sGuild Shipsfaction ability andTrade Convoyspromissory note provide no benefit while playing with theAge of Commerceevent. However,Trade Convoysmay still be played as a component action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Commerce
--- CONTENT: If the Empyrean player receives commodities from a player with theirDark Pactpromissory note in their play area equal to that player’s printed commodity value, then both players will gain one trade good. This need not be all of the giving player’s current commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Commerce
--- CONTENT: When a player’sTrade Agreementpromissory note is played, they give only the number of commodities that they just gained due to replenishing commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Commerce
--- CONTENT: A player may share any number of technologies in a single transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Exploration
--- CONTENT: If there are no more blue–backed or red–backed tiles available, a player does not place any tile if they roll the corresponding dice result.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Exploration
--- CONTENT: TheDark Energy Taptechnology retains all its printed abilities when it is exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Exploration
--- CONTENT: New tiles cannot be placed adjacent to the Creuss or Rebellion home systems, the wormhole nexus, or systems that comprise The Fracture.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Age of Fighters
--- CONTENT: The Vuil’raith player still captures ships that they destroy via their various abilities. These ships are purged when they would be returned to their original owner.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Cosmic Phenomanae
--- CONTENT: Only ships moving out of gravity rifts may apply the +2 to their move value; ships moving through cannot.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Cosmic Phenomanae
--- CONTENT: For ships moving out of a gravity rift, the active player chooses for each one whether it applies +1 or +2 to its move value, and then rolls for removing with the corresponding threshold.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Cosmic Phenomanae
--- CONTENT: Ships that move out of a gravity rift outside of the movement step of a tactical action, such as through retreating from a space combat, must still roll for removal. Their owner may choose which threshold to use.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Dangerous Wilds
--- CONTENT: The player may research the technology before or after they explore the planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: During setup, if a player places a minor faction system with two planets, that player chooses which planet gets two neutral infantry and which planet gets one.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: During setup, if a player is dealt the Creuss reference card, they place the Creuss Gate (tile 17) in the equidistant, and place the Creuss home system (tile 51) in the common play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: During setup, if a player is dealt the Rebellion reference card, they place the Sorrow (tile 94) in the equidistant, and place the Rebellion home system (tile 118) in the common play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: During setup, if a player is dealt the Keleres reference card, then they select a home system at random from amongst the Argent, Mentak and Xxcha, excluding any that have already been placed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: If Mahact exists as a minor faction, the player that controls Ixth gains access to the ability of Il Na Viroset, the Mahact commander.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: Commander abilities of minor factions do not need to be unlocked; they are available as soon as a player takes the corresponding alliance card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: When a player gains control of a minor faction planet, if it is not controlled by another player, they explore it. They choose which planet trait they explore it as.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: A player only loses a minor faction’s alliance card if a single other player controls each planet in that minor faction’s system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: The planets in a minor faction’s system are not home planets, nor is the system a home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: All neutral infantry have a combat value of 8, and otherwise have no special abilities, regardless of which minor faction they belong to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Minor Factions
--- CONTENT: Minor factions are not players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Monuments to the Ages
--- CONTENT: If a player would gain their final victory point at the start of the status phase from a monument, they immediately win the game. Players will not score objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Rapid Mobilization
--- CONTENT: During setup, if a player gains and readies a planet with a technology specialty, they may exhaust that planet when they research a technology to ignore a prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Atomics
--- CONTENT: If all players have removed their control token fromStellar Atomics, then no player will vote on agendas, and the speaker will decide which outcome is resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Atomics
--- CONTENT: Players may still resolve non–action card abilities during the action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Atomics
--- CONTENT: If the Xxcha player has Elder Qanoj, their commander, unlocked, they will be able to vote after removing their control token fromStellar Atomics.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Total War
--- CONTENT: Commodities on planets are not treated as commodities for any game effect, other than those that appear on theTotal Warevent card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Total War
--- CONTENT: If a player gains control of a planet in another player’s home system, without controlling at least one planet in their own home system, then any commodities on the planet they gained control of remain on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Wild, Wild Galaxy
--- CONTENT: A player with no planets remaining in their home system is not prevented from scoring public objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Events
--- SECTION_ID: Wild, Wild Galaxy
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player’sNova Seedhero ability replaces a player’s home system with a supernova, then that supernova becomes that player’s home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Board
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The game board consists of all system tiles in play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Board
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The game board consists of all system tiles that were placed during setup, even if the sides of those tiles do not touch any other system tiles, such as the Ghosts of Creuss’ home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Board
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A system tile is on the edge of the game board if any of its sides are not touching another system tile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Board
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the edge of a system tile is touching a hyperlane tile, that edge does not cause that system tile to be on the edge of the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Game Board
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Mitosis
--- CONTENT: If the Arborec player produces one or more units with a space dock, and produces any infantry with their Letani Warriors, the produced infantry may be placed on the same planet as the space dock, regardless of if that planet contains any Letani Warriors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec

--- CONTENT: The Arborec player may produce Letani Behemoth with their space docks.

--- SECTION_ID: Mitosis
--- CONTENT: Placing the infantry during the status phase is mandatory (unless the Arborec player controls no planets).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Stymie(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Stymiehas no effect while it is in a player’s hand.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Stymie(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Stymieis returned when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the Arborec player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Stymie(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Activating a system containing only the Arborec player’s structures will still causeStymieto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Stymie(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the Arborec player’s units (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeStymieto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Stymie Ω(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player has no command tokens in their reinforcements, that player places one command token of their choice from their command sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Stymie Ω(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Stymiecannot place a command token in the home system of an eliminated player.
