### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Bioplasmosis(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Any number of infantry may move, but all movement is done simultaneously, and no infantry may move beyond an adjacent system. For example, consider a series of systems A–B–C. Only systems connected by a “–” are adjacent. In this case:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Bioplasmosis(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Bioplasmosiscannot move Letani Behemoth.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Letani Warrior(Unit)
--- CONTENT: The Arborec player cannot use the secondary ability of theWarfarestrategy card to use theProductionability of a Letani Warrior.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Letani Warrior(Unit)
--- CONTENT: When multiple units use theirProductionability, theProductionvalue is pooled. As such, if the Arborec player has two Letani Warrior I in a system, they may produce two infantry for one resource, rather than two.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Letani Warrior(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If Letani Warriors are on different planets, any produced ground forces may be split between those planets, regardless of the production value of the Letani Warriors on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Duha Menaimon(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: The produced units must be paid for.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Duha Menaimon(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: TheDuha Menaimondoes not haveProduction. As such, theSarween Toolstechnology and similar such effects do not apply to theDuha Menaimon.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Duha Menaimon(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: TheDuha Menaimonmust be in the system when it is activated for its effect to trigger. It will not trigger if it is moved into the active system later in the turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Letani Ospha(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The replaced ship is not destroyed. The replacing ship is not produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Letani Ospha(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the player wishes to place a ship, but there are none of that type left in their reinforcements, they may remove a ship of that type from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. This ship will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Letani Ospha(Agent)
--- CONTENT: A fighter may be placed with Letani Ospha.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Dirzuga Rophal(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The produced unit must be paid for.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Dirzuga Rophal(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The unit is produced before ships move. A ship may be produced if no other player currently has ships in that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Dirzuga Rophal(Commander)
--- CONTENT: No unit is using itsProductionability. TheSarween Toolstechnology and similar effects will not apply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Dirzuga Rophal(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If a ground force is produced, it may be placed on any planet the Arborec player controls in that system, regardless of what units, if any, the Arborec player has on that planet. The produced ground force may also be placed in the space area of that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Arborec
--- SECTION_ID: Dirzuga Rophal(Commander)

--- CONTENT: The following promissory notes qualify for scoringBetray a Friend:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Betray a Friend
--- CONTENT: The defender cannot scoreBetray a Friend.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Brave the Void
--- CONTENT: Any system containing a Vuil’raith player’s Dimensional Tear is a gravity rift, and thus, an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Brave the Void
--- CONTENT: A wormhole is not an anomaly.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Centralize Galactic Trade
--- CONTENT: The trade goods must be spent during the status phase. Any trade goods that were spent during the action phase will have no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Conquer the Weak
--- CONTENT: The planet may be in the home system of an eliminated player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Control the Borderlands
--- CONTENT: The number of units in the system is irrelevant, if there is at least one.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Control the Borderlands
--- CONTENT: A ship, ground force, or structure will all qualify forControl the Borderlands.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Control the Borderlands
--- CONTENT: The units may be in another player’s home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Control the Borderlands
--- CONTENT: The Creuss Gate is not a home system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Control the Borderlands
--- CONTENT: The Wormhole Nexus and the Creuss home system are both on the edge of the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Control the Borderlands
--- CONTENT: If the edge of a system tile is touching a hyperlane tile, that edge does not cause that system tile to be on the edge of the game board.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Control the Region
--- CONTENT: Any ground forces or structures are irrelevant.

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Demonstrate Your Power
--- CONTENT: A player need not win the combat to scoreDemonstrate Your Power; they are able to score it if their opponent plays theSkilled Retreataction card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Demonstrate Your Power
--- CONTENT: A player involved in a combat due to the Mahact player’sBenedictionhero ability may scoreDemonstrate Your Powerafter that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Demonstrate Your Power
--- CONTENT: Units that are temporarily ships for the duration of a space combat, such as those made so by the Nekro player’s flagship,The Alastor, or the Naaz–Rokha player’s Z–Grav Eidolon mechs, may count towards scoringDemonstrate Your Power.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Demonstrate Your Power
--- CONTENT: The Mentak player may use theSleeper Cellability of their hero, during the last round of combat to place ships before scoringDemonstrate Your Power. However, fleet pool limits are also checked before scoring.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Destroy Heretical Works
--- CONTENT: A player will not gain a relic when scoringDestroy Heretical Works.

--- SECTION_ID: Destroy Heretical Works
--- CONTENT: The relic fragments may be the same or different types.

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Destroy Their Greatest Ship
--- CONTENT: If a player destroys their own flagship or war sun during combat, such as via the effect ofThe Crown of Thalnosrelic, their opponent cannot scoreDestroy their Greatest Ship.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Destroy Their Greatest Ship
--- CONTENT: Destroy their Greatest Shipis scored as soon as the war sun or flagship is destroyed; it does not require waiting until the end of the combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Destroy Their Greatest Ship
--- CONTENT: A player may scoreDestroy their Greatest Shipoutside of a combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Develop Weaponry
--- CONTENT: AValefar Assimilatortechnology will count if it is currently copying another player’s faction unit upgrade technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Develop Weaponry
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player owns both a generic unit upgrade technology and a faction unit upgrade technology of the same type, only the faction unit upgrade technology will count forDevelop Weaponry.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Dictate Policy
--- CONTENT: Dictate Policyis scored after the third law resolves. As such, theDeadly Plotaction card will prevent any player from scoringDictate Policy.

--- SECTION_ID: Dictate Policy
--- CONTENT: Dictate Policyis scored before any rider action cards are resolved.

--- SECTION_ID: Dictate Policy
--- CONTENT: If there are three laws in play at the start of the agenda phase, a player may scoreDictate Policyimmediately.

--- SECTION_ID: Dictate Policy
--- CONTENT: If thePolitical Data NexusXxcha hero ability puts a third law in play during the action phase,Dictate Policycannot be scored until the agenda phase.

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Discover Lost Outposts
--- CONTENT: The number of attachments a planet has is irrelevant, if it has at least one.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Drive the Debate
--- CONTENT: Any “For”/“Against” agenda cannot count forDrive the Debate, even if the outcome affects only a single player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Drive the Debate
--- CONTENT: Drive the Debateis scored immediately before the agenda resolves. TheConfounding Legal TextandConfusing Legal Textaction cards will allow only the newly elected player to scoreDrive the Debate, and theDeadly Plotaction card will prevent any player from scoringDrive the Debate.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Objectives
--- SECTION_ID: Drive the Debate
--- CONTENT: ScoringDrive the Debateimmediately before theColonial Redistributionagenda is resolved may change which player(s) can be chosen to place the infantry on the elected planet.

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Relics are powerful artifacts with unique abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can use the abilities of hazardous, cultural, and industrial relic fragments in their play area to draw cards from the relic deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player is instructed to gain a relic, they draw the top card of the relic deck and place it faceup in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can use the abilities of relics that are in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Relics cannot be traded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the relic deck is empty, a player may still purge three relic fragments as an action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an eliminated player had any relic fragments, they are discarded to their respective exploration discard piles. If an eliminated player had any relics, they are purged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific relics, see therelic notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit upgrade is a type of technology card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Unit upgrades share a name with a unit that is printed on a player’s faction sheet, but have a higher roman numeral. For example, a player’s “Carrier I” unit is upgraded by the unit upgrade technology “Carrier II”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players place unit upgrades they gain faceup on their faction sheets, covering the unit that shares a name with that upgrade card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The white arrows next to an attribute on a faction sheet indicate that the attribute will improve when the unit is upgraded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a player gains a unit upgrade card, each of that player’s units that correspond to that upgrade card is treated as having the attributes and abilities printed on that upgrade card. Any previous attributes of that unit, such as the one printed on that player’s faction sheet, are ignored.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A mech unit card is not a technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is playing a faction with a faction–specific unit upgrade, they cannot research or otherwise gain the generic upgrade for that unit type.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific generic unit upgrades, see theunit component notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about a unit upgrade technology of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Technology
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Unit Upgrades
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Units
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the strategy phase, each player chooses a strategy card to use during the round.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the strategy phase, players perform the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1: Starting with the speaker and proceeding clockwise, each player chooses one strategy card from the common play area and places it faceup in their play area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2: The speaker places one trade good token from the supply on each strategy card that was not chosen.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player chooses a strategy card, but later loses it, they will keep any trade goods that were on the strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Action Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Game Round
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Speaker
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Strategy Card
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategy Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Trade Goods
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: The Tribunii
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player chooses their starting technology after all other players, including the Argent, Bastion, Deepwrought, Firmament, Ral Nel, Rebellion, and Winnu players, have gained their starting technologies.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: The Tribunii
--- CONTENT: If there are not two unique starting technologies amongst those owned by other players, the Keleres player will start the game with fewer technologies. This will most commonly happen in a three player game, where one of the other players is playing as N’orr or Winnu.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Council Patronage
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player must mandatorily replenish their commodities and gain a trade good every strategy phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Council Patronage
--- CONTENT: If the Keleres player already has two commodities, they will still replenish their commodities during the strategy phase. This will not give them additional commodities, but will trigger any effects that happen when the Keleres player replenishes their commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Council Patronage
--- CONTENT: If another player is holding the Keleres player’sTrade Agreementpromissory note, they may use it when the Keleres player replenishes commodities fromCouncil Patronage.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Law’s Order
--- CONTENT: The blanked laws come back into effect at the end of the turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Law’s Order
--- CONTENT: If this ability is used, all laws are blanked. The Keleres player cannot choose for some laws to remain in effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Law’s Order
--- CONTENT: If the Keleres player owns thePolitical Censurelaw, they will not lose a victory point when it is blanked, and they may use action cards during this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Law’s Order
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player and all of the other players treat all laws as blank for the turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Keleres Rider(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: After playingKeleres Rider, a player may use additional abilities, including playing other rider cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Keleres Rider(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The effect of a successfulKeleres Riderwill be resolved after the effect of the agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Keleres Rider(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player who cannot vote may still play aKeleres Rider.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Keleres Rider(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player who cannot play action cards may still play aKeleres Rider.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Agency Supply Network(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that trigger “when/after a unit usesProduction” will trigger an additional time, for example, theSarween Toolstechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Agency Supply Network(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The additionalProductionability cannot belong to the same unit as the originalProductionability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Agency Supply Network(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player may use Custodia Vigilia as the additionalProductionability, and when they use Custodia Vigilia as the originalProductionability, they may use an additionalProductionability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Agency Supply Network(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The originalProductionability must be fully resolved, before the Keleres player may use an additionalProductionability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Keleres player draws one of theClassified Document Leaks,Judicial Abolishment,Miscount DisclosedorNew Constitutionagendas, they will discard it if required and reveal a new agenda from the deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If theMiscount Disclosedagenda is resolved, the players will also vote on the elected agenda during the Keleres player’s action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If thePublic Executionagenda is resolved, the elected player cannot vote in the agenda phase following the current action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If an agenda would give multiple players a victory point, those players gain that victory point in initiative order, starting with the player with theLeadershipstrategy card (or next lowest initiative value should no player have theLeadershipstrategy card), regardless of the Keleres player’s initiative.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Other players may still perform one transaction total with the Keleres player during this turn, if they are neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Players exhaust planets to cast votes when resolvingExecutive Order, even if theRepresentative Governmentlaw is in play, which only affects voting during the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If a third law is put into play, theDictate Policysecret objective cannot be scored until the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: TheDrive the Debatesecret objective cannot be scored while resolvingExecutive Order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Effects from agenda outcomes that occur “at the end of this agenda phase” will instead resolve at the end of the next agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Order(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Effects from agenda outcomes that occur “at the start of the next strategy phase” will still resolve at the start of the next strategy phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: I.I.H.Q. Modernization(Technology/Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Keleres player is neighbors with another player, that player is neighbors with the Keleres player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: The Custodia Vigilia planet card is gained exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: Units cannot be placed on Custodia Vigilia.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: Custodia Vigilia is not adjacent to any system, unit, player or other planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player cannot lose control of Custodia Vigilia.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: Custodia Vigilia may be used to qualify for objectives, if it meets any other requirements listed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: Custodia Vigilia may be elected by any “elect planet” agendas. However, Custodia Vigilia may be immune to the effects of the agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: A player gains victory points from the Imperial strategy card only if they control Mecatol Rex. If they use the Imperial strategy card to score an objective, then they gain victory points from that objective, and not the Imperial strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player may use a command token to perform the secondary of Imperial during the same strategic action that they gained that token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: When the Keleres player uses theProductionability of Custodia Vigilia, it is treated as though the Keleres player was using theProductionabilitiy of one of their units on Mecatol Rex.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Custodia Vigilia(Legendary Planet)
--- CONTENT: The Ul player’sTerraformfaction promissory note may be attached to Custodia Vigilia.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Artemiris(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If a player cannot spend two influence, they cannot activate the system containing theArtemiris.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Xander Alexin Victori III(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Xander Alexin Victori III applies to only a single instance of spending trade goods.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Suffi An(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The trade good to unlock Suffi An is spent after, and independent of, any trade goods spent while resolving the action card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Suffi An(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Keleres player uses their additional action to perform another component action, they may perform another additional action. They may do this any number of times.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Suffi An(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Suffi An does not trigger from the component action of the action card used that was to unlock her.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Suffi An(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If a player’s turn is ended by a game effect, they cannot use Suffi An to perform an additional action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Suffi An(Commander)
--- CONTENT: A player cannot use Suffi An to pass on the same turn they performed an action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Suffi An(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If a player’s additional action would be to use a component action to play an action card, and that card is cancelled, they are not required to perform an alternate additional action on that turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Kuuasi Aun Jalatai — Overwing Zeta(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player must be participating in the combat in order to resolveOverwing Zeta.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Kuuasi Aun Jalatai — Overwing Zeta(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to place a ship, but there are none of that type left in their reinforcements, they may remove a ship of that type from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Kuuasi Aun Jalatai — Overwing Zeta(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Overwing Zetamay be played at the start of any round of combat, not just the first.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Odlynn Myrr — Operation Archon(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The additional votes are not cast until the Keleres player casts votes normally.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Odlynn Myrr — Operation Archon(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Keleres player may vote for a different outcome than the one they predicted. If they do, they will gain one trade good and one command token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Council Keleres
--- SECTION_ID: Omniopiares(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If a planet contains multiple mechs, the invading player must pay one influence for each, as separate payments. For example, if all four mechs were on a planet, the invading player could only exhaust Meer to pay for one instance of the ability; they would still have three instances of a single influence to pay.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Cost is an attribute of some units that is presented on faction sheets and unit upgrade technology cards. A unit’s cost determines the number of resources a player must spend to produce that unit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To produce a unit, a player must spend a number of resources equal to or greater than the cost of the unit they are producing.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the cost is accompanied by two icons – typically for fighters and ground forces – a player produces two of that unit for that cost.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a unit does not have a cost, it cannot be produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Whenever a unit is produced, its cost must be paid, unless the effect that is producing the unit explicitly says otherwise.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player does not have to pay a unit’s cost to resolve that unit’sDeployability. However, theDeployability itself may have a cost that must be paid.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Cost (Attribute)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Modifiers
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Producing Units
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Resources
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some cards can be exhausted. A player cannot resolve abilities or spend the resources or influence of an exhausted card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To exhaust a card, a player flips the card facedown.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During theReady Cardsstep of the status phase, each player readies all of their exhausted cards by flipping those cards faceup.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player exhausts their planet cards to spend either the resources or influence on that card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Abilities, including some found on technology cards, may instruct a player to exhaust a card to resolve those abilities. If a card is already exhausted, it cannot be exhausted again.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a player performs a strategic action, they exhaust the strategy card that corresponds to that action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Planets will also ready at the end of each agenda phase. Leaders, relics and technologies will not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a game effect instructs a player to exhaust a planet, the exhausted planet must be controlled by that player, unless the game effect specifies otherwise.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Influence
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exhausted
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Leaders
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Planets

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Masters of Trade
--- CONTENT: If the Hacan player has the Muaat player’sAlliancepromissory note, they will not gain a trade good from it when they use their Masters of Trade ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Guild Ships
--- CONTENT: This ability does not make the Hacan player neighbors with all other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Guild Ships
--- CONTENT: Either player may initiate negotiations for a transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Guild Ships
--- CONTENT: The Hacan player is still limited to one transaction with every other player per turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Arbiters
--- CONTENT: Any number of action cards may be traded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Arbiters
--- CONTENT: A player may receive action cards even if doing so would put them over the seven action card hand limit. They must immediately discard down to seven action cards in this case.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Arbiters
--- CONTENT: If the Hacan player has more than seven action cards, they must immediately discard down to seven action cards. They cannot trade away the excess.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Arbiters
--- CONTENT: If the Hacan player has theirPolitical Secretplayed during an agenda, they may still trade action cards, asArbitersis a passive ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: This ability does not make the player neighbors with all other players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Either player may initiate negotiations for a transaction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The player withTrade Convoysin play is still limited to one transaction with every other player per turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Trade Convoyshas no effect while it is in a player’s hand.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Trade Convoysis returned when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the Hacan player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Activating a system containing only the Hacan player’s structures will still causeTrade Convoysto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Convoys(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the Hacan player’s units (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeTrade Convoysto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Datahub Node(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If either strategy card had trade goods on it at the start of the strategy phase, those trade goods remain with the player that originally chose the strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Datahub Node(Technology)
--- CONTENT: In a three– or four–player game, the Hacan player chooses which strategy cards are swapped.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Quantum Datahub Node(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Hacan player must have three trade goods before they spend the command token; they cannot use the Muaat player’sAlliancepromissory note to gain the third trade good.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Wrath of Kenara(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: This ability may be triggered only once for each die rolled. The Hacan player cannot spend two (or more) trade goods to apply +2 (or more) to a single die, but they may spend two (or more) trade goods to apply +1 to each of two (or more) dice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Carth of Golden Sands(Agent)
--- CONTENT: A player that has their maximum number of commodities may have their commodities replenished. If this happens, they will take no commodities. However, they will still trigger any “when [this] player replenishes commodities” effects, most notably theTrade Agreementpromissory note.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Carth of Golden Sands(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The Hacan player cannot have more than six commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Carth of Golden Sands(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The ability of Carth of Golden Sands cannot be resolved while another ability is resolving. For example, if the Hacan player is exploring an industrial planet and has revealed the card, they cannot use the ability of Carth of Golden Sands until after they resolve the card’s effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Gila the Silvertongue(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Additional votes must be cast for the same outcome as the other votes the Hacan player cast.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Harrugh Gefhara — Galactic Securities Net(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Production limits still apply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Pride of Kenara(Mech)
--- CONTENT: Structures are also moved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Pride of Kenara(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The planet cannot be traded during combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Emirates of Hacan
--- SECTION_ID: Pride of Kenara(Mech)
--- CONTENT: If the Pride of Kenara is on a planet in a gravity rift, any units moved must roll for removal if the planet is transacted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The tactical action is the primary method by which players produce units, move ships, and extend their dominion within the galaxy. To perform a tactical action, the active player performs the following steps:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – Activation: The active player must activate a system that does not contain one of their command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Movement: The active player may move any number of ships that have a sufficient move value from any number of systems that do not contain one of their command tokens into the active system, following the rules for movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 3 – Space Combat: If two players have ships in the active system, those players must resolve a space combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 4 – Invasion: The active player may use theirBombardmentabilities, commit units to land on planets, and resolve ground combat against other players’ units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 5 – Production: The active player may resolve each of their unit’sProductionabilities in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Each of these five steps happen during every tactical action, unless explicitly skipped; the active player does not have to choose between fighting a combat or producing units, for example.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Tactical Action
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that occur at the end of an action happen before any abilities that occur at the end of a player’s turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Asteroid Field
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: An asteroid field is an anomaly that affects movement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Asteroid Field
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ship cannot move through or into an asteroid field.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Asteroid Field
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player with theAntimass Deflectorstechnology may move their ships through asteroid fields.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Asteroid Field
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will place the ship movement restrictions of anomalies upon all units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Asteroid Field
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Anomalies
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Asteroid Field

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Book of Latvinia
--- CONTENT: If a player owns all technologies without prerequisites when they draw theBook of Latvinia, they will not research any technologies.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Book of Latvinia
--- CONTENT: A player cannot gain a technology with a prerequisite by ignoring that prerequisite, such as by exhausting a planet with a technology specialty.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Book of Latvinia
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player draws theBook of Latvinia, they will gain six command tokens and zero technologies, even if they own all technologies without prerequisites.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Book of Latvinia
--- CONTENT: When a player uses the component action of theBook of Latvinia, it is purged, regardless of which outcome is resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Book of Latvinia
--- CONTENT: If a player uses the component action of theBook of Latviniawhen they control planets with each type of technology specialty, they mandatorily gain a victory point; they cannot choose instead to gain the speaker token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Circlet of the Void
--- CONTENT: The player that ownsCirclet of the Voidmay move through or into supernovae and/or asteroid fields.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Circlet of the Void
--- CONTENT: The player that ownsCirclet of the Voidmay move through nebulae, and their ships in nebulae do not have their movement values reduced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Circlet of the Void
--- CONTENT: The player that ownsCirclet of the Voidstill applies the movement bonus to their ships that will move through gravity rifts.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Circlet of the Void
--- CONTENT: The player that ownsCirclet of the Voidwill still ignore anomaly movement effects and not roll for gravity rifts ifCirclet of the Voidis exhausted.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Codex
--- CONTENT: The action card discard is shuffled to form a new action card deck as soon as the action card deck has zero cards in it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Codex
--- CONTENT: It is public knowledge which action cards a player takes usingThe Codex.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Thalnos
--- CONTENT: A player may only reroll combat rolls withThe Crown of Thalnos. They cannot reroll anti–fighter barrage rolls and similar.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Thalnos
--- CONTENT: If a unit rolls multiple combat dice, it will not be destroyed if it produces at least one hit from its original roll, and that dice is not rerolled, even if it produces no hits from its reroll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Thalnos
--- CONTENT: A reroll caused by any other effect will not cause a unit to be destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Thalnos
--- CONTENT: Units destroyed byThe Crown of Thalnosare destroyed at the end of theRoll Dicestep, before theAssign Hitsstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Thalnos
--- CONTENT: A unit with theSustain Damageability cannot use it to avoid being destroyed when it fails to produce a hit with the reroll fromThe Crown of Thalnos.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Dynamis Core
--- CONTENT: If a player uses the purge ability ofDynamis Core, they will need to return commodities if they now exceed their original commodity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: JR–XS455–O
--- CONTENT: JR–XS455–Ois an agent. All rules that apply to agents (and leaders) apply toJR–XS455–O.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Maw of Worlds
--- CONTENT: The player does not have to meet the prerequisites of the technologies they acquire usingMaw of Worlds.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Metali Void Shielding
--- CONTENT: The affected ship may be destroyed by theDirect Hitaction card after it uses theSustain Damageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Metali Void Shielding
--- CONTENT: A player may play theReflective Shieldingaction card after it uses theSustain Damageability viaMetali Void Shielding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Metali Void Shielding
--- CONTENT: If a player ownsMetali Void Shielding, and their opponent plays theWaylayaction card, they may useMetali Void Shieldingfor both theAnti–Fighter Barrageand combat rolls in that round of space combat.

--- SECTION_ID: Metali Void Shielding
--- CONTENT: Metali Void Shieldinghas no effect when the Argent player resolves theirRaid Formationfaction ability.

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Nano–Forge
--- CONTENT: The attached planet will not have a corresponding legendary planet ability card. However, it will be legendary for effects such as scoring theMake Historypublic objective and similar objectives, transferring theShard of the Thronerelic, and the Winnu player's commander, Rickar Rickani. The attached planet will also no longer be non–legendary for effects such as theStellar Converterrelic.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: A player may useNeuraloopto purgeNeuraloopitself, resolving its ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: A player may useNeuraloopto purgeNano–Forge, even if it is attached to a planet, if they control that planet. That planet loses the increase to its resources and influence values, and is no longer legendary.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto purge another relic that has a purge ability, that purge ability is not resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto purge theCirclet of the Void, that player’s units may remain in and move out of any supernovae and/or asteroid fields they are currently in, but cannot move additional units into or through, unless they have another ability that would allow them to do so, such as theAntimass Deflectorstechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto purge theDynamis Core, and they have more commodities than their faction’s printed commodity value, they return any extras to the supply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto purgeThe Obsidian, that player must discard one unscored secret objective if they have a total of four scored or unscored secret objectives. There is no effect if they have four scored secret objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto purge theShard of the Throne, that player loses a victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto purge another relic, then that player may useNeuraloopagain to replace the new objective with yet another objective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: If a player usesNeuraloopto reveal a secret objective as a public objective, that objective does not count towards the limit of three scored or unscored secret objectives for any player that scores it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: A player can score a maximum of one objective of any type during or after each combat. A player cannot score the secret objective revealed byNeuraloopand one of their own secret objectives from the same combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: A secret objective revealed byNeuraloopbecomes a public objective and stops being a secret objective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Neuraloop
--- CONTENT: The discarded objective is shuffled into its respective deck after the replacement objective is revealed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Prophet’s Tears
--- CONTENT: A player cannot use the ability ofThe Prophet’s Tearswhen they directly gain a technology.

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: The Prophet’s Tears
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player may use the ability ofThe Prophet’s Tearsto draw an action card when they would have researched a technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Emelpar
--- CONTENT: If a player has no command tokens in their reinforcements, they must use a command token from their command sheet instead when they use the ability of theScepter of Emelpar.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Emelpar
--- CONTENT: TheScepter of Emelparmay be used whenever a command token would be spent from a player’s strategy pool. This includes when spending to perform the secondary ability of a strategy card, for faction abilities, and when scoring objectives.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Emelpar
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat player uses the ability of theScepter of Emelpar, they will not gain a trade good from the ability of their commander, Magmus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Shard of the Throne
--- CONTENT: When the player that owns theShard of the Throneloses control of a legendary planet or a planet in their home system, they immediately give it to the player who gained control of that planet. No abilities may be resolved before this.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Shard of the Throne
--- CONTENT: If the player that gainsShard of the Thronecontrols no legendary planets or planets in their home system, they cannot lose it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Converter
--- CONTENT: The chosen planet must be in a system adjacent to the unit withbombardment; the planet and unit cannot both be in the same system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Converter
--- CONTENT: A system that contains a planet destroyed byStellar Converter, and no other planets, is considered to contain no planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Relics
--- SECTION_ID: Stellar Converter

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a ship moves, it may transport any combination of fighters and ground forces, but the number of units it transports cannot exceed that ship’s capacity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The ship can pick up and transport fighters and ground forces when it moves. During a tactical action, it can pick up and transport units from the active system, the system it started its movement in, and each system it moves through.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Any fighters and ground forces that a ship transports must move with the ship and remain in the space area of a system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Fighters and ground forces cannot be picked up from a system that contains one of their faction’s command tokens other than the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can land ground forces on a planet in a system during theInvasionstep of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship that can both move and be transported (i.e. Fighter II) cannot do both by “meeting” a ship with capacity partway through a tactical action movement, as all movement is simultaneous.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship may transport as it retreats or is otherwise moved out of the active system, as the units it transports will be picked up from the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship may pick up ground forces from a planet in the active system, usually to invade a different planet in the same system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship cannot pick up more units from a planet than it has capacity. However, a ship may pick up any units (including none) in a system as it transports, even if doing so would cause units to be removed due to capacity limits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will allow a player’s ships to transport units from systems that contain that player’s command token when those ships move outside of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Capacity
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Ground Forces
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Transport
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A system tile represents an area of the galaxy. Players place system tiles during setup to create the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The back of each system tile is colored green, blue, or red.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: System tiles with a green–colored back are home systems and faction–specific tiles. Each home system is unique to one of the game’s factions.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: System tiles with a blue–colored back each contain one or more planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: System tiles with a red–colored back are anomalies or are systems that do not contain planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Planets are located in systems. Ground forces and structures are usually placed on planets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Any area on a system tile that is not a planet is space. Ships are usually placed in the space area.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Double–sided tiles that have lines crossing from one edge to another are hyperlane tiles. Hyperlane tiles are not systems.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Active System
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Adjacency
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Anomalies
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Game Board
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: System Tiles

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Wormholes
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The wormhole nexus is a system tile where several wormholes converge.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The wormhole nexus begins the game in play with its inactive side up.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a player moves or places a unit into the wormhole nexus, or gains control of the planet Mallice, that player flips the wormhole nexus to its active side.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The wormhole nexus will flip if a unit exists in the system while inactive, even if that unit did not move through a gamma wormhole.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: As the wormhole nexus becomes active at the end of theMovementstep, only units with theDeep Space Cannonability in systems containing a gamma wormhole will be able to produce hits during theSpace Cannon Offensestep during that action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If the Creuss player moves theirHil Colishflagship into the inactive wormhole nexus, the wormhole nexus will not flip before they move any other ships. Any other ships they wish to move into the wormhole nexus must do so via either a delta wormhole or a gamma wormhole, unless the Creuss player is utilizing the ability of their agent, Emissary Taivra.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Any units and tokens on the inactive side are transferred to the active side when the wormhole nexus flips.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A ship in the wormhole will single–handedly qualify for theBecome the Gatekeeperobjective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Movement
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: System Tiles
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Wormhole Nexus
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Wormholes
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Munitions Reserves
--- CONTENT: Munitions Reservesmay only be triggered once per round. The Letnev player cannot spend four (or more) trade goods to get two (or more) rerolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Armada
--- CONTENT: If the Letnev player has zero command tokens in their fleet pool, they may still have ships on the game board. While this is the case, effects that remove command tokens from a player’s fleet pool cannot affect the Letnev player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: War Funding(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may playWar Fundingwhen the Letnev player has zero or one trade goods. The Letnev player will lose the single trade good, if applicable, and the other effects will resolve as normal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: War Funding(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may receiveWar Fundingin a transaction during a combat. If received at the start of a round, that player may play it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: War Funding Ω(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may receiveWar Funding Ωin a transaction during a combat. If received after dice are rolled, that player may play it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: War Funding Ω(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may only reroll combat rolls withWar Funding Ω. They cannot reroll anti–fighter barrage rolls and similar.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: L4 Disruptors(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A player may still use theSpace Cannonability of their units against the Letnev player’s ships during theSpace Cannon Offensestep in this system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Non–Euclidean Shielding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Non–Euclidean Shieldingmay be applied when a Dunlain Reaper uses itsSustain damageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Non–Euclidean Shielding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Non–Euclidean Shieldingapplies whenever hits are produced. This includes hits produced byBombardmentandSpace Cannonabilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Non–Euclidean Shielding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If there are multiple hits that can be cancelled, then the Letnev player must cancel two hits whenever one of their units uses itsSustain damageability; they cannot cancel just one.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Non–Euclidean Shielding(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Say the Letnev player has exactly one hit produced against them remaining, and one of their units uses itsSustain damageability to cancel it. If additional hits are produced against the Letnev player's units, such as with theReflective Shieldingaction card, the Letnev player cannot retroactively use the previous use ofSustain damageto allowNon–Euclidean Shieldingto cancel a second hit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Arc Secundus(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: TheArc Secundusis not repaired at the end of combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Arc Secundus(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: TheArc Secundusonly uses its repair ability during combats it is participating in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Arc Secundus(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: If the ability of theArc Secundusresults in no units on a planet having thePlanetary Shieldability, then the ability of theMagen Defense Gridtechnology cannot be used during ground combat on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Viscount Unlenn(Agent)
--- CONTENT: This ability only applies to combat rolls. It does not apply to dice rolls for a unit’sAnti–Fighter Barrageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Viscount Unlenn(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The extra dice is mandatory for the chosen unit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Rear Admiral Farran(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Letnev player has more ships in a system than allowed for by their fleet pool plusArmada, they must first remove ships to meet this limit before they can unlock Rear Admiral Farran.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Rear Admiral Farran(Commander)
--- CONTENT: This effect may be applied when a Dunlain Reaper uses itsSustain damageability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Rear Admiral Farran(Commander)
--- CONTENT: A unit that becomes damaged without using itsSustain Damageability will not trigger this effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Rear Admiral Farran(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If multiple units use theirSustain Damageability within a single step, the trade goods are gained one at a time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Darktalon Treilla — Dark Matter Affinity(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The game round ends after the agenda phase (or the status phase if the custodians token is yet to be removed from Mecatol Rex).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Darktalon Treilla — Dark Matter Affinity(Hero)
--- CONTENT: At the end of the game round the Letnev player might need to remove ships from the board to satisfy fleet pool limits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Dunlain Reaper(Mech)
--- CONTENT: ADeployability may be resolved only once per timing window. As such, the Letnev player may only place one Dunlain Reaper this way per ground combat round.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Dunlain Reaper(Mech)
--- CONTENT: ADeployability may only be resolved for units in a player’s reinforcements. If all four Dunlain Reapers are already on the board, no Dunlain Reaper may be deployed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Gravleash Maneuvers(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If a ship has its movement value increased by an ability such as theGravity Drivetechnology, then other ships will have their movement values increased to match the modified value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Gravleash Maneuvers(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The ship with the highest move value in a system may increase the move value of other ships that move from that system, even if the ship with the highest move value itself does not move during that action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Barony of Letnev
--- SECTION_ID: Gravleash Maneuvers(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Letnev player owns the Fighter II unit upgrade technology, another ship may have its move value increased to match that of a Fighter II in that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Influence
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Influence represents a planet’s political power. Players spend influence to gain command tokens using theLeadershipstrategy card, and the influence values of planets are used to cast votes during the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Influence
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A planet’s influence is the rightmost value (surrounded by a blue border) found on the planet’s system tile and planet card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Influence
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can spend a planet’s influence by exhausting that planet’s card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Influence
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can spend a trade good as if it were one influence.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Influence
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Agenda Phase
##################################################
