### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Assimilate
--- CONTENT: Any space docks that are placed by this ability during a tactical action may produce units during theProductionstep of that tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Assimilate
--- CONTENT: If the L1Z1X player resolves theirAssimilateability, and then plays theInfiltrateaction card, or vice versa, they will replace zero PDS and space docks with zero PDS and space docks when they resolve the latter ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Assimilate
--- CONTENT: If the L1Z1X player would have to place a structure, but there are none of that type left in their reinforcements, they may remove a structure of that type from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Assimilate
--- CONTENT: The L1Z1X player must mandatorily replace every structure. However, if there are none of that type in their reinforcements they are not forced to do so.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Harrow
--- CONTENT: ThePlanetary Shieldability will prevent the use of theHarrowability on a planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Harrow
--- CONTENT: The L1Z1X player cannot use theirHarrowability if they are not the active player. This will most commonly occur due to the effect of the N’orr player’s commander, G’hom Sek’kus.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Harrow
--- CONTENT: The L1Z1X player may use theirHarrowability at the end of the round in which their last ground force was destroyed. This may cause the combat to end in a draw.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Harrow
--- CONTENT: During theBombardmentstep, each of the L1Z1X player’s units with theBombardmentability is assigned only one planet to bombard. However, during ground combat, every unit in the system with theBombardmentability may use it against the planet the ground combat is taking place on.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Harrow
--- CONTENT: The L1Z1X player may use the ability of theX–89 Bacterial Weapon ΩorX–89 Bacterial Weapon ΩΩtechnologies whenever they bombard.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Cybernetic Enhancements(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If the L1Z1X player has no command tokens in their strategy pool,Cybernetic Enhancementscannot be played.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Inheritance Systems(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The two resources forInheritanceSystems must be paid in addition to and separately from any other costs paid to research the technology. For example, if the L1Z1X player is performing the secondary of theTechnologystrategy card, they cannot spend the five resources of [0.0.0] plus one trade good to pay for the costs of bothTechnologyandInheritance Systems. Instead, they would have to spend [0.0.0] to pay for the cost ofTechnology, wasting the fifth resource, then spend two trade goods to pay for the cost ofInheritance Systems.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: I48S(Agent)
--- CONTENT: The infantry must be in the system when it is activated for it to be eligible to be replaced. It cannot be replaced if it is moved into or produced in the active system later in the turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: I48S(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to place a mech, but there are none left in their reinforcements, they may remove a mech from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. The mech will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: 2RAM(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Those units still havePlanetary Shield. The player that owns those units may still use the ability of theMagen Defense Gridtechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: The Helmsman — Dark Space Navigation(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships in systems with one of the L1Z1X player’s command tokens may move.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: The Helmsman — Dark Space Navigation(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships may transport units only if their origin system does not contain one of the L1Z1X player’s command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: The Helmsman — Dark Space Navigation(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships move directly to their destination system. They may only transport units from their origin system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: The Helmsman — Dark Space Navigation(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships moving out of a gravity rift must roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: The Helmsman — Dark Space Navigation(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships cannot move into a nebula or supernova, even if it contains one of the L1Z1X player’s command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: The Helmsman — Dark Space Navigation(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Dark Space Navigationmay be used to move ships into the wormhole nexus. If the nexus is inactive, this will cause it to activate.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Annihilator(Mech)
--- CONTENT: An Annihilator may bombard when using the L1Z1X player’sHarrowability if that mech is not currently participating in ground combat, even if it has been committed to a different planet, and has been or will be involved in another ground combat during the current invasion.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Annihilator(Mech)
--- CONTENT: An Annihilator may bombard any one planet during theBombardmentstep of an invasion.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Fealty Uplink(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the L1Z1X player gains control of an uncontrolled planet, they may choose if they place the infantry before or after they explore the planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The L1Z1X Mindnet
--- SECTION_ID: Fealty Uplink(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The L1Z1X player must mandatorily place the infantry.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Abandoned Warehouses
--- CONTENT: A player cannot have more commodities than their commodity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Cultural Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: If the relic deck is empty, a player may still purge three Cultural Relic Fragments as an action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Cultural Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: If an eliminated player had any Cultural Relic Fragments, they are discarded to the cultural planet exploration discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Dead World
--- CONTENT: If the relic deck is empty,Dead Worldwill be discarded with no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Demilitarized Zone
--- CONTENT: After the active player has returned ground forces on the planet to the space area, if they do not have enough capacity in the space area for the returned ground forces, including zero capacity, they will have to remove fighters and/or ground forces to meet capacity limits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Derelict Vessel
--- CONTENT: A player with three scored secret objectives may draw a fourth. However, they must immediately shuffle it into the secret objective deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Enigmatic Device
--- CONTENT: A player cannot playEnigmatic Deviceas a component action if they have less than six resources available.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Freelancers
--- CONTENT: A planet may be exhausted to spend its influence or resources, but not both.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Freelancers
--- CONTENT: If a player is to gain multiple planets in a system, they choose the order in which they gain them, and explore each planet as they gain it before gaining the next. As such, a player cannot place ground forces produced byFreelancerson a planet in the active system that they are yet to gain and explore.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Freelancers
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to place a unit, but there are none of that type left in their reinforcements, they may remove a unit of that type from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. This unit will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Functioning Base
--- CONTENT: A player cannot have more commodities than their commodity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Hazardous Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: If the relic deck is empty, a player may still purge three Hazardous Relic Fragments as an action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Hazardous Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: If an eliminated player had any Hazardous Relic Fragments, they are discarded to the hazardous planet exploration discard pile.

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards

--- CONTENT: If the relic deck is empty, a player may still purge three Industrial Relic Fragments as an action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Industrial Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: If an eliminated player had any Industrial Relic Fragments, they are discarded to the industrial planet exploration discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Ion Storm
--- CONTENT: The active player chooses which side of the Ion Storm token is initially face up.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Ion Storm
--- CONTENT: All ship movement is simultaneous. If the Ion Storm token system is the active system, and the token is currently on the alpha side, a player cannot move a ship from a system with an alpha wormhole, flip the token, then move a ship from a system with the beta wormhole (then flip the token again).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Ion Storm
--- CONTENT: If the Ion Storm token is in a system containing a wormhole of the same type, a player chooses which wormhole they use when moving through a wormhole of that type. The Ion Storm token only flips if it was the chosen wormhole.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Ion Storm
--- CONTENT: If ships are moved through the Ion Storm token wormhole outside of theMove ShiporRetreatsubsteps of a tactical action, such as by the effect of theSkilled Retreataction card, the Ion Storm token is not flipped.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Local Fabricators
--- CONTENT: A player cannot have more commodities than their commodity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Local Fabricators
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to place a mech, but there are none left in their reinforcements, they may remove a mech from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. The mech will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Unknown Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: A player cannot purge three Unknown Relic Fragments to gain a relic. At least one cultural, hazardous or industrial relic fragment must be purged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Exploration Cards
--- SECTION_ID: Unknown Relic Fragment
--- CONTENT: If an eliminated player had any Unknown Relic Fragments, they are discarded to the frontier exploration discard pile.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A nebula is an anomaly that affects movement and combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ship can only move into a nebula if it is the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A ship that begins theMovementstep of a tactical action in a nebula treats its move value as “1” for the duration of that step.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a space combat occurs in a nebula, the defender applies +1 to each combat roll of their ships during that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot retreat (or similar) into a nebula, since it would not be the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The +1 modifier for the defender does not modify anti–fighter barrage, bombardment or space cannon rolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The +1 modifier for the defender has no effect during ground combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will place the ship movement restrictions of anomalies upon all units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Nebula
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A future rule change will allow ships to move into a nebula when it is not the active system.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Active System

--- SECTION_ID: Military Support(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Military Supportmay be played when the Sol player has no command tokens in their strategy pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Military Support(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: A player may receiveMilitary Supportin a transaction during the Sol player’s turn. If received at the start of the Sol player’s turn, that player may play it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Genesis(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: Placing the infantry during the status phase is mandatory. After, the Sol player might need to remove an infantry or fighter to meet capacity limits.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Evelyn DeLouis(Agent)
--- CONTENT: This ability only applies to combat rolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Claire Gibson(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If an invasion involves ground combat on multiple planets, an infantry will be placed on each.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Claire Gibson(Commander)
--- CONTENT: If the Sol player has no ground forces on a planet they control, ground combat will not occur, and so they cannot place an infantry on that planet. This includes if they lose the last of their ground forces during theBombardmentstep of the invasion.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Claire Gibson(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The start of ground combat occurs after theSpace Cannon Defensestep. If all of the ground forces committed to a planet are destroyed in that step, then the ground combat will be skipped on that planet, and this ability will not trigger.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Bellum Gloriosum(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Sol player produces multiple ships simultaneously, the combined capacity is used to determine how many fighters and ground forces do not count towards theProductionlimit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Federation of Sol
--- SECTION_ID: Bellum Gloriosum(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The additional fighters and ground forces are produced simultaneously with any other fighters and ground forces, and the resources paid will be determined by their combined cost.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A unit that has theSpace Cannonability can use it during two different steps of a player’s tactical action: after theMove Shipssubstep (Space Cannon Offense) and during an invasion (Space Cannon Defense).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player isnotrequired to be the active player to use theirSpace Cannonability of their units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – Roll Dice: The player rolls dice for each of their units in the active system that has theSpace Cannonability; this is a space cannon roll. One hit is produced for each result that is equal to or greater than the unit’sSpace Cannonvalue.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: This ability can be used even if no ships were moved during theMove Shipsstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Assign Hits: The player whose units have been targeted bySpace Cannonmust choose and destroy one of their ships in the active system for each hit result produced against their units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1 – Roll Dice: Each player may use theSpace Cannonability of each of their units on the invaded planet by rolling a specific number of dice for each of those units; this is called a space cannon roll. A hit is produced for each die roll that is equal to or greater than the unit’sSpace Cannonvalue.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2 – Assign Hits: The active player must choose and destroy one of their ground forces on the planet for each hit the space cannon roll produced.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: “Deep Space Cannon” is not a term with meaning within the rules. It is, however, used within the notes on this website as a shorthand forSpace Cannonabilities that can be used against ships in an adjacent system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: TheSpace Cannon Offensestep happens before combat. Any secret objectives that require winning a combat or similar cannot be scored if all of one player’s ships in a system are destroyed during this step.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player chooses to use theSpace Cannonability of their units, they must do so for all of their eligible units with theSpace Cannonability. This includes units in adjacent systems, if applicable.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may use theSustain Damageability of a ship in the active system to cancel a hit produced during theSpace Cannon Offensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may use theSustain Damageability of a mech committed to a planet to cancel a hit produced during theSpace Cannon Defensestep by a unit on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If multiple players are resolving theSpace Cannonability of their units against the active player, the active player must resolve capacity limits after assigning one player’s hits and before the next player makes their space cannon roll.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot assign hits produced by a space cannon roll to their own units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Space Cannon (Unit Ability)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The “0” side of the d10 represents a result of 10.
##################################################

--- CONTENT: If a player gains then loses theAntimass Deflectorstechnology, their units may remain in and move out of any asteroid fields they are currently in, but cannot move additional units into or through.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Radical Advancement(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Deepwrought player replaces theAntimass Deflectorstechnology, their units may remain in and move out of any asteroid fields they are currently in, but cannot move additional units into or through.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Radical Advancement(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The Deepwrought player may replaceRadical Advancementitself for a biotic technology with two prerequisites.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Aello(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Deepwrought player does not have the capability to prevent other players from using the ability of Aello.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Ta Zern — Wave Function Collapse(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If they also owned the purged technology, the Deepwrought player too will research another technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Ta Zern — Wave Function Collapse(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player purges a technology, they will gain three command tokens instead of researching another technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Visionaria Select(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: WhenVisionaria Selectis exhausted, all other players have the opportunity to participate; the Deepwrought player does not choose which players will participate.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Visionaria Select(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Deepwrought player already owns a technology that a participating player researches, then the Deepwrought player will not gain a technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Deepwrought Scholarate
--- SECTION_ID: Visionaria Select(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Nekro player participates, they will gain three command tokens. The Deepwrought player will not gain a technology this way.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Zeal
--- CONTENT: Additional votes must be cast for the same outcome as the other votes the Argent player cast.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Zeal
--- CONTENT: The Argent player always votes first, even if they are the speaker.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Zeal
--- CONTENT: Other players vote in their regular order after the Argent player votes; clockwise starting with the player to the left of the speaker (skipping over the Argent player as necessary).
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Raid Formation
--- CONTENT: TheAnti–Fighter Barragestep happens during each space combat, even if no fighters are present in the system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Raid Formation
--- CONTENT: Raid Formationoccurs when hits are produced, not after hits are assigned. As such, cancelling any hits will not prevent an opponent’s ships from becoming damaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Raid Formation
--- CONTENT: The Argent player may choose a damaged ship. This will have no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Raid Formation
--- CONTENT: The chosen ship becomes damaged, it does not use itsSustain Damageability. As such, effects that trigger when a ship uses itsSustain Damageability, such as theDirect HitorReflective Shieldingaction cards, cannot be played.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Raid Formation
--- CONTENT: If the Argent player plays theWaylayaction card, hits in excess of their opponent’s fighters will first cause chosen ships to become damaged, then those same hits must still be assigned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Raid Formation
--- CONTENT: If the Argent player is in combat with the Nekro player, and the Nekro player has their mechs participating in the space combat via the effects ofThe Alastor, those mechs may become damaged by the effect ofRaid Formation.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Aerie Hololattice(Technology)
--- CONTENT: The planet with “Production1” is considered to be on itself for the purposes of producing ground forces.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Aerie Hololattice(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A player with theLight/Wave Deflectortechnology cannot move their ships through systems containing the Argent player's structures, if the Argent player ownsAerie Hololattice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Strike Wing Alpha(Unit)
--- CONTENT: When a Strike Wing Alpha II rolls a 9 or 10 for theiranti–fighter barrageability, infantry are destroyed at the end of theRoll Dicestep. This occurs before any ship may use itsSustain Damageability at the start of theAssign Hitsstep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Strike Wing Alpha(Unit)
--- CONTENT: Effects that cancel hits, such as theShields Holdingaction card, cannot prevent the infantry from being destroyed. If an effect rerolls any anti–fighter barrage dice, the new result will determine how many infantry are destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Strike Wing Alpha(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If the last of a player’s ground forces are destroyed by the ability of a Strike Wing Alpha II, and that player meets the other conditions for elimination, that player is immediately eliminated. All of their units are removed from the board, and the Argent player wins the combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Quetzecoatl(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: A player may still use theSpace Cannonability of their units against the Argent player’s ground forces during theSpace Cannon Defensestep of an invasion in this system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Trrakan Aun Zulok(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Ships that gainBombardmentdue to theBlitzaction card will contribute to the unlock condition.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Trrakan Aun Zulok(Commander)
--- CONTENT: “Combat” is a unit attribute, not a unit ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Fighters may be moved without being transported.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships in systems with one of the Argent player’s command tokens may move.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships may transport units only if their origin system does not contain one of the Argent player’s command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships move directly to their destination system. They may only transport units from their origin system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships moving out of a gravity rift must roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Ships cannot move into a nebula or supernova, even if it contains one of the Argent player’s command tokens.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Mirik Aun Sissiri — Helix Protocol(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Helix Protocolmay be used to move ships into the wormhole nexus. If the nexus is inactive, this will cause it to activate.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Aerie Sentinel(Mech)
--- CONTENT: An Aerie Sentinel cannot be transported by a ship without a capacity value.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Argent Flight
--- SECTION_ID: Wing Transfer(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Argent player produces units on their turn in the active system, they will have to satisfy fleet pool and capacity limits there before they may move units to adjacent systems.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player who is eliminated is no longer part of the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player is eliminated when they meetallof the following three conditions:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player becomes eliminated, all of the units, command tokens, control tokens, promissory notes, technologies, command sheets, and the faction sheet that matches that player’s faction or color are returned to the game box, including those in their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player becomes eliminated, all agenda cards they own are discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player becomes eliminated, each promissory note they have that matches another player’s faction or color is returned to that player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player becomes eliminated, each action card in their hand is discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player becomes eliminated, their strategy cards are returned to the common play area whether those cards have been exhausted or not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player becomes eliminated, their secret objectives are shuffled back into the secret objective deck whether those secret objectives have been completed or not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the speaker becomes eliminated, the speaker token passes to the player to the speaker’s left.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a game that started with five or more players becomes a game with four or fewer players due to elimination, the players continue to select only one strategy card during the strategy phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When players are eliminated, faction–specific components interact with the game as follows:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player becomes eliminated, any units they have captured are returned to the reinforcements of their original owners.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: While the Arborec flagship may produce units, it does not have theProductionability. Having it on the game board will not prevent the Arborec player from being eliminated. This applies to all similar effects in the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: An eliminated player’s home system remains a home system for game effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If an eliminated player had any relic fragments, they are discarded to their respective exploration discard piles. If an eliminated player had any relics, they are purged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Elimination
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is eliminated, any of their units that are captured remain with the player that captured them. When the capturing player would return them, the units are instead returned to the game box.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Indoctrination
--- CONTENT: Indoctrinationis limited to once per ground combat.

--- SECTION_ID: Indoctrination
--- CONTENT: If an invasion involves ground combats on multiple planets,Indoctrinationmay be used at the start of each of them.

--- SECTION_ID: Indoctrination
--- CONTENT: If the Yin player’s opponent only has mechs in the ground combat,Indoctrinationcannot be used.

--- SECTION_ID: Indoctrination
--- CONTENT: If the last of a player’s ground forces in a ground combat are removed byIndoctrination, that player loses the combat immediately. They will be unable to use any “start of combat” abilities.

--- CONTENT: When resolvingDevotion, the Yin player chooses which ship is assigned the hit.

--- CONTENT: TheShields Holdingaction card may be used to cancel the hit.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood

--- CONTENT: If a player retreats, the Yin player will be unable to useDevotionto destroy an opponent’s ship.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Devotion
--- CONTENT: If the Yin player is in a combat with the N’orr player, then the two players will alternate when resolving end of combat round abilities, starting with the attacker.

--- SECTION_ID: Greyfire Mutagen(Promissory Note)

--- SECTION_ID: Impulse Core(Technology)
--- CONTENT: When resolvingImpulse Core, the Yin player’s opponent chooses which ship is assigned the hit.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood

--- CONTENT: Effects that cancel hits, such as theSustain Damageability, may be used to cancel a hit produced byImpulse Core.

--- CONTENT: Impulse Corewill resolve before theAnti–Fighter Barragestep of a space combat. As such, any destroyed destroyers will not make an anti–fighter barrage roll.

--- CONTENT: The two infantry must be placed together.

--- SECTION_ID: Van Hauge(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: When theVan Haugeis destroyed, it will not destroy any of the Saar player’s Floating Factories present in the system.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Van Hauge(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: TheVan Haugewill not destroy ground forces in the system. However, each player must then remove ground forces, if necessary, from the space area of that system to meet capacity limits.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Van Hauge(Flagship)
--- CONTENT: As both players will have zero ships in the active system after the Van Hauge is destroyed, the combat will end in a draw.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Brother Milor(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If all of a player’s ships are destroyed during combat, they may still place ships with this ability. If they do, combat will continue.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Brother Milor(Agent)
--- CONTENT: Capacity is not checked during combat. As such a player may use Brother Milor to place fighters into a space combat where they have no spare capacity. After that combat ends, that player must remove fighters and/or ground forces to meet their capacity limit in that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Brother Milor(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Yin player uses Brother Milor after theVan Haugeis destroyed during a space combat, they will win that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Brother Milor(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If all ships in the system are destroyed, and there are excess hits that have not been assigned to a ship, those hits will lapse, and cannot be assigned to the newly placed fighters.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Yin Brotherhood
--- SECTION_ID: Brother Milor(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If all ships in the system are destroyed by hits produced from a space cannon roll, the player that produced those hits may score theTurn Their Fleets to Dustsecret objective before the new fighters are placed.

--- SECTION_ID: Brother Milor Ω(Agent)

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Technology cards allow players to upgrade units and acquire powerful abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player places any technology they have gained faceup near their faction sheet. For the duration of the game, theyownany technology cards they gain and can use the abilities on those cards.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player does not own any technology card that is in their technology deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player can gain a technology card from their technology deck by researching technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Any technology card that a player has not gained remains in their technology deck. A player can look through their technology deck at any time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If an ability instructs a player togaina technology, they do not research it; they take it from their technology deck and place it in their play area, ignoring prerequisites.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some technologies are unit upgrades. Unit upgrades share a name with a unit that is printed on a player’s faction sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each technology that is not a unit upgrade has a colored symbol displayed in the lower–right corner of the card and on its card back that indicates that technology’s color.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Most technology cards have a column of colored symbols displayed in the lower–left corner of the card. Each symbol in this column is a prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To research technology, a player gains that technology card from their technology deck and places it in their play area near their faction sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot research a faction technology that does not match their faction.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When researching technology, a player must satisfy each of a technology’s prerequisites to research it. To satisfy a technology’s prerequisites, that player must own one technology of the matching color for each prerequisite symbol on the technology card they wish to research.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When researching technology, a player can exhaust a planet they control that has a technology specialty to ignore one prerequisite symbol of the matching type on the technology card they are researching.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the planet card is already exhausted, it cannot be used to ignore a prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Basic units printed on faction sheets are not technologies and are not eligible targets forValefar Assimilator.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player becomes eliminated while one of their technologies has a Valefar Assimilator token on it, the Nekro Virus player places that technology in their play area; it is not removed from the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a Valefar Assimilator token is removed from the SaarFloating Factoryunit upgrade, each of the Nekro Virus’ space docks must be placed on an eligible planet they control in that space dock’s system, or the space dock is returned to their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a Valefar Assimilator token is removed from a war sun unit upgrade and the Nekro Virus player does not have the standard war sun unit upgrade, each of the Nekro Virus player’s war suns are returned to their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The Nekro Virus player may upgrade their units with units of the same type (e.g., “dreadnought” or “infantry”) even if those unit’s names do not match. If the Nekro Virus gains a unit upgrade technology of the same unit type as a unit upgrade technology they already have, the previous upgrade is removed, and they must use the same Valefar Assimilator token that was used to copy the previous upgrade.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a Valefar Assimilator token is on a technology, that technology’s color and type count toward objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is instructed to research a technology by any game effect, that player must meet the prerequisites for the technology they research.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is instructed to gain a technology, that player does not have to meet the prerequisites, although most game effects that do this will specify what technologies may be gained by that effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is playing a faction with a faction–specific unit upgrade, they cannot research the generic upgrade for that unit type.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific generic technologies, see thetechnology notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific generic unit upgrades, see theunit notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Technology
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about a technologies of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attach
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some game effects instruct a player to attach a card to a planet card. The attached card modifies that planet card in some way.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attach
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To attach a card to a planet card, a player places the card with the attach effect partially underneath the planet card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attach
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player gains or loses control of planet that contains a card with an attach effect, the attached card stays with that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attach
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a card is attached to a planet card, place the corresponding attachment token on that planet on the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attach
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: There is no limit on how many attachments a single planet may have.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Attach
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The Custodians Token is not an attachment.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Reinforcements
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player’s reinforcements is that player’s personal supply of units and command tokens that are not on the game board or otherwise in use.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Reinforcements
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The components in a player’s reinforcements are limited.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Reinforcements
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to place a unit, but there are none of that type left in their reinforcements, they may remove a unit of that type from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Reinforcements
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Command tokens on a player’s command sheet are not in that player’s reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Reinforcements
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Captured units are not in any player’s reinforcements.
##################################################
