--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Units
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Anti–Intellectual Revolution
--- CONTENT: WhenAnti–Intellectual Revolutionis a law in play, a player that directly gains a technology will be unaffected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Anti–Intellectual Revolution
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player’sValefar Assimilatortechnologies count for the “Against” effect, whether their tokens are on another player’s faction technology or not.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Anti–Intellectual Revolution
--- CONTENT: A player with no non–fighter ships on the game board may still research technology whenAnti–Intellectual Revolutionis a law in play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Anti–Intellectual Revolution
--- CONTENT: A player may only exhaust planets they control for the “Against” effect ofAnti–Intellectual Revolution.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Archived Secret
--- CONTENT: A player with three scored secret objectives may draw a fourth. However, they must immediately shuffle it into the secret objective deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Archived Secret
--- CONTENT: If a player draws theDrive the Debatesecret objective while resolvingArchived Secret, they cannot score it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Checks and Balances
--- CONTENT: If there are any trade goods on a chosen strategy card whileChecks and Balancesis a law in play, the player who chose the strategy card gains them, not the player who receives that card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Checks and Balances
--- CONTENT: ThePublic Disgraceaction card may be played after a player has chosen a strategy card and announced which player will be receiving it. The player must choose a different strategy card, and then choose the same or a different player to receive it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Clandestine Operations
--- CONTENT: If the “For” effect ofClandestine Operationsis resolved, the removed tokens may be from any pool or pools on a player’s command sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Classified Document Leaks
--- CONTENT: IfClassified Document Leaksis revealed when only one secret objective is in play, players may only vote for that secret objective or abstain. If no votes are cast, the speaker must decide for that secret objective to be elected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Classified Document Leaks
--- CONTENT: The player that originally owned the secret objective elected byClassified Document Leakscannot score it again after it becomes a public objective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Classified Document Leaks
--- CONTENT: The elected secret objective no longer counts towards the original player’s limit of three secret objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Classified Document Leaks
--- CONTENT: IfClassified Document Leaksis discarded, the elected secret objective is not returned to the original player, and it is no longer scorable as a public objective. It remains in play, not discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Classified Document Leaks
--- CONTENT: A player can score a maximum of one objective of any type during or after each combat. A player cannot score the elected objective and one of their own secret objectives from the same combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Classified Document Leaks
--- CONTENT: The elected objective becomes a public objective and stops being a secret objective.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Colonial Redistribution
--- CONTENT: If the player that originally controlled the elected planet has the fewest victory points, they may choose themselves to place an infantry on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Colonial Redistribution
--- CONTENT: If the elected planet has theDemilitarized Zoneexploration card attached, no infantry will be placed on it. Control of the planet will remain with the original player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Committee Formation
--- CONTENT: Committee Formationis resolved after any riders have been played, if the owner so chooses. Riders will resolve if the predicted outcome matches the player elected by the effect ofCommittee Formation.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Committee Formation
--- CONTENT: TheConfusing Legal TextandConfounding Legal Textaction cards may be played afterCommittee Formationhas been discarded to change who the elected player is, which will negate the effects ofCommittee Formation.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Compensated Disarmament
--- CONTENT: All trade goods are gained together.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Compensated Disarmament
--- CONTENT: Each destroyed infantry will provide one trade good and each destroyed mech will provide one trade good.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Compensated Disarmament
--- CONTENT: A planet with zero units on it is eligible to be elected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Compensated Disarmament
--- CONTENT: Structures are unaffected byCompensated Disarmament.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Conventions of War
--- CONTENT: WhenConventions of Waris a law in play a player may still use theTactical Bombardmentaction card, theX–89 Bacterial Weapontechnology or theStellar Converterrelic on a cultural planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Core Mining
--- CONTENT: A planet with zero infantry on it may be elected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Covert Legislation
--- CONTENT: If the Speaker drawsClassified Document Leaks,Judicial Abolishment,Miscount DisclosedorNew Constitution, when that agenda would be discarded if revealed, both the hidden agenda andCovert Legislationare discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Covert Legislation
--- CONTENT: Any effects that take place when or after an agenda is revealed instead take place when or after the speaker has drawn and announced the possible outcomes for the hidden agenda.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Covert Legislation
--- CONTENT: If an effect, such as theVetoaction card, would discardCovert Legislation, both it and the hidden agenda are discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Covert Legislation
--- CONTENT: The hidden agenda is only revealed as it is resolved. All abilities that may be played after voting, such as theBribery,Confounding Legal Text,Confusing Legal TextorDeadly Plotaction cards, must be played before the agenda is revealed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Covert Legislation
--- CONTENT: The speaker may still vote onCovert Legislation.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Emphidia
--- CONTENT: IfThe Crown of Emphidialaw is discarded, no player loses a victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: The Crown of Emphidia
--- CONTENT: If the player that gainsThe Crown of Emphidiacontrols no planets in their home system, they cannot lose it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Economic Equality
--- CONTENT: If the “For” outcome ofEconomic Equalityis resolved, the Mentak player may resolve theirPillagefaction ability against each of their neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Enforced Travel Ban
--- CONTENT: The effect of theEnforced Travel Banlaw does not affect the Creuss player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Enforced Travel Ban
--- CONTENT: Enforced Travel Banonly prevents movement using the normal adjacency provided by wormholes. Other effects that create adjacency, such as theWormhole Reconstructionagenda or theLost Star Chartaction card, may be used to allow movement between systems containing wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Enforced Travel Ban
--- CONTENT: When theEnforced Travel Banlaw is in play, units cannot move through wormholes, even by effects that move ships outside of theMovementstep of a tactical action, such as while retreating.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Enforced Travel Ban
--- CONTENT: When theEnforced Travel Banlaw is in play, hits may still be produced against ships in the active system by units with theDeep Space Cannonability in systems that are adjacent via a wormhole during theSpace Cannon Offensestep of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Enforced Travel Ban
--- CONTENT: Players may still be neighbors via systems that are adjacent via wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Enforced Travel Ban
--- CONTENT: The “Against” effect ofEnforced Travel Banwill affect PDS in or adjacent to systems containing an alpha, beta, delta or gamma wormhole.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Executive Sanctions
--- CONTENT: The effect of theExecutive Sanctionslaw does not affect the Yssaril player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Fleet Regulations
--- CONTENT: The effect of theFleet Regulationslaw does not prevent the Letnev player from using theirArmadafaction ability. They may have up to six non–fighter ships in a system if they have four command tokens in their fleet pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Fleet Regulations
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player may only have up to four command tokens in their fleet pool when theFleet Regulationslaw is in play, regardless of which faction the command tokens belong to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Crisis Pact
--- CONTENT: Players resolve the secondary ability of the elected strategy card in speaker order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Crisis Pact
--- CONTENT: The secondary ability is resolved immediately, during the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Crisis Pact
--- CONTENT: Players must pay the influence or resource costs to resolve the abilities of theLeadership,WarfareorTechnologystrategy cards if they are elected. Any planets used to pay these costs will ready at the end of the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Crisis Pact
--- CONTENT: If theTechnologystrategy card is elected, a player may exhaust a planet with a technology specialty to ignore a prerequisite on a technology as normal. This planet will ready at the end of the agenda phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Galactic Crisis Pact
--- CONTENT: If a player has a strategy card in their play area due to the effect of thePolitical Stabilityaction card, that strategy card is eligible to be elected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Holy Planet of Ixth
--- CONTENT: If theHoly Planet of Ixthlaw is discarded, no player loses a victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Homeland Defense Act
--- CONTENT: If theHomeland Defense Actlaw is discarded, players might have to remove PDS so that they have no more than two on each planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Imperial Arbiter
--- CONTENT: If either strategy card had trade goods on it at the start of the strategy phase, those trade goods remain with the player that originally chose the strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Imperial Arbiter
--- CONTENT: In a three– or four–player game, the owner ofImperial Arbiterchooses which strategy cards are swapped.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Ixthian Artifact
--- CONTENT: A player must still meet the prerequisites for the technology they research.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Ixthian Artifact
--- CONTENT: A player with three or fewer units in a system adjacent to the Mecatol Rex system destroys all of their units in that system. Otherwise, a player chooses which three units are destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Ixthian Artifact
--- CONTENT: All units are destroyed simultaneously.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Ixthian Artifact
--- CONTENT: To cast votes against or to play a rider onIxthian Artifactis to commit heresy.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Judicial Abolishment
--- CONTENT: IfJudicial Abolishmentis revealed when only one law is in play, players may only vote for that law or abstain. If no votes are cast, the speaker must decide for that law to be elected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Commerce
--- CONTENT: Minister of Commercetriggers when its owner has their commodities replenished by any game effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Commerce
--- CONTENT: All trade goods are gained together.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Exploration
--- CONTENT: If the owner ofMinister of Explorationgains control of multiple planets during one invasion, the trade goods are gained one at a time.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Industry
--- CONTENT: All units in that system may use theirProductionability, not just the placed space dock.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Industry
--- CONTENT: The produced units must be paid for.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Industry
--- CONTENT: A space dock cannot be placed on a planet already containing a space dock.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Industry
--- CONTENT: An ability that puts a space dock on the game board by “replacing”, rather than “placing”, such as theInfiltrateaction card, will triggerMinister of Industry.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Peace
--- CONTENT: Once a player resolves the ability ofMinister of Peace, the active player cannot use any “after you activate a system” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Peace
--- CONTENT: The active player may still use any “at the end of your turn” abilities when their turn is ended byMinister of Peace.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Peace
--- CONTENT: The player that ownsMinister of Peacedoes not have to have any of their units in the active system to resolveMinister of Peace, so long as any non–active player owns at least one unit in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Policy
--- CONTENT: The owner ofMinister of Policywill draw action cards during theDraw Action Cardsstep of the status phase, and again at the end of the status phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of Policy
--- CONTENT: Neural Motivatordoes not apply when the owner ofMinister of Policydraws action cards from its effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Minister of War
--- CONTENT: Effects that trigger at the start or end of a player’s turn will not trigger between each of those player’s action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: IfMiscount Disclosedis revealed when only one law is in play, players may only vote for that law or abstain. If no votes are cast, the speaker must decide for that law to be elected.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: The elected law remains in play, and remains elected to the same object if applicable, while it is being voted on.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: Once the law is elected, any riders onMiscount Disclosedwill resolve. Following that, the elected law is then treated as being revealed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: After all players have voted forMiscount Disclosed, theDeadly Plotaction card may be played. If so, the elected law is not voted on and remains in play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: After all players have voted for the elected law, theDeadly Plotaction card may be played. If so, the elected law is discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: Players who resolved a transaction while voting on and resolvingMiscount Disclosedmay resolve an additional transaction voting on and resolving the elected law.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Miscount Disclosed
--- CONTENT: IfHoly Planet of Ixth,Shard of the ThroneorThe Crown of Emphidiais elected byMiscount Disclosed, the owner will not lose a victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Mutiny
--- CONTENT: If the “For” outcome ofMutinyis resolved, players gain victory points in speaker order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: New Constitution
--- CONTENT: If a player controls planets in another player’s home system, those planets are not exhausted by the “For” outcome ofNew Constitution.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Nexus Sovereignty
--- CONTENT: The effect of theNexus Sovereigntylaw does not affect the Creuss player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Nexus Sovereignty
--- CONTENT: When theNexus Sovereigntylaw is in play, units cannot move through the alpha and beta wormholes in the wormhole nexus, even by effects that move ships outside of the movement step of a tactical action, such as while retreating.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Nexus Sovereignty
--- CONTENT: When theNexus Sovereigntylaw is in play, hits may still be produced against ships in the active system by units with theDeep Space Cannonability in systems that are adjacent via a wormhole during theSpace Cannon Offensestep of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Nexus Sovereignty
--- CONTENT: Players may still be neighbors via systems that are adjacent via wormholes.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Political Censure
--- CONTENT: When a player is elected forPolitical Censure, they may play theConfusing Legal TextorDeadly Plotaction cards before it resolves.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Prophecy of Ixth
--- CONTENT: Other effects that produce units without a unit using itsProductionability will not causeProphecy of Ixthto be discarded.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Publicize Weapon Schematics
--- CONTENT: If thePublicize Weapon Schematicslaw is in play, and a player is the first to gain the war sun unit upgrade technology, from then on, prerequisites for the war sun unit upgrade technology will be ignored.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Publicize Weapon Schematics
--- CONTENT: If the Muaat does not own their Prototype War Sun II faction unit upgrade technology, they do not own a war sun technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Publicize Weapon Schematics
--- CONTENT: The Muaat player’s Prototype War Sun will lose itsSustain Damageability, regardless of if the Muaat player owns their Prototype War Sun II faction unit upgrade technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Rearmament Agreement
--- CONTENT: A player that controls no planets in their home system will not place a mech if the “For” outcome of Rearmament Agreement is resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Rearmament Agreement
--- CONTENT: If a player wishes to place a mech, but there are none in their reinforcements, they may remove a mech from any system that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that instead. The mech will be placed undamaged.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Rearmament Agreement
--- CONTENT: A player that has no mechs on the game board is unaffected by the “Against” effect of Rearmament Agreement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Research Grant Reallocation
--- CONTENT: A player may gain any technology, regardless of the number of command tokens in their fleet pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Research Grant Reallocation
--- CONTENT: The number and colors of technologies a player owns will have no effect on the number of command tokens they remove.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Research Team: Biotic
--- CONTENT: The agenda card, not the planet, is exhausted to ignore the prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Research Team: Cybernetic
--- CONTENT: The agenda card, not the planet, is exhausted to ignore the prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Research Team: Propulsion
--- CONTENT: The agenda card, not the planet, is exhausted to ignore the prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Research Team: Warfare
--- CONTENT: The agenda card, not the planet, is exhausted to ignore the prerequisite.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Search Warrant
--- CONTENT: A player with three scored secret objectives may draw a fourth. However, they must immediately shuffle it into the secret objective deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Search Warrant
--- CONTENT: If the elected player has three secret objective cards, and they would draw another, the drawn secret objective card is revealed before that player chooses which card to discard. This applies both when the elected player initially draws the secret objective cards from the effect ofSearch Warrantwhen they are elected, and if they later draw secret objective cards from another effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Search Warrant
--- CONTENT: If a player draws theDrive the Debatesecret objective while resolvingSearch Warrant, they cannot score it immediately.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Seed of an Empire
--- CONTENT: If multiple players have the most or fewest victory points, they gain victory points in speaker order.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Shard of the Throne
--- CONTENT: If theShard of the Thronelaw is discarded, no player loses a victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Shared Research
--- CONTENT: If theShared Researchlaw is in play, a player still cannot move into a nebula unless it is the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Shared Research
--- CONTENT: If theShared Researchlaw is in play, a ship that begins theMovementstep of a tactical action in a nebula still treats its move value as one for the duration of that step.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Swords to Plowshares
--- CONTENT: Mechs are ignored by the “For” effect ofSwords to Plowshares.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Reconstruction
--- CONTENT: WhileWormhole Reconstructionis in play,Enforced Travel Banwill have no effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Reconstruction
--- CONTENT: The “Against” effect ofWormhole Reconstructionwill cause each player to place command tokens in each system that contains an alpha, beta, delta or gamma wormhole and one or more of that player’s ships.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Research
--- CONTENT: A player with ships in a delta or gamma wormhole may research a technology from the “For” effect. Those ships will not be destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Research
--- CONTENT: A player must still meet the prerequisites for the technology they research.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Research
--- CONTENT: Ground forces in the space area of a system containing an alpha or beta wormhole will be removed due to lack of capacity after the ships in that system are destroyed; those ground forces will not trigger any “destroyed” effects. Fighters will be destroyed, and will trigger any “destroyed” effects.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Research
--- CONTENT: IfAnti–Intellectual Revolutionis in play as a law, players who research a technology will destroy a ship due toAnti–Intellectual Revolutionbefore they destroy ships in systems containing alpha or beta wormholes. As such, they may choose a ship in a system containing an alpha or beta wormhole to destroy forAnti–Intellectual Revolution
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Agendas
--- SECTION_ID: Wormhole Research
--- CONTENT: The Saar player’s Floating Factories will not be destroyed byWormhole Research.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategic Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, the active player may perform a strategic action to resolve the primary ability on their strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategic Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability on their strategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may resolve that strategy card’s secondary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategic Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After each player has had an opportunity to resolve a strategy card’s secondary ability, the active player exhausts their strategy card so that it is facedown – this indicates that they cannot use this card again this round and is a reminder that they can now pass during one of their later turns.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategic Action
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player is resolving either the primary or secondary abilities from a strategy card, that player resolves each of the ability’s effects from top to bottom.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategic Action
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Action Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Strategic Action
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Strategy Card
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Units
--- CONTENT: For notes about specific faction unit upgrade technology, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: War Sun
--- CONTENT: A player without the war sun unit upgrade technology cannot produce, place or have a war sun on the board for any reason.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: War Sun
--- CONTENT: If a war sun’s ability results in no units on a planet having thePlanetary Shieldability, then the ability of theMagen Defense Gridtechnology cannot be used during ground combat on that planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Flagship
--- CONTENT: For notes about the flagship of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Fighter
--- CONTENT: Fighters and ground forces do not count towards capacity during combat. As such, any number of Fighter II may be in a system during combat, regardless of capacity and fleet pool. This will usually only be caused by effects that place units in a system during combat. When combat ends however, units will need to be removed to meet capacity and fleet pool requirements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Fighter
--- CONTENT: A ship cannot move through a system that contains Fighter II that are controlled by another player during theMovementstep of a tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Fighter
--- CONTENT: Ships may be moved into, produced in or placed in a system even if doing so would exceed the fleet pool limit. However, some of those ships must immediately be removed to satisfy the limit. If some of those ships are fighters II, they may instead count towards that player’s capacity in that system. If capacity is exceeded, fighters or ground forces must be removed to meet the limit.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Mech
--- CONTENT: See themechs pageof the Rules Reference.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Mech
--- CONTENT: For notes about the mechs of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Infantry
--- CONTENT: If a player controls no planets in their home system, at the start of their turn, any Infantry II that have been placed on that player’s Infantry II unit upgrade technology card are returned to that player’s reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Infantry
--- CONTENT: A player need not use one of their twelve plastic infantry units to represent the infantry on their Infantry II unit upgrade card that will be placed in their home system at the start of their next turn, and may use cardboard infantry tokens to represent any and all of these infantry.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: PDS
--- CONTENT: See thePDS pageof the Rules Reference.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Units
--- SECTION_ID: Space Dock
--- CONTENT: See thespace dock pageof the Rules Reference.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Edict
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player is ever required to remove one of their command tokens from their fleet pool, and they only have other players’ command tokens in their fleet pool, they must remove one of those tokens, and return it to the reinforcements of the player that owns it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Edict
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player is ever limited by the number of tokens they may have in their fleet pool, such as by theFleet Regulationslaw, they may still add a command token to their fleet pool when they are at the limit, but must then remove one command token and return it to the corresponding reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Edict
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player wins a combat against a player that has no command tokens in their reinforcements, and none of their command tokens are on the Mahact player’s command sheet, that player must choose one of their command tokens on their command sheet to remove and place on the Mahact player’s command sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Edict
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player is required to place a command token from their reinforcements on the board, such as when they retreat from a space combat, or the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card, if they have no tokens in their reinforcements, they must use a Mahact token from any pool of their command sheet, and not another player’s token in their fleet pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Edict
--- CONTENT: When the Mahact player wins a space combat, they add the command token to their fleet pool before they resolve fleet pool requirements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Edict
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player wins a combat against the Mentak player and gains one of their command tokens, they cannot resolve the ability of S’ula Mentarion, the Mentak commander, from winning that same combat to take a promissory note from the Mentak player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Hubris
--- CONTENT: If a game effect would force another player to give a promissory note to the Mahact player, but the only promissory note that player has is theirAlliancepromissory note, that player does not give anything to the Mahact player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Dominion(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player already has a command token in the chosen system, they do not place a command token there.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Dominion(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player has no command tokens in their reinforcements, that player places one command token of their choice from their command sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Dominion(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: There is no mechanism to create a binding deal between the Mahact player and another player regarding which system that player will choose when resolvingScepter of Domination.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Dominion(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player will also place a command token in the chosen system, unless their command sheet has none of their own tokens on it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Scepter of Dominion(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Scepter of Dominioncannot place command tokens in the home system of an eliminated player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Genetic Recombination(Technology)
--- CONTENT: A player that cannot vote due to a game effect or because they have zero influence on readied planets cannot be targeted byGenetic Recombination.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Crimson Legionnaire(Unit)
--- CONTENT: If multiple Crimson Legionnaires are destroyed at the same time, the Mahact player decides whether to gain a commodity or convert a commodity to a trade good individually for each.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Jae Mir Kan(Agent)
--- CONTENT: When resolving the secondary ability of theConstructionstrategy card, the active player’s command token is placed in the system the Mahact player places their structure.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Jae Mir Kan(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player has the Muaat player’sAlliancepromissory note, they will not gain a trade good from it when they use the ability of Jae Mir Kan.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Il Na Viroset(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player cannot use any “when/after you activate a system” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Il Na Viroset(Commander)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player may still use any “at the end of your turn” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Fighters and ground forces in the space area of the origin system are moved. Ground forces on planets are left behind.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that trigger when a player moves ships trigger from the perspective of the Mahact player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that trigger when a player’s ships move trigger from the perspective of the player that owns them.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that trigger when a player moves their ships do not trigger.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player may move another player’s ships into an asteroid field only if that player owns theAntimass Deflectorstechnology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player may move another player’s ships into a supernova only if that player owns theMagmus ReactorMuaat factional technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player moves a player’s ships out of a gravity rift, that player must roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player cannot move ships through a wormhole while theEnforced Travel Banlaw is in play.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player cannot move the Creuss player’s ships from a system with an alpha wormhole into a system with a beta wormhole (and no alpha wormhole), or vice versa.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player moves the Muaat player’s war sun, the Muaat player cannot trigger theirNova Seedhero ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The system the combat is taking place in is considered the active system during that combat.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The player whose ships were moved is considered to be the attacker, the other player is considered to be the defender.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: ResolvingBenedictionis not a tactical action. TheActivation,Movement,InvasionandProductionsteps are not resolved.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Airo Shir Aur — Benediction(Hero)
--- CONTENT: Either player in the combat may score theBrave the Void,Darken the Skies,Demonstrate Your Power,Destroy their Greatest Ship,Fight with Precision,Spark a Rebellion, orUnveil Flagshipsecret objectives.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Starlancer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: Once the Mahact player resolves the ability of a Starlancer, the active player cannot use any “after you activate a system” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Starlancer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The active player may still use any “at the end of your turn” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Starlancer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Mahact player may use the ability to end their own turn and gain their own spent command token from their fleet pool.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Starlancer(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Starlancer must be in the system before activation to be able to use its ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Vaults of the Heir(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The purged technology must be one that the Mahact player has in their play area, and not from their technology deck.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Vaults of the Heir(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: Once a technology has been purged, the Mahact player cannot regain it for the remainder of the game.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Vaults of the Heir(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player purges theAntimass Deflectorstechnology, their units may remain in and move out of any asteroid fields they are currently in, but cannot move additional units into or through.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Mahact Gene–Sorcerers
--- SECTION_ID: Vaults of the Heir(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: If the Mahact player purges their War Sun unit upgrade technology, they must remove each of their war suns from the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Fragile
--- CONTENT: TheFragileability does not affect anti–fighter barrage, bombardment or space cannon rolls.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Fragile
--- CONTENT: The effect of theFragileability is mandatory.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Research Agreement(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If the Jol–Nar player will research several technologies in a row, then after each, the player holdingResearch Agreementmay play it. The Jol–Nar player does not decide the next technology they will research until after the player holding theResearch Agreementplays it or declines to.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Research Agreement(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a player receivesResearch Agreementin a transaction immediately after the Jol–Nar player researched a technology, that player may play it immediately to gain that technology.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Research Agreement(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Any deal between the Jol–Nar player and another player regarding whenResearch Agreementwill be played, if made beforeResearch Agreementis exchanged, is non–binding.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Research Agreement(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: If a faction has a faction–specific unit upgrade as one of their faction technologies, they cannot gain that unit upgrade fromResearch Agreementwhen the Jol–Nar player researches the generic version of that unit upgrade.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Research Agreement(Promissory Note)
--- CONTENT: Research Agreementmay be triggered when the Jol–Nar player reseaches a technology outside of theTechnologystrategy card. For example, it may be triggered by theDivert Fundingaction card, theFocused Researchaction card, theReveal Prototypeaction card, theTechnology Rideraction card, theIxthian Artifactagenda, theWormhole Researchagenda, or theEnigmatic Deviceexploration card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: E–Res Siphons(Technology)
--- CONTENT: E–Res Siphonsability is triggered when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the Jol–Nar player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: E–Res Siphons(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the Jol–Nar player’s ships (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeE–Res Siphonsability to trigger.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Spatial Conduit Cylinder(Technology)
--- CONTENT: Other players may use theDeep Space Cannonability of units in the same system as a Jol–Nar player’s unit to produce hits during theSpace Cannon Offensestep.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Spatial Conduit Cylinder(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If the Jol–Nar player moves ships out of a gravity rift, they must still roll for removal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Spatial Conduit Cylinder(Technology)
--- CONTENT: If its move value is high enough, a ship may still travel through other systems as it moves to the active system. This will allow a ship with capacity to transport units as normal from a system it did not start its movement in.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Doctor Sucaban(Agent)
--- CONTENT: If the Jol–Nar player has the Infantry II unit upgrade, any of their infantry removed with Doctor Sucaban will not roll for resurrection.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Ta Zern /Agnlan Oln(Commander)
--- CONTENT: “Combat” is a unit attribute, not a unit ability; Ta Zern cannot reroll combat dice.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Ta Zern /Agnlan Oln(Commander)
--- CONTENT: Ta Zern cannot be used to reroll dice for an Infantry II resurrection ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Rin, The Master’s Legacy — Genetic Memory(Hero)
--- CONTENT: The Jol–Nar player does not have to meet the prerequisites of the technologies they acquire.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Rin, The Master’s Legacy — Genetic Memory(Hero)
--- CONTENT: All replacements happen simultaneously. If this ability returns a specific technology, it cannot then be regained via this ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Rin, The Master’s Legacy — Genetic Memory(Hero)
--- CONTENT: If the Jol–Nar player later gains a technology they returned, they gain it readied.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Shield Paling(Mech)
--- CONTENT: The Shield Paling itself is still affected by theFragileability.

--- CONTENT: The Jol–Nar player cannot useSpecialized Compoundswhen researching a unit upgrade.

--- SECTION_ID: Specialized Compounds(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: A technology with zero or completely ignored prerequisites must still match the color of the planet’s technology specialty to useSpecialized Compounds.

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Specialized Compounds(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Jol–Nar player cannot use a technology specialty planet to both pay for the research withSpecialized Compoundsand to ignore a prerequisite of the researched technology simultaneously.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: The Universities of Jol–Nar
--- SECTION_ID: Specialized Compounds(Breakthrough)
--- CONTENT: The Jol–Nar player cannot use the synergy ability ofSpecialized Compoundsto research a cybernetic technology with a biotic technology specialty planet or vice versa.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A deal is an agreement between two players that may or may not include a transaction that involves physical components.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players can make deals with each other at any time, even if they are not neighbors. However, deals that include a transaction must follow the rules for transactions, including that the players be neighbors.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Deals are binding or non–binding according to the conditions of the deal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the terms of a deal can be resolved immediately, it is a binding deal. When a deal is binding, a player must adhere to the terms of the agreement and whatever transactions, if any, were agreed upon.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If the terms of a deal cannot be resolved immediately, it is a non–binding deal. When a deal is non–binding, a player does not have to adhere to any part of the agreement.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: In general, only the terms of the deal that a player can immediately perform, even without the deal taking place, are binding. For example:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Deals
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The following are further examples of non–binding deals:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Promissory Notes
--- CONTENT: For notes about a promissory notes of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Alliance
--- CONTENT: AnAlliancemust be played by the receiving player as soon as it is received. It cannot be kept secret.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Alliance
--- CONTENT: Allianceis returned when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the other player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Alliance
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the other player’s units (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeAllianceto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Alliance
--- CONTENT: Activating a system containing only a player’s structures will still cause theirAllianceto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Alliance
--- CONTENT: For notes about a commander of a specific faction, see that faction’s notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Ceasefire
--- CONTENT: The active player may still use theSpace Cannonability of any units during theSpace Cannon Offensestep of the tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Ceasefire
--- CONTENT: If a player has units in the active system from before the tactical action in which theirCeasefireis played, those units will remain in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Ceasefire
--- CONTENT: If the active player already has units with capacity in the active system, they may transport ground forces on planets in that system into the space area of that system. Those units may then be committed to invade a planet during this tactical action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Ceasefire
--- CONTENT: If a system containing only a player’s ground forces or structures is activated, that player may still play the active player’sCeasefire.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Ceasefire
--- CONTENT: Ceasefiredoes not prevent a player from producing or placing units in the active system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Political Secret
--- CONTENT: A player may still use abilities from their faction technology, leaders, or mechs after theirPolitical Secrethas been played.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Political Secret
--- CONTENT: If an agenda is discarded, eachPolitical Secretthat has been played is returned. The affected players may vote on the next agenda as normal.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Political Secret
--- CONTENT: The effect ofPolitical Secretdoes not stop a player from using their passive faction ability, only the abilities that player may choose to use.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Support For The Throne
--- CONTENT: ASupport For The Thronemust be played by the receiving player as soon as it is received. It cannot be kept secret.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Support For The Throne
--- CONTENT: Support For The Throneis returned when the system is activated, even if the active player will perform no hostile acts towards the other player this turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Support For The Throne
--- CONTENT: If an effect other than activating a system during a tactical action places a command counter in a system with the other player’s units (for example, the primary ability of theDiplomacystrategy card), this will not causeSupport For The Throneto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Support For The Throne
--- CONTENT: Activating a system containing only a player’s structures will still cause theirSupport For The Throneto be returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Support For The Throne
--- CONTENT: If two players trade theirSupport For The Throneto one another simultaneously, the active player will be the first to gain a victory point.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Agreement
--- CONTENT: If a player has their maximum number of commodities, and is instructed to replenish their commodities, they will take no commodities. However, that player’sTrade Agreementmay be played.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Agreement
--- CONTENT: A player does not have to be neighbors with the player that plays theirTrade Agreementto give them their commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Promissory Notes
--- SECTION_ID: Trade Agreement
--- CONTENT: Trade Agreementcannot be played when a player gains commodities, only when they replenish commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Some abilities instruct a player to capture a unit, preventing the unit’s original owner from using it.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player captures a non–fighter ship or mech, they place it on their faction sheet. When such a unit is returned, it is placed into the reinforcements of the original owner.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A captured non–fighter ship or mech is returned under the following circumstances:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player captures a fighter or infantry, it is placed in its reinforcements instead of on the capturing player’s faction sheet; the capturing player places a fighter or infantry token from the supply on their faction sheet instead.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a captured fighter or infantry is returned, it is placed in the supply.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: While a unit is captured, it cannot be produced or placed by its original owner until it is returned.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If one or more of a player’s space docks is being blockaded, that player cannot capture units from the blockading players.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: For additional information, see theVuil’raith faction notes page.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Units are returned as soon as a space dock is blockaded. If this occurs at the end of theSpace Combatstep of a tactical action, the units will be returned before theInvasionstep, in which the space dock could potentially be destroyed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A captured unit may only be returned to the player that originally owned it, and not to another player.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: The Nekro player and the Yssaril player are able to capture units by copying the Vuil’raith player’s abilities, but they will be unable to spend the captured units.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player is eliminated, any of their units that are captured remain with the player that captured them. When the capturing player would return them, the units are instead returned to the game box.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player captures their own units, they cannot be returned to that player’s reinforcements, unless instructed to do so by a game effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player has all of their units of one type on the game board or captured, and so have none in their reinforcements, and would place a unit of that type, they may remove a unit from any system on the game board that does not contain one of their command tokens and place that unit in their reinforcements, before placing that unit on the game board.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Capture
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player cannot capture fighter or infantry tokens corresponding to units belonging to a player that is blockading one of their space docks.
##################################################

--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Blockaded

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheConstructionstrategy card allows players to construct structures on planets they control. This card’s initiative value is “4”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has theConstructionstrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: To resolve the primary ability on theConstructionstrategy card, the active player may place either one PDS or one space dock on a planet they control. Then, that player may place an additional PDS on a planet they control.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theConstructionstrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend one command token from their strategy pool and place that command token in any system. If that player already has a command token in that system, the spent token is returned to their reinforcements instead. Then, that player places either one PDS or one space dock on a planet they control in that system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: When a player places either a PDS or space dock using theConstructionstrategy card, they take that PDS or space dock from their reinforcements.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may have a maximum of one space dock on each planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may have a maximum of two PDS units on each planet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Structures cannot be placed on the planet with theDemilitarized Zoneexploration card attached.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Construction (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Initiative Order

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Each player has a command sheet that contains a strategy pool, a tactic pool, a fleet pool, a trade good area, and a quick reference.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The pools on the command sheet are where players place their command tokens. Command tokens in a player’s pools are used by that player to perform strategic and tactical actions and to increase the number of ships that player can have in each system.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: The trade good area on the command sheet is where a player places their trade good tokens; trade tokens in a player’s trade good area can be spent by that player as resources, influence, or to resolve certain game effects that require trade goods.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Players who are familiar with the game can hide the quick reference by placing that portion of the command sheet under their faction sheets.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: When a command token is gained, it may be placed in any of the three pools if no specific pool is specified by the gaining effect.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Command Tokens
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Fleet Pool

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics

##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Command Sheet
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Trade Goods
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: TheTradestrategy card allows players to gain trade goods and replenish commodities. This card’s initiative value is “5”.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, if the active player has theTradestrategy card, they can perform a strategic action to resolve that card’s primary ability. To resolve the primary ability on theTradestrategy card, the active player resolves the following effects in order:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 1: The active player gains 3 trade goods.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 2: The active player replenishes their commodities by taking the number of commodity tokens necessary to have an amount equal to the commodity value on their faction sheet. Then, they place those tokens in the commodity area of their faction sheet.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: Step 3: The active player chooses any number of other players. Those players use the secondary ability of this card without spending a command token.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After the active player resolves the primary ability of theTradestrategy card, each other player, beginning with the player to the left of the active player and proceeding clockwise, may spend one command token from their strategy pool to replenish their commodities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Say, for example, Alice is the active player, and is performing a strategic action with theTradestrategy card. To her left is Bob. To his left is Cheng, then Diego, then Esther, then Fahd. The full order of steps is:
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Trade (Strategy Card)
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If a player has their maximum number of commodities, and is instructed to replenish their commodities, they will take no commodities. However, they will still trigger any “when [this] player replenishes commodities” effects, most notably theTrade Agreementpromissory note.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During the action phase, each player takes a turn in initiative order. During a player’s turn, they perform a single action. After each player has taken a turn, player turns begin again in initiative order. This process continues until all players have passed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: During a player’s turn, they may perform one of the following three types of actions: a strategic action, a tactical action, or a component action.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: If a player cannot perform an action, they must pass.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After a player has passed, they have no further turns and cannot perform additional actions during that action phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: A player cannot pass until they have performed the strategic action of their strategy card.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Rules Reference
--- CONTENT: After all players have passed, play proceeds to the status phase.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Players may still play non–component action action cards after they have passed.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: Any abilities that occur at the end of an action happen before any abilities that occur at the end of a player’s turn.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: A player may resolve “at the start of your turn” and “at the end of your turn” abilities on the turn that they pass.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Notes
--- CONTENT: If all other players have passed, a player will continue to resolve “at the start of your turn” and “at the end of your turn” abilities.
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Active Player
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Component Action
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Game Round
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Initiative Order
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Status Phase
##################################################

### RULE_SOURCE: Action Phase
--- SECTION_ID: Related Topics
--- CONTENT: Strategic Action
##################################################
